Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee  
Foreword  
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo  

Table of Contents  
  Foreword …………………………………………………… 3  
1) The whole universe is searching for a day of love  
1 Corinthians 13:1-13  
<Prayer> Father! We do not know the original heart of the Father who created humanity, and we realize that we do not feel the love of the Father that can drive away our sorrow.  
Now, we must seek the Father’s love even if it means sacrificing everything, and we must restore the original relationship between the Father and us.  
Father! Your sons and daughters gathered here, now open our hearts and allow us to find what Your heart is and what Your love is, and open our ears so that we can hear Your voice, and grant us eyes to see the figure of the Father who is looking for sons and daughters who can receive the gifts that Heaven allows.  
Thus, allow us to see and hear, and to know the hand of the Father who has worked for us, and allow us to feel the heart of the Father who has endured. We know a little of the heart of the Father who has labored and endured, so at this time, please govern our hearts and bodies entirely as Yours.  
If there are sons and daughters who are caught in the realm of death due to ignorance, Father, please stretch out Your hand of grace once more to raise the entire history of creation, and allow us to face the heart of the original appeal and to respond before the heart of the Father.  
On February 16, 1958 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).  
7  
We earnestly hope that You will allow us the time. We have come to know that there is a purpose in the providence that the Father has managed with all His heart, and that there is a historical path that has walked out to the heavenly way. We understand that this has been accomplished through those who have sought a value system that can connect with Heaven and face Heaven.  
If we have a mission to eradicate the root of all historical sins, all contemporary sins, and all future sins, then we earnestly hope and wish that the direct love of the Father will manifest, allowing us to feel the impulse of gratitude within the Father’s love without being led by sin and without being burdened by it.  
Today, we know that our hearts do not move centered around ourselves, and that our bodies move away from ourselves. If my heart has also departed from me and my body has also departed from me, we can feel how the Father’s heart must feel in having to govern such beings.  
It has come to the time when we cannot do without the truth of heavenly principles, and we cannot do without the personality of heavenly principles, and we have come to the time when we cannot do without the love of the Father.  
Father, please allow the words that can introduce Your love to all humanity to manifest, and allow a person who can testify to Your love to appear before the multitudes at the end of today.  
Please grant us the mental preparation and foundation to follow that truth, and may the day when all things can be revealed before Your will quickly appear in history, Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Father! Now, let us be those who can feel the painful heart of the Father that Paul spoke of, and allow us to feel the heart of the Father’s love that he could not feel in his heart. Just as Jesus Christ became a sacrifice on the cross, let us be children who can become offerings before this people and build the entire altar, and allow us to share in the heart of the Father’s love.  
8  
The whole universe is searching for a day of love.  
Father, the way toward heavenly principles is this one path, the way to indemnify all the labors of Jesus Christ is this one path, and the way to resolve the grievances of the prophets and sages is also this one path. Please allow this one hour to be a time when we can offer a sacrificial offering of atonement before the Father on behalf of Heaven and Earth.  
Now, we have entrusted everything to You, so please govern it again. Allow us to convey the words of the Father that we wish to convey, and do not let the hearts of the giver and the receiver become separate. Allow this one hour to be a time when our bodies and hearts can move together with Heaven. Please remove Satan and govern everything personally, and we ask this in the name of the Lord. Amen.  
<Words> You may know that there is a term “heavenly universe” within the principles. And you may also know that this term encompasses both the invisible world and the visible world.  
However, both the Creator who created the created world and the creatures created by Him are all searching for a day of love.  
What is most necessary for us humans, and what is most urgent and significant above all, is to possess God. Next, it is to become a true person equipped with a true heart and true body. Then, it is to possess true substance. What comes next? It is to have love, which is indispensable for us humans. These are the important matters that are essential for fallen humanity to live today.  
When we look at our own existence today, we cannot deny that we need God centered around ourselves, true people centered around ourselves, and true good substances centered around ourselves. Furthermore, we need a connection of love that can unify everything centered around ourselves.  
9  
So, when you look at yourselves today, do you know where the God you need is? Do you know where the true person and true substance you need are? When faced with these questions, there is not a single person who can confidently step forward with assurance and capability.  
Therefore, if there is anything to boast about among all of you gathered here today, it must be a new heart and a new consciousness. It is time that we must have this. Today, we cannot live a life of peace and ease in our journey because we do not possess all the elements necessary for ourselves, and we cannot experience the love of God that can face the eternal creation ideal and sing our lives. You must have felt this through the lives you have lived until now.  
Thus, you cannot deny that it is time to lament the fact that you have nothing to boast about before the whole universe. This is why this fact is the sorrow of Heaven, the sorrow of humanity, and the sorrow of all things, as Paul clearly expressed. You have been given the responsibility to resolve this sorrow, and you must carry this responsibility as those who live within the realm of restoration.  
Therefore, if you have a heart that laments your position where you must now encourage yourselves, you should be concerned about the history that is surrounding you, and you should also be concerned about the times related to your current life, and you should be concerned about the future after this time.  
However, if there are people who are struggling without thought regarding what they should be concerned about, there is no one more pitiful than that. When those who have the mission to resolve the conditions of lament left behind before Heaven and Earth due to the fall do not realize their position and appear before all creation in a shameful manner, what must the heart of God feel as He looks upon that? Here, you must realize that you are in a shameful position that increases the lament of God.  
10  
The whole universe is searching for a day of love.  
So, where is that one loyal person who can boldly step forward to take responsibility for the lament of the whole universe while stepping on such conflicting environments? If humanity has hope, it is to become that one loyal person.  
So, what must we do to become such loyal people? We must become beings who can unify God, true people, and true things that are necessary for us today, and discuss love before God.  
Until now, we humans have made various prayers to God through the process of providential history and have upheld His will, but you must understand that not a single person has yet gone to the place where we can resolve the deep grievances that are embedded in God’s heart and discuss love. Although Jesus came to this earth, humanity could not establish a loving relationship with God through Him, which is why He must come again.  
Jesus Christ came with the mission to complete the 4,000-year history of restoration, but when asked, “Has humanity established a relationship of love with God?” no one can stand in a position to answer, “Yes.”  
Because we are such beings, if it is pitiful, there is nothing more pitiful than this, and if there is a reason to lament, there is nothing more to lament than this.  
So, what do you have to boast about today? Do you have knowledge? The knowledge you possess is extremely insignificant compared to the principles and truths of Heaven and Earth. No matter how advanced 20th-century civilization may be, it remains within the realm that cannot establish an absolute principle. Therefore, even if we have something to boast about, you must feel that a new era is approaching where this must be reanalyzed.  
11  
As Heaven looks upon historical destiny, contemporary destiny, and future destiny, and has sought to find ourselves, if you wish to establish yourselves before Heaven and wish to boast about yourselves, you must first become people who can possess Heaven. You must become true people. You must also become people who can face true things. This is a serious issue.  
And you must equip yourselves with the qualifications to govern all things that God created and said to Adam and Eve to govern, and be able to say, “I understand that this is what the Father wished for and what the Father has blessed, so please establish Your heavenly love connection with me.” This is the highest purpose of God’s providence that has been carried out until now, and it is the highest standard of Jesus Christ who has worked hard until now.  
But why have humans reached the current state? It is due to the fall of humanity. Today’s humans are descendants of fallen humanity, and there is not a single person who lives outside the fallen appearance and form. As the fallen lives of individuals combine to form a global fallen nature, a principle that can break and remove this global fallen nature must emerge.  
Before a principle that can guide humans in the opposite direction of the fall emerges, no matter what ideals of goodness or truths humans claim, you must remember that they cannot relate to our hopes or fundamental joys.  
So, what must we pursue as the descendants of the fall who cannot escape the yoke of fallen history? It is to become true people who can represent the ideals of the whole universe and possess values that can govern all things. Furthermore, if we long for God’s love, there is something we must not forget. What is it? It is the fact that we are a lineage that has inherited the bloodline of the fall.  
And if you feel that the tendencies of the fall are lurking within your hearts, you will come to realize that something new is emerging that you have not thought of or considered until now. Now, as a creature or as a person representing the whole universe, you must go before God and cry out, “I am a lineage of the fall.” If you do not have a moment of such prayer, you cannot escape the realm of lament that still remains before the universe.  
What does the fall of Adam and Eve mean? It means having abandoned God, losing the ideal human nature, and losing the environment of the original dominion. In other words, it means losing God, losing true people, and losing true substances. Then, it means losing God’s word and losing God’s love. This was the fall.  
However, humanity has not been able to transcend this result.  
Now we must fight to recover and pioneer these things from the opposite direction. If you do not become such a pioneer, you must understand that you cannot escape the historical realm of sin and the realm of Satan that opposed God’s providence.  
Through the fall, humanity has become estranged from God’s embrace, estranged from true human nature, and estranged from the true universe. The history to restore this is the history of God’s re-creation and the providence that God has been working on until now.  
The first Adam’s fall caused grievances to be bound, but what must the second Adam, Jesus, who came in the position of the restored Adam, do? First, He must allow God to come into His heart, and He must possess the will of the true person in His body, and He must become the true subject. He came to this earth as such a reality to testify to heavenly love, to testify to human love, and to testify to the love of all things, so that He could unify them into one.  
That is why Jesus claimed the kingdom of heaven in His heart when He came to this earth. And He claimed that God was in His heart, asserting His oneness with God. He also declared that the whole universe must be under His dominion. And to all humanity, He raised the banner of love, saying, “I am the Son of God, and you are my friends and brothers.”  
You must understand that the value of Jesus as the Messiah is contained in these words.  
Jesus had the mission to move families, societies, nations, the world, and even the universe centered around Himself, but the nation of Israel betrayed Him, the church betrayed Him, even the chosen John the Baptist betrayed Him, and families betrayed Him.  
Thus, Jesus personally established the apostles and sought to use them as a foundation to form the worldwide second Israel and realize the ideal of worldwide Canaan restoration, which you must know well through the principles. At that time, because the nation of Israel, formed by the 12 tribes, opposed Him, the formation of the 12 tribes was broken, and He lost the foundation established by Moses and the foundation centered on the 12 brothers established by Jacob, so He only traveled with the 12 disciples.  
Although Jesus was to be at the forefront as the founder of the second Israel, when the 12 apostles, like Jacob’s twelve sons, broke apart, He had to go back and take on the form of Noah’s family, taking the three disciples who were the sons of Noah to wander in the Garden of Gethsemane. However, when these three disciples could not unite with Jesus,
Jesus fell into the position of Adam at the time of the Fall. You must understand that this was the situation of Jesus. Today, Christians do not know this well. They also do not understand that Jesus prayed for ignorant humanity and the sorrowful heart of Jesus.  
As the main character who governs the world, Jesus was to introduce God's heart to all of humanity, and He was to govern all things, yet He was rejected by the world and rejected by His own family.  
Thus, Jesus lost His global foundation and became a pitiful figure who lost His national foundation. Consequently, Jesus found Himself in the position of Adam, who lost Eve due to the Fall.  
He came as the True Parents to humanity, which had lost the True Parents, but He lost His family and even lost the three disciples He had raised as children, placing Jesus in the position of Adam who lost Eve. Therefore, Jesus left behind the term "bridegroom" and "bride" on this earth. You must understand that Jesus was in such a sorrowful situation.  
Furthermore, Jesus could not convey all the words that could unify the world and the words that could unify the global second Israel, represented by Christian believers, who replaced the twelve tribes of Israel, as well as personal laws, social ethics, and family systems that could stand before heaven. This was Jesus's greatest sorrow.  
However, today, people do not know these historical facts. Even Christians, who claim to believe in God, do not know this. How could God, looking at such people, not sigh? The sorrow of God was further compounded by the breakdown of His plan to bless the Jewish people as the second Israel and establish a second Canaan during Jesus's time.  
What is needed for the returning Lord?  
If Jesus were to come again to this earth, where would He come and to whom? Jesus cannot come directly to the fallen world of humanity. He must come through the path of restoration, so He must surpass the stages of Noah's family and Adam's family. The historical process that must take on this responsibility and reach the world is what lies behind today's believers.  
However, today's believers do not know this. If they do not know this, even if they claim to believe in Jesus well, there is no way for them to welcome Him.  
The returning Lord will come as the main character of the world. However, the Lord must first have a family centered on heaven, a tribe, a nation, and a country. Only then can He become the main character of the world. This is the principle.  
If Christianity today wishes to represent the Lord's ideology of restoring the world, it must first consider whether there is a heavenly family centered on Jesus that can serve as a global foundation. Without establishing a heavenly tribe and heavenly denomination centered on Jesus and creating an expectation that can transcend national concepts, who can say that even if Jesus returns to this earth, He will not become a sorrowful Jesus? You must not forget that historical facts prove this.  
The fortunes of heaven and earth are passing through you. Whether you know it or not, whether your nation knows it or not, whether the country rises or falls, all the twists and turns of history are passing through you.  
What was God's will in overseeing the 2,000 years of history after Jesus? It was to establish a center that could represent the entire heavenly ideology through Jesus and realize true love on this earth. However, because Jesus's will was not fulfilled due to His crucifixion, the mission to complete that will remains with humanity on this earth.  
So what should you do now? You must appeal to heaven to send a true leader who can possess true people and true things, as humanity has lost Jesus.  
Because humanity killed Jesus, who came as the second Adam, we need the Lord who brings forth the words hidden in God's heart, who comes to represent the personality of heaven and build the kingdom of heaven, and who has the qualifications to govern all things. This is the hope of humanity.  
Now we must know how to uphold our dignity before God, who governs humanity. Otherwise, even if Jesus returns to this earth, we will not be able to meet Him. After that, you must remember that when Jesus came to this earth, the people who were to support Him allowed Him to die, falling into a position of a second Fall, thus abandoning God, the kingdom of heaven, true love, and the entire universe. You must always believe in and uphold the Lord.  
What should the leaders of the new era do? The most important thing is to build the kingdom of heaven through the love of Jesus. So where does the kingdom of heaven begin? It begins with knowing the love and character of Jesus and understanding the dominion of all things that Jesus can govern. Those who do not know the love and character of Jesus, nor the dominion of all things, cannot find God.  
When we look back at the 2,000 years of history after Jesus, we can see that many Christian believers have engaged in movements to find God again. As a result, the severely persecuting Rome eventually recognized Christianity, and ultimately established the papacy in Rome, leading to a political system centered around the papacy and the formation of a feudal society.  
However, as we entered the Middle Ages, the papacy became corrupt, and the humanistic ideology entered Christianity, leading to the loss of God for Christians after the Middle Ages. In other words, many people drifted into humanistic thought. Thus, through the Enlightenment, materialism emerged.  
This is based on the rationalism and empiricism that emphasize human reason. As a result, the world has fallen into a state where materialism, valuing material worth, prevails due to the influence of materialism and capitalism.  
Jesus came to this earth as the second Adam, carrying the mission to unify the entire providence on behalf of heaven, but our ancestors rejected Jesus, preventing us from escaping the history of sin. Thus, we could not find God, true humanity, or true material. No matter how much we struggled to find true people, we found ourselves in a situation where we could not find them.  
So who destroyed the feudal society of the Middle Ages? Heaven destroyed it. God intended to fulfill His will centered on the papacy, but as the papacy became corrupt, He broke it. When those who believe in heaven betrayed the will of heaven and established humanistic thought, they were struck down.  
Nevertheless, in order not to lose the point of providence, God initiated the Reformation centered on one person who cared for heaven, Luther. In this way, God has been carrying out a providence of breaking down and establishing.  
Through Christianity, God has led us through the pattern of the second Israel, the Renaissance, and after experiencing great chaos, He has been working to oppose the Enlightenment centered on humanistic rational philosophy.  
Enlightenment figures like Voltaire, Rousseau, and Montesquieu believed that Christianity would be destroyed. However, pure individuals emerged in Germany, advocating for practical inner experiences of God. This led to the revival movement of the Wesley brothers in England. Moreover, the Quakers emerged to facilitate mystical inner experiences.  
On the other hand, humanity has forgotten to love God and has also forgotten the reason to love humanity, reaching a point where they can only love material things. Even fallen humans must return to their original position, so there will come a time when they will strike against the material-centered ideology.  
Today, the age centered on God in the Middle Ages has passed, the age dominated by rational philosophy has also disappeared, and the materialistic ideology established in the 18th century is losing its light. The future world will be one where even if humans love material things, they will not find satisfaction, and following the teachings of historical figures will not solve the problems of reality. Therefore, the ideology of communism, which aims for societal prosperity through material production, cannot possibly govern the world.  
For this reason, with the advent of the 21st century, we are entering an era that will destroy the global dominance of material civilization. What kind of era will come next? An era that seeks and enjoys love will come. A time when we give to one another is approaching us.  
Thus, you must become wise individuals who can take on the mission of being a central existence capable of integrating and synthesizing all historical values, so that you can stand tall and proud before the universe in the coming era of love.  
Furthermore, you must recognize that you are in a position where you cannot avoid the path of the fallen Adam and Eve, and that you do not yet possess the qualifications to inherit the mission of the second Adam. Additionally, you should understand that today's history is a history that seeks to find God, true humanity, and true material, which were lost due to human fall.  
What was the cause of Adam's Fall? It originated from being drawn into the temptation of unjust love that God did not permit, leading to the destruction of the heavenly principle. The angelic form that occurred in the Garden of Eden is manifesting in many ways in our lives. We are passing through an era where what is not the right path pretends to be the right path, and thus we cannot avoid the chaotic age of love.  
God's providence is working in reverse through opposing paths. When we reflect on the 6,000 years of history, we can see that the Old Testament era was a time of seeking material, a time when one could approach God by offering material as a sacrifice, and the New Testament era was a time when the true Adam, Jesus, was offered as a sacrifice.  
In the future, the era of the New Covenant will be a time when all humans become substantial offerings before God, transcending the standard that can unify all things, and it will be an era governed by love.  
However, the external aspects of the world are being eliminated, and the internal aspects are being established, which is something that today's Christian believers do not understand. In other words, they do not know the content of God's internal providence that strikes the external aspects of history while encompassing the internal aspects.  
So what is God seeking through 6,000 years of providence? He is seeking the eternal words of promise made between God and humanity. That word is to establish a true relationship of parent and child, to become one.  
You know through the principle that the cause of human fall was an illicit and wrongful relationship. Therefore, you who are at the end must be cautious. Any man who is not careful may find himself in a position of dealing with two women, and women can easily be swept away into this.  
So how will this be resolved? How will this handle be moved? This is the question.  
The era of material civilization centered on infinite power is coming. Initially, there was the era of raw food, followed by the era of cooked food, and then the era of water food, which is the time to take in the nutrition of water. In the future, there will be an era where we can adequately preserve our health through scientific food. We will surpass the era that requires human effort.  
At that time, what will we do? What will remain is artistic culture, and we will wander in search of beauty and love. That is a good thing.  
However, if humanity strays from the heavenly law in search of that path, where will they ultimately go, and what will happen? This is something that those who revere religion today should be concerned about.  
Modern civilization has reached a stage where it does not know the true state of the world and does not need struggling religions. Therefore, today, religion bears the mission of presenting a path that humanity cannot avoid. Looking back at 2,000 years of history, there have been numerous revolutions. You must understand that humanity has been aiming for a unified world through the process of these revolutions.  
A world centered on God's love is a world of justice.  
When we consider that humans have intellect, emotion, and will, we can see that the Creator, who created humanity and is the principal protagonist of all creation, is the subject of a higher principle that can govern intellect, emotion, and will. Moreover, looking at history, it expands from individuals to families, from families to tribes, from tribes to nations, and to the world. We are also entering an era that prioritizes internal thoughts and ideas through such external forms.  
In individual beings, we are also moving from external aspects toward internal spiritual aspects. Since the spirit is dominant, only by unifying this spirit can we establish a value, and thus walk the correct path toward a unified purpose.  
The same is true for the world. Because there is a world perception in the world, a structure can emerge that can unify the world into one for the purpose of spiritual unity. This is precisely the situation where democracy and communism are opposing and fighting against each other today. At this time, you must understand that God, who created the spiritual world and the universe, desires to realize the unity of the universe, and thus the ideologies of the spiritual world and the earthly world clash.  
On earth, the historically dominant and inferior nations are progressing toward one worldview through the history of conflict. There will come a time when all spirits from the spiritual world will return to the earth. When that happens, there will be great chaos and all kinds of conflicts and fights on earth. At that time, you must play a leading role in ensuring that these events culminate in the direction that heaven desires. To do this, you must become a qualified individual who can represent God's heart and the ideology of the heavenly law. This is the hope that God desires at the end of history, but today's Christianity cannot fulfill that hope.  
Throughout the historical process, there have been numerous revolutions, but there has never been a revolution concerning human emotional issues. All systems of society and nation have been unable to eliminate the revolutionary elements that have sprouted over time and have instead been broken by revolutions.  
However, the emotional bonds between parents and children, between husband and wife, and between siblings have not yet experienced revolution. While every ethic, morality, philosophy, and ideology has gone through revolutionary processes, the issue of emotional love has not sparked a revolution.  
So today, have you become true parents who can stand before heaven with these emotional issues? Have you become true spouses? Do you have true children? If not, then you are falling short of the heavenly law.
Therefore, Jesus brought the love of God to this earth and introduced that love, declaring Himself to be the Son of God. The bond of love that Jesus established with God has not been broken by anyone to this day. No matter how strong the forces of Satan may be on this earth, they have not been able to break it. Furthermore, it means that what Jesus said, "You are my bride and my brothers," has not been broken either. 

Because of this foundation, Christianity has developed through the course of history. Thus, Christianity has become the core of heaven and has developed through history to form a family structure that can represent the heavenly realm through one person. 

No matter how powerful a person may be or how high their academic status, if they do not have a positive connection with heaven, they are pitiable. Therefore, those who understand these principles are grateful for Jesus. If Jesus had not made that claim, what would have happened to the human world? It would have turned into a world of darkness, a world of disbelief, struggle, conflict, and discord. 

For this reason, a new empirical world of love must be built centered on God's love, uniting the positive aspects of humanity, so that the era of peace can finally arrive. Therefore, you who are in this end time must not center on yourselves in rational matters. You should love your family more than yourself, love your nation, state, and the world more than your family, and have a heart that loves the cosmos more than the universe itself. 

All human plans and divine plans that have emerged throughout history must be able to be fully connected in this end time. Therefore, it is time to hear the good news that you can abandon all the negative issues you have had until now and start anew. 

The words that Jesus spoke 2,000 years ago, urging us to love more than anyone else, must reappear in this end time. Having passed through an era that respected human reason and an era of materialism, now the era of love is dawning. 

For this reason, it is necessary to have the words of heaven that can solve human issues and love issues. That time has come. 

To exchange love with God,
Until now, humanity has pursued only positive ideologies through the course of history, but that cannot be the case. Heaven is positive, and humanity is like a negative. Thus, religion teaches that humans should not be proud. It also teaches that one should not love oneself. It instructs to deny everything about oneself and even to strike one's own body. This is because heaven is positive, and humanity must become negative in order to exchange with heaven. 

Positive and positive are opposites. They repel each other. What is Satan? It is the position that, despite God being in a positive position, one refuses to stand in a negative position and insists on standing in a positive position. This is Satan. As mentioned earlier, in the life of virtue, asceticism is proclaimed. This is to strike the positive side belonging to Satan, or evil, and to convert it into a negative position. 

To strike the body means that the body should stand in a negative position, but since it tries to stand in a positive position, it must be struck to turn it into a negative position so that it can completely exchange with heaven (+). Therefore, unless you remove all conditions centered on your body, you cannot stand as a complete negative before the complete positive of heaven. 

The entire cosmos is waiting for a day when such a being can appear on this earth to exchange eternal love with God. 

Let us not lose our determination toward heaven.
Genesis 19:18-29, 1 Corinthians 9:23-27
<Prayer> We know that the day of victory that our Father desires has not yet appeared. When we think of the path of struggle that our Father has walked with blood and sweat for the final victory until today, we do not know where to place our bodies. 

We know that we must arm ourselves with truth and uphold the will of the Father, and to spread the good will that the Father desires, we must fight with all our might. Therefore, please allow our hearts and bodies to be mobilized, and allow the saints scattered on this earth and the heavenly hosts to be mobilized as well. We earnestly hope and wish that the day will soon come when we can give glory to the Father. 

In order to find this one day, our ancestors have endured fatigue and suffering throughout the course of history, waiting earnestly for the time of the Lord, and we know that the sorrow that has not yet been realized due to us humans is deeply felt in both the earth and heaven. 

We, who are lacking and insignificant, and powerless, ask that you make us aware that there has been a blood-stained struggle to find the glorious day that the Father desires. We thank you for granting us the determination and resolution to fight with all our hearts and bodies for your will. 

At this time, please sanctify our hearts again and receive us as offerings, completely separating the conditions of Satan's accusations so that we may become sons and daughters whom only the Father can take and boast of. 

Now, regarding the desired will, may we serve with all our hearts and bodies, and allow us to feel a new grace at this time, so that we may experience the overflowing glory of the Father. 

Now, I wish to convey the Father's words, so please allow the heart of the speaker and the heart of the listener not to be separate. Thus, I earnestly hope and wish that this hour may be one that can resonate with the heart of heaven. 

Please allow us to lay before the Father the content of our lives until now and the responsibilities we have not fulfilled. If we acknowledge that the contradictory knowledge of flawed humans cannot replace the truth of the Father, we earnestly hope and wish that we may lay everything before the Father and allow ourselves to be deeply immersed in the Father's grace. 

Please allow this time to be one in which Satan cannot find any foothold, and may it be a precious time to encounter the grace that has been granted. We earnestly hope and wish for this, and I pray in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

<Words> I will speak under the title, "Let Us Not Lose Our Determination Toward Heaven." 

The Value of Determination
Among you gathered today, there may be some who hold certain determinations in their hearts. There may also be those who can confidently assert, "My determination is right" in front of others. 

However, you must think about whose determination your own is. In other words, you must consider whether the determination you have is for yourself alone, or if it can also serve your nation, or even the world, and ultimately God. 

Above all, you must not forget that the time has come for you to reflect on whether the determination you hold is for heaven or not. 

Today, the determinations people have are diverse. The determination of one person differs from that of another, just as the determination of a man differs from that of a woman. Similarly, different nations have different determinations. 

So, what is the ultimate purpose of each person's determination? When you set yourself up and ask yourself this question coldly, you will realize that you cannot help but feel despair. 

In this end time, we, or humanity living on this earth, must ask ourselves whether the determination we hold can move our nation, whether it can move the world, whether it can even move the countless saints in heaven, and ultimately whether it can move God. When we reflect on this, we will have no choice but to confess that it cannot. 

For such a "me," for such "us," if there is a heavenly wind, we hope that we will consider what we should cherish in our hearts, what we should hope for, and what we should pursue as the most important issue. 

Throughout history, many people have held various ideologies and asserted them, but if those ideologies do not possess any elements that can move our hearts today, then their assertions, that is, the ideologies asserted by countless sages and saints throughout history, will have no relation to us. 

So, what has the history of humanity developed for? It has developed for the happiness of humanity or to establish the eternal ideals of humanity, and if we acknowledge the existence of heaven, we cannot deny this. As long as heaven exists, it must introduce to humanity what the garden of happiness is like and must enable humanity to build the eternal garden of joy. 

To fulfill that responsibility, the God who has been guiding the course of history until today has an inseparable relationship with us who are in the end stage of history. 

Therefore, those who do not have the foundation in their hearts to align themselves with heaven's will and to determine themselves according to heaven's will are those who violate history and betray God's hopes. 

God's Determination
The laws governing the operation of the entire universe follow the principles of heavenly providence, and if there is providence to achieve the overall purpose within that operation, then God must also follow the laws of that providence, and humanity must also go through those laws. 

Now, I must consider my own self in front of my nation. What is God's will regarding this nation, and what is God's determination to awaken this nation? Have you ever thought about this? If not, you must understand that you are standing in a position that obstructs leading the nation toward heavenly principles. 

And if there is something sorrowful in our hearts today, it is that this nation cannot struggle with a united heart centered around one ideology to walk the path it must take. You must realize that the inability of the entire world of humanity to unite in front of heavenly principles is the sorrow of heaven and the sorrow of humanity. 

Today, you must coldly analyze and critique what position you are standing in. Heaven is asking whether you have the foundation in your heart to confidently step forward in front of your nation and to confidently face heavenly principles. 

If God has the greatest hope for humanity, what would that be? First, it is to fulfill God's determination to achieve the purpose of creation on this earth. God had a determination before creating heaven and earth, and He created all things according to that determination. We know that God has gone through a history of sorrow because that determination has not yet been realized in this created world. 

Now, we who know this must search thoroughly throughout the universe for God's determination. We must find it and fulfill it. We must resolve God's sorrow and sadness. 

Therefore, today we must have the determination, assertion, and resolution to undergo a great revolutionary process centered on this will. Only then can we resolve God's sorrow. 

God has walked the historical process of labor to inform humanity on this earth of the will He has determined without our knowledge, and this is the history of providence up to now. 

The determination of God must be revealed by a savior who stands in the place of humanity on this earth, and he must confront all the forces of evil and defeat them. If a representative who carries out such a mission does not appear on this earth, God's will cannot be fulfilled. Furthermore, the standards of God's determination and humanity's hope must be connected on a certain day. 

The one sent as a central being to fulfill the will that God aims for on this earth in place of humanity is Jesus Christ. God has labored for 4,000 years, allowing Him to walk the path of struggle in all difficult circumstances, and the one who walked that path is the Jesus we believe to be our savior. Jesus came to restore God's determination of creation that was not fulfilled due to the fall of the first human ancestors, Adam and Eve. In other words, God sent Jesus to this earth as a second Adam figure to reveal God's determination before the universe. 

For this reason, Jesus claimed, "I am one with God." God and Jesus are not two but one. You must understand that a condition has been established that can please God. Furthermore, Jesus was so confident that He said, "God is my Father. Even if this is opposed and blocked, the content I feel and determine cannot be taken away by anyone." In other words, Jesus boldly proclaimed this, even at the risk of losing His life. 

The purpose of Jesus' 2,000 years of labor was to reveal God's determination to the many believers who believe today. We must understand that God has labored for 6,000 years without rest to send Jesus. 

The Determination of Jesus and the Role of the Holy Spirit
Now, if you have stepped forward to face heaven, heaven will ask you whether you have ever felt the image of Christ, who determined to stand in place of God's will, as your own image. 

Jesus came to this earth and lived a life of unimaginable suffering for over 30 years, ultimately walking the path of the cross in a tragic life. Yet, He kept His center intact, which could never be broken by anything. Because of this, Jesus is instilling the determination toward heaven in our hearts today. Even if death comes, even if the disciples who follow Him betray Him, even if the chosen nation and the church betray Him, He maintained an unchanging position because He knew the content of the determination that the Father had from before creation. 

What did the protagonist of that determination come to establish before humanity on this earth? It was to pass on to His loving disciples the determination of God that He held in His heart from before creation. However, among the countless saints who appeared throughout history, how many have fought to fulfill God's will with the determination that Jesus had? When we think about this, we must realize that God's sorrow does not lie with the unbelievers. It lies with the believers who say they trust in the name of Jesus. We must understand that God is saddened by the believers who lack a firm determination in place of heaven. 

Jesus sought to find a counterpart on this earth who would recognize His determination.

Let us not forget the lessons learned from their experiences as we navigate our own spiritual journeys.
Based on what they have established, they were able to be sent into the world of Satan and enter Egypt. However, even after establishing an environment from individuals to families and kinship, they did not walk a peaceful path. Representing the 70 disciples in a familial way, they stood on the stage of trials to form a nation centered on God, engaging in a national struggle to create a people. This is what you know as the 400 years of hardship in the royal palace.

During this period of hardship, the chosen Israelite nation was to regret how their ancestors had complained against God and betrayed His will, and they had to return with a longing for God. The stronger that longing was, the more the people of Israel could overcome the extreme hardships in Egypt and unite to easily enter Canaan with 600,000 people.

For this reason, Moses, who had to guide the Israelite nation suffering in Egypt, spent 40 years in the royal palace in deep mental anguish unknown to others, ignited by a spirit of love for his nation. However, the act of killing an Egyptian became the motive for him to lead a miserable shepherd's life in the wilderness. In that position, Moses abandoned all the glory of the luxurious Egyptian palace and, even if he faced hardships in Midian, he harbored an unchanging heart and a determination to care more for God's will than for his own love.

Even if he tasted the sorrow of being battered by all kinds of storms in the wilderness, he pushed it all aside, and despite being ostracized by his nation, Moses' unwavering determination to hold onto God allowed the nation to unite in difficult circumstances, and God was able to raise Moses to fulfill His providence.

To establish a nation chosen again, one of God's methods is to push that nation into global trials and engage in an offensive struggle. Therefore, the Messiah who comes to build a nation centered on God faces opposition from the chosen Israelite nation. This is because it is a process of restoration.

In the family of Adam, the Eve who should have followed Adam struck him, Noah's son who should have followed Noah struck him, and the 600,000 people of the Israelite nation should have followed Moses, yet they drove him into the wilderness of Midian. Because of this historical process, when Jesus came as the main character, the chosen people were in a bride-like position before Jesus, yet they opposed Him.

Jesus, who knows the laws of heaven, was ostracized by the Israelite nation and rejected by the Jewish community. He was not only rejected by his own people but also by the chosen John the Baptist and the apostles who followed him. He was rejected by the three disciples whom He could not exchange for heaven and earth. However, who knew that Jesus had a reason to hold onto them and bring them before heaven? Just as Adam faced various wicked schemes and temptations from Eve, Jesus was also in a position where he had to seek out his nation. Just as Moses lived a sorrowful life in the wilderness before the Israelite nation, when Jesus was ostracized by his nation, he was also placed in a position where he had to be ostracized before the world.

If at such a time, one could say, "Even if the nation betrays and the denomination betrays, who can take away my unwavering heart toward my Father? Even if John the Baptist, whom heaven has raised, betrays my determination, it is not a problem; even if my disciples betray me, it is not a problem," and furthermore, if one had the determination that their own body is not a problem, then even in sorrowful situations, they could not feel sorrow, and they could not show sorrow in the place of grief. We must understand the heart of Jesus, who bore the destiny of restoration.

Let us become those who feel God's sorrow.  
Romans 8:12-27  
<Prayer> Father! Please allow us to examine our hearts at this time, and allow us to consider our bodies, and guide us to be sons and daughters who can resonate with your heart.  
All the saints in heaven are aware that they cannot lift their heads before the Father because they are the descendants of the fallen. We, who are on the earth, must bow our heads before the Father and strive to carry the Father's heart, so please allow us to have no shamelessness in our hearts and no unfaithfulness in our conduct before the Father, dear Father, we earnestly desire and wish for this.  
Let those who do not realize that they have nothing to boast of before the Father understand that they are held by the hand of death. The closer we draw to the Father, the more we cannot help but bow our heads and feel compelled to confess our sins. This is our appearance as we strive toward our heavenly nature, but we must not become unfaithful sons and daughters who do not know where to place our bodies or how to conduct ourselves before the Father's will, dear Father, we earnestly desire and wish for this.  
Let us acknowledge that we are sinners, waiting for the Father’s mercy and loving hand, and grant us a sincere heart that can bow our heads and long for the Father’s heart. If there are any dark roots of sin remaining in us, we earnestly hope and wish for you to remove them.  
At this time, though there are many gathered, please allow us to become one heart, and though our bodies may be many, let us all become one. So that we may be able to pave a new path according to the command of the Father that we receive at this time. Please grant us the original power of heaven that can receive new authority and initiate new actions, dear Father, we earnestly desire and wish for this.  
Now at this time, may heaven protect us, and may Satan not find any opportunity to invade. If we have any theories or knowledge, doctrines, assertions, or concepts, dear Father, at this time let us forget them all and become a pure heart that can long for only you, and allow us to quietly offer all that we have in body and heart at the altar. Thus, we earnestly hope that we may be reshaped with new words and that the direct work of recreation that allows us to be embraced in the Father's loving arms may manifest here.  
Father! Now we wish to convey your words, so please do not let the heart of the speaker or the heart of the listener become two. We know that the greater the gap between the heart of the speaker and the heart of the listener, the more opportunities Satan has to intrude, so dear Father, please allow us to feel your sorrowful heart at this time.  
So that we may relieve the Father’s worries and become true sons and daughters who can bring joy and glory to the Father, dear Father, we earnestly desire and wish for this.  
We earnestly ask and wish for the Father’s merciful hand to be upon all gathered here, and we pray all these things in your name. Amen.  
<Word> Today, I will speak to you for a brief moment under the title "Let Us Become Those Who Feel God's Sorrow."  
Even if someone on this earth is enjoying glory and living happily, everyone knows that upon deep reflection, there is no one without sorrow. This applies not only to individuals but also to families. Furthermore, we must understand that even God, who created ideologies and governs the world, nation, and universe, has sorrow as He looks forward to the day when His will is fulfilled.  
If you have sorrow in your heart, you must realize that this sorrow is not limited to your individual self but transcends your environment and affects the whole environment.  
The relationship between God and humanity centered on sorrow.  
Today, I am an exceedingly insignificant being, but the sorrow I feel is not confined to me; it connects to the entire creation, transcending nations, the world, and even the heavenly principles. It is time for you to feel this tremendous truth. If one recognizes that the sorrow they endure is a sorrow endured on behalf of their nation, the world, and even heaven and earth, they may seem pitiful when viewed solely through the lens of sorrow, but we must recognize that they are indeed close to heaven.  
Until now, we have struggled to resolve our individual sorrows with our own strength, but we have not yet succeeded in resolving them. Now that there is heaven, a connection between heaven and me, and God's will governing through history, we must regard this sorrow that remains in our individual selves as a sorrow that represents the historical process or as the sorrow of God who has governed history. Such a person is a sorrowful individual, yet they have many friends; they may be a lonely individual, but they have a historical background, representing all realistic environments and being capable of standing in for the future heavenly principles. It is time for us to find our position in this regard.  
Now, if you have deep sorrow in your heart, will that sorrow remain limited to a certain boundary? Your sorrow must be stirred so that the earth can mourn, and the nation can mourn. Furthermore, there must come a day when the entire world can mourn, and God can mourn alongside us. However, the sorrow of your individual self remains as sorrow for yourself, becoming an obstacle before humanity and before the world and heavenly principles. You are unable to manifest sorrow on this earth that can respond to heaven and earth in the same situation and environment. Consequently, the heart of God, who possesses a sorrow greater than that of humanity, is blocked from being felt through the world, nation, people, and down to your individual self.  
Now, what is the greatest sorrow we have? It is the situation where when I mourn, heaven cannot mourn with me, and when I mourn, my entire family cannot mourn, and all of humanity on this earth cannot mourn with me. Today, we must feel that this is the greatest sorrow.  
So how can we feel the sorrow of heaven and all humanity when I mourn? If I focus on my own individual sorrow, I cannot find that position of sorrow. Therefore, if we are to mourn, we must learn to mourn for our families, and beyond the family level, we must have a heart that can mourn for the nation, the world, and even heaven. Only then will God's sorrow return to me through the world, nation, and family.  
What has God made us believe in during His restoration providence up to now? Before starting the work of recreation, what did He first make us feel? It is not joy. First, He made us feel sorrow for our individual selves. Then, He allowed us to feel sorrow for our families, societies, tribes, nations, and the world, and even for the heavenly principles. Only then can we find a way to stand before God. This is the principle.  
Therefore, the truth of Christianity is that it leads us to shed tears of sorrow and to go through a process of repentance.  
Then, when will the sorrowful twists and turns that have been bound in God's heart since the fall of humanity be resolved? This remains a fateful task that all humanity, the universe, and even heavenly principles must resolve. Thus, until the roots of this sorrow bound to God are uprooted, there will be no fundamental solution to humanity's own sorrow.  
God has created all things and has governed the providential history for 6,000 years, but He has never had a day of joy where He could reveal Himself as the embodiment of glory before all creation by relieving that sorrow. You must feel this sorrowful situation of heaven.  
The release from sorrow and Jesus.  
While we try to feel God's heart, the surrounding elements of evil and social environments often lead our bodies to take paths contrary to our hearts, placing our hearts and bodies in opposing positions.  
And when we look at our individual selves, we will feel that there are two aspects of sorrow. There is the sorrow that yearns for goodness and the sorrow that arises from our own desires. In other words, there is the sorrow that arises from the desires of the heart and the sorrow that arises from fulfilling the desires of the body.  
If we must feel sorrow as fallen humans, what kind of sorrow should we feel to escape the realm of this fall? We must feel a sorrow that reaches God's heart. Otherwise, we cannot escape from all realms of sorrow.  
However, humans living on this earth cannot create an environment where they can stand on God's side and share in God's circumstances and feel sorrow alongside God. Therefore, God sent Jesus, who could take on God's sorrow, among humans and made it so that humans could believe in Him.  
Jesus came to prevent humanity from relating to the sorrows of the world of Satan and to elevate them to the relative position of God, who feels sorrow.  
So what did Jesus bring to this earth? He brought love. However, to establish that love, Jesus had to overcome the mountain of sorrow. Yet, He could not overcome that mountain of sorrow, and thus, He completed about thirty years of life. Jesus bore a heart that others did not know and shed tears for the nation, worrying and weeping for Judaism and heaven.  
Therefore, even if fallen humanity wishes to understand Jesus' heart, they cannot do so as it is. Only when they stand in the position of having taken on all the elements of sin that have been woven into the long history of four thousand years and take responsibility for Jesus' heart, will they finally be able to feel Jesus' sorrow. Thus, the Jewish believers who simply believed as they were or the Israelites who boasted of their chosen status were in a position completely unrelated to Jesus' sorrow.  
When Jesus came to this earth and felt sorrow, He felt it on behalf of God.
Yes, the prayers offered were not for one's own sake but were prayers on behalf of the ideology that stands with God. They were prayers made with the heart to relieve God's lament and to fulfill the garden of God's love, yet at that time, there was no one among the people who could understand the voice of that prayer. Furthermore, no one was able to comprehend the essence of the gospel (New Testament) that Jesus spoke of.

Thus, Jesus had to convey the sorrow He had carried to humanity, creating an environment where humans could feel Jesus' sorrow and lament on behalf of God. Because this overall meaning was not conveyed to humanity, even after ascending to heaven, Jesus continues to lament. Therefore, we must understand that the sorrow of God still remains in the providential history due to the failure to fulfill the purpose for which Jesus came. 

Now, you must experience God's sorrow and the sorrow of Jesus Christ. You must become true people who can worry about heaven with the sorrowful heart you have felt. However, while you may have sorrow centered on your own self, you have yet to possess the sorrow that can replace the heavenly connection and allow us to pave the way for restoration.

For this reason, if you abandon all worldly sorrows for your own self and take time to feel the heavenly sorrow and God's sorrow while shedding tears, a new hope will begin from you. If there is a true person who can hold onto God's sorrow and shed tears on behalf of all humanity to resolve that sorrow, you must understand that the fate of the earth moves around the place where that person is.

Now, a nation that cannot lament on behalf of God will perish. Churches, families, societies, and nations that cannot lament on behalf of heaven will also perish. If this nation had become a people who could hold onto the heavenly principles and shed tears from the rulers to the common people, it would not have ended up as it is today. It is now time for us to awaken anew.

True Tears
Christianity is a religion of tears. Therefore, when we truly experience God's heart, we cannot look at the nation, the state, the world, and heaven without tears. We must stand in such a position, yet despite this, we are not shedding tears of inspiration and are instead being shameless and reckless towards heaven and the heavenly principles.

Even true friendships in this world are formed on the condition of tears, so how can fallen humans not shed tears in this situation of experiencing the heart of the heavenly principles? For this reason, there must be a time when we shed infinite tears in the place where we realize our sinful selves after believing in Jesus. In that place, we will feel that we do not know where to place ourselves and that we deserve to be punished a million times. Even if we sit without being able to lift our heads before heaven, we will feel a level of shame that prevents us from finding our position. Therefore, you must truly become people who lament and shed tears. Otherwise, your individual path will be blocked. You must also become a family that holds onto the heavenly will and worries about it. If not, the path of your family will also be blocked.

The fallen humans living on this earth are becoming more and more divided as their sorrowful hearts increase. If one laments centered on oneself, it leads to the division characteristic of evil people, while if one laments for the sake of goodness, the divided elements come together. In other words, the divided heart and body become one, achieving the point of unity with the heavenly principles.

So why must we go through the path of miserable fate? It is because humanity, having fallen, lost the ideal garden where they could live feeling God's love, thus causing infinite sorrow to God. In other words, because humanity has caused God to feel a heart-wrenching sorrow, there remains a necessity to go through such a path.

So what kind of time is this today? Today is the end time, and the time for shedding tears for oneself has passed, as has the time for shedding tears for one's family. The time for shedding tears for the nation has also passed. Now is the time to shed tears for the world. Therefore, you must not only shed tears for the world but also shed tears for the heavenly principles and the spirit world, and you must be able to shed tears for heaven. You must feel God's joy as your joy and God's sorrow as your sorrow. Only by becoming such a person can you stand as a rightful heir who can govern the world as a son of the Father who created all things.

To overcome this global sorrow, individuals and churches have sacrificed until now. But now is the time for us to go through the process of sacrificing for the world. In the future, we will go through the path of global sacrifice. That day, the time to settle accounts for not knowing God's inner sorrow is what Christianity speaks of as the end time.

When we think of this, what kind of environment are you in today? What position are you in? The Jesus we believe in also went through a life course that transcended the individual to replace the heart of the heavenly principles. Reflecting on this, we can see that today we are people who owe tears to God for not shedding tears equal to the tears God has shed for humanity.

Therefore, you should not just sit idly by today. You must build an altar of tears for this nation, this country, and for the world and the universe, where the sorrow within you erupts unknowingly. Furthermore, you must completely forget your own sorrow and pray with a heart that worries about God's will.

You must pray, "God! Please relieve your sorrow through me," and comfort God and Jesus, but you have not been able to make such prayers. You have prayed only for yourself. Thus, you must recognize that you have the responsibility to transcend such a position.

Facing the God of Sorrow
Now, you must throw all your sorrows before heaven and become a person who dedicates everything to heaven. Only then will you come to know that God sheds tears for you and is the Father who sheds tears for the world.

Moreover, you must understand that only when you recognize that the Father is the one who holds you and sheds tears can that Father become your Father and Jesus become your Lord. If there is someone who lives in such a position, they will come to know in what circumstances God is shedding tears for us.

Originally, if humanity had not fallen, they would not have come from the lineage of sin, and they would not eat the lamenting creation to survive. They would not die while carrying the burdens of heaven and earth's sorrow. However, due to the fall, humanity has come to bear all the conditions of lamentation and has found themselves in a position where they must escape from it.

Jesus died bearing the label of a sinner, but His heart of love for humanity did not change. If there is someone on this earth who laments for God—not privately, but publicly—God wishes to rescue them from sin.

God has had no choice but to grieve while seeing humans who are stained with sin, eating and wearing things that are tainted with sin. You must feel that God laments over the fact that you are in an environment where you can be invaded by Satan. This is why the Israelites spent three years sanctifying all things in the land of Canaan, and the Bible records the circumcision of the heart and the body. This signifies that God has not yet realized an environment where even the smallest of all things can be fully taken as His.

There are no sons or daughters whom God can freely embrace and love. Even if He can love, there is the sorrowful situation of a Father who can only love while setting Satan on either side. A son or daughter who receives God's love will feel that they do not want to eat food that is not appropriate when they see it. This is God's heartbreaking situation.

Now we must become one who can feel God's heart and, like what is described in Romans 8, become sons and daughters who can eat and rejoice in the things given to us in an environment free from the lamentation of all creation.

If you possess any material, you must understand that it is material that must compensate for the global sorrow. Your body is not yours either. Where is the source of life and material? It is God. Therefore, you must clearly understand that everything that belongs to you can only be recognized as yours after going through God. Thus, you must be able to sacrifice your body and mind for the will of heaven.

The Path of Justice and Morality

God is working hard at this time, hoping for the eternal heaven to be established on this earth for humanity and the generations of humanity. Yet, today, humanity forgets such facts.

God Cannot Be Looked Upon Without Tears
A person who lives while feeling God's heart, which governs through historical sorrow, cannot look at God without tears, no matter where they are. You must become true sons and daughters who can bow their heads before such people. Only then can you inherit the great work of the creation of heavenly principles. Are there such sons and daughters on this earth? You must become that person. If you cannot become such a person, you must remember that you will become a sinner who cannot dare to lift your face before heaven.

What is the purpose of the ears you hear with, the eyes you see with, the mouth you speak with, and the feelings you experience? They exist to fulfill the will of heavenly principles. However, if they stray from the will of heavenly principles, they will inevitably face a day of judgment. Knowing this fact, you must first judge yourselves and then be able to judge your surrounding environment. In other words, the path of the cross for you is to judge yourself, starting with judging your own life and even judging your own death. Only after going through the day of resurrection can you finally become true sons and daughters recognized by heaven.

The Mission of True Children

If there is such a person, they may seem to be failing outwardly, but they will never perish. Even if they are despised and chased away, a successor will surely emerge from such a person.

Today, you are walking a different path. Do not blame anyone. Rather, through the tears you shed for them, you will receive the benefits of indemnity. You must not forget that all those people are your family.

If there is a flock that holds hands on this earth, weeping and worrying about God's will and heavenly principles, and bowing their heads before God, then even heaven will bow its head before them. Because he is an invisible sacrifice, all people will bow their heads before him. The sacrifice that Abraham offered long ago was small, but not only did Abraham bow his head before that sacrifice, but all of heaven and earth also bowed their heads.

Therefore, as you stand in the position of a sacrifice for any environment in your life journey, you must always consider what kind of conditions for sacrifice you will establish. Will you set conditions for a personal sacrifice? Or will you set conditions for family, social, national, or global sacrifices? The heavenly value will be determined according to the conditions of the sacrifice you offer.

So what is our desire after pioneering difficult environments? It is to become true sons and daughters who can empathize with God's sorrow and worship before the Father; this is our only hope.

And you must become a unified family that can communicate the Father's heart and circumstances and raise the banner of the struggle to relieve that sorrow.

Thus, in the process of your life, you must feel the sorrow of heaven and resolve the universal sorrow that has remained until this day, and also restore all things that have been permeated with the conditions of lament. The Original Garden of Eden and God

We know that a garden without the fall is a garden where God can freely interact with all things, a garden where God can freely visit humans and discuss with them. This garden is not only for humans but also a glorious garden where all created beings made for humans can host God, and it is a joyful garden where humans can discuss with God. However, from the day the term "fall" came into being, humans became beings who could not face God, and all things became beings that could not enjoy God.

God, who created heaven and earth, created humans as the center of all creation to dwell with them forever. Thus, all created beings should manifest God's glory through humans and give joy to God through humans. However, because they could not become such a created garden, God set that day as the endpoint of history and the standard of hope, and has been working through providence, which we must newly recognize today.

So what kind of garden is it that the countless people of today, who have inherited the bloodline of the fall and cannot escape the lineage of the fall, seek, long for, and admire? That garden is one where I can call God, the Creator of heaven and earth, my Father, a garden where I can feel the joy of the Creator while hosting Him. Moreover, it is a garden that can convey that joy to all creation through us humans. If such a garden does not exist, then all of God's creation ideals will fail, and the purpose of providence that humanity has upheld throughout history will also fail. If this happens, even the creation that looked upon humanity will return to a state of lament, and you must have a day when you feel this deeply.

My heart must resonate with this feeling, and my body must feel this sensation. In such a position, I must be able to yearn for the Creator's image towards heaven and become a being that possesses the original beauty towards all things. Only then can I become a resurrected being through which the Father can operate. There must be a time when I can reveal myself and analyze myself before the Creator and all the creatures of the universe. If there is no such time, you must understand that God's heart cannot permeate your body, and the lament of all things cannot be resolved through you.

Originally, humans were to live with God and rejoice with Him. However, today we are in a state of having lost the Father who created us and the protagonist who should govern us.

Thus, we have become pitiful beings like orphans. From the moment we realize this fact, we can begin to seek the new purpose of providence.

However, when have humans called the Creator, whom they lost in the Garden of Eden, our Father, and felt that the garden of goodness lost in Eden is the environment in which we should live? Thousands of years of history have passed until today, but such a time has not yet appeared in the world of humanity.

The Mission of Humanity

Today, we must recognize that what we possess cannot replace the absolute unique goodness of heaven, and that we are fallen descendants of sin who cannot dare to face the Father. What should we do? We must rise up and seek the Father's will. Even if we lose everything we have and sacrifice everything, we must be able to call God, the protagonist of the ideals our ancestors longed for, our Father. And only when we can manifest that God within our living sphere can we stand as sons of God. However, if we do not have that day when we can manifest God within our living sphere and before all creation, we must understand that the providential path our ancestors have walked through history will return to failure.

So now, what should you awaken your sleeping hearts to resolve, and what should you rise up and run towards? We must earnestly seek the heart that God had for Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden. You must be able to feel the heart of the Father who wanted to rejoice over humanity while feeling the beauty of creation towards all things within the realm of substantial time. If you do not have such a heart, no matter how much the garden of ideals may come in the end times, or how much the Father may return to this earth, you must understand that it will have no relation to you.
Who will close the gap between God and me, and who will settle this pit of resentment? Today, we feel that this has been a historical lament and grievance.  
Then, who created this gap between me and heaven? It is the lineage of sin caused by the fall of our human ancestors that has created this. Therefore, we must step on this and ascend to receive the heavenly lineage, establishing a relationship with heaven from our bodies and minds, and we have the mission to connect our families, societies, nations, worlds, and the universe with heaven.  
When you reflect on your past today, you cannot help but feel that you have inherited the lineage of sin before the heavenly principle. This is the reason for heaven's lament until now and the cause of all creation's lament. We must understand that God has gone through a history of effort to save such people until now.  
Now, you must be able to pray, "Father, please come quickly!" in place of the unfallen Adam who was able to meet God in the Garden of Eden, stepping over all internal barriers.  
God is coming to find the lost Garden of Eden through the connection of restoration with fallen humanity. The history of providence that God is working to restore fallen humanity and to build the joyful garden where He once met the unfallen Adam and Eve, and to establish a global ideology based on heavenly joy, is the history of salvation and the restoration that we must walk today.  
Therefore, you who are walking the path of restoration today must calmly place yourselves before the path of heavenly principle and critically examine yourselves. You must reflect on what position you are in and from what standpoint you are struggling. You need to understand that it is because of God's love that He wanted to teach humanity about that position and direction, which is why a religion representing humanity has been established today.  
Thus, God is seeking to find humanity through the historical process centered on religion, establishing faith as a noun. Until this moment, God has been tirelessly working to live among humanity, desiring to be with us. Because God is an incorporeal being, He has a heart that transcends temporal distance and has come to humanity until today.  
When we consider that God, who has transcended time and space to find those who have betrayed Him, has not been met by many humans, we must recognize that we, as descendants of the fall, are beings who should rightly receive lashes before heaven. Nevertheless, you must understand that God has been working for 6,000 years in providence.  
Then, if my individual self, as one person among thirty million, can host God and bring Him to dwell on this earth, then I will become a being of value greater than thirty million, greater than the entire 2.4 billion humanity, and even greater than all creatures in the created world. You must understand that it is this Father who has worked hard to meet such a being as us.  
God's Heart Desiring Unity with Humanity  
Today, we humans often forget the value of the important parts within ourselves. Even though humans should bow their heads before the will of heavenly principle, they have forgotten the will of providence through the historical process, lost their dignity and status, and are unable to find the direction to move forward. You must feel God's painful heart as He looks upon such humans, and you must recognize that the time has come when we cannot neglect the will of God's providence.  
If we say we want to make such a God, such a Creator, the subject of our faith, but in reality, we are centered on ourselves, then we have no relationship with heaven.  
When we look at ourselves as individuals, we are merely one out of 2.4 billion, yet God wants to believe in us as beings of value representing the entire universe, to love us, and to live with us. However, today, humanity cannot even think of such a Father's heart.  
Heaven approaches us with infinite hope, while we approach heaven with limited hope. Who will take on the task of reconciling this difference between limited hope and infinite hope? The greater this difference, the more Satan accuses us before heaven regarding our own selves.  
Therefore, you must acknowledge yourselves as being caught in such a predicament, within the historical realm of sin, and bow your heads before heavenly principle. Thus, with a heart of repentance, you must become like clay and water, able to be reshaped again. Yet, many today disregard heavenly principle because of their own assertions. You must understand that what they do and commit is not limited to one individual but is connected to entire nations, or even the whole world, or the entire universe.  
So, to whom will heaven entrust such matters? You must take on that responsibility today. You must become people who can fulfill the will of providence from the position you are in and be those who can host God. To do that, what must you do? First, you must understand the standard of God's hope. You must understand the heart of the Father who rejoiced at the creation of humanity at the beginning, and you must understand the ideal of creation that He desired to enjoy.  
Then, what kind of heart did God have when creating this world? He created it with the desire that all things could infinitely believe in Him, and that humanity could become beings who could infinitely believe in Him. Therefore, you must remain unchanged in your relationship with heaven, even as countless years pass, within the integral realm of ideals where the noun of faith is not even necessary. God wanted to believe in humanity to the extent that He would not even feel the need for the noun of faith, standing in a position of oneness with humanity. However, this heart of God, who wanted to believe in humanity forever, has been lost due to the fall of humanity.  
God also wanted to inject His eternal life into humanity, establishing them on this earth in the form of immortality, but due to the fall, humanity has become a being that is as good as dead even while alive. The foundation of God's love, where humanity and God could eternally become one and be immersed in the integral ideal, was broken due to the fall of humanity.  
As a result, humanity has become a being that cannot be trusted by God, and a being that lacks the traces of God's life. Thus, God's love could not be realized, and our ancestors were expelled from the Garden of Eden, the ideal of God's creation.  
The Consequences of Human Fall  
However, it was not only humanity that fell; even all created beings fell outside the realm that God could trust. We can no longer find the movement of God's life in all things, nor can we express the stimulating impulse of beauty towards God's love.  
Therefore, today we must become true parents who do not receive the invasion of Satan, centered on God.
