If the human ancestors had lived as true parents with God, their children would have established a family ideal that could live with God forever. However, due to the fall, their descendants have inherited the lineage of fallen parents and are living a life where they serve Satan instead of God.  
Because our ancestors broke the garden of goodness that God desired, we, their descendants, have inherited that sin and, as a result of being invaded by sin, have come to hold a faith that should not be believed, to have pleasures that should not be had, and to engage in loves that should not be pursued. You must understand this.  
From this perspective, when I think of myself, I realize that I am someone whom heaven cannot trust, and that I am not a living being that can stand before God. Furthermore, I do not possess the heart of love that can stand before God. Thus, humanity, who has fallen from parents of the fall, can no longer enjoy eternal joy with God in the original garden, the eternal world of heaven. Humanity, who should live joyfully with God, possessing God's eternal life and being within the realm of God's eternal love, has become unable to do so. The world of humanity has become a world of sin, where humans believe what they should not believe, possess lives they should not have, and engage in loves they should not pursue. Moreover, by becoming a world that cannot be believed, a path that cannot be believed has been left, which is the hell of the spirit world and the hell of the earth.  
You must understand that the contradictory positions of these two worlds are weighing upon me today. On one hand, the disbelief of hell is appealing to me, and on the other hand, God's love is appealing to me. In other words, on one side, the love of death in this world is appealing to me, while on the other side, there is an appeal for me to have eternal faith and eternal love. You may feel that you are in such a position.  
Due to the fall of humanity, our bodies have grown by consuming all things within the realm of God's lament. When we analyze our bodies, which are within the realm of God's lament, that is, the realm of sin, we find that there are more elements of evil than elements of goodness. Therefore, in the overall journey of my life, in the journey of faith, and in the journey of love, this evil is moving more strongly.  
The purpose for which the Creator made this created world was to be centered on humanity. However, due to the fall, you may feel that there are wounds and curves deeply felt in the hearts of humanity.  
No matter how evil a murderer may be, he will feel a pang of conscience about his evil actions. This is human nature. Because the law of heavenly principle is such, even if humanity has fallen by violating the law of heavenly principle, they cannot escape from it. Therefore, when humanity has committed evil by violating the law of heavenly principle, they cannot help but feel a pang of conscience.  
Today, many people lament and resent the universe, feeling that they cannot believe anything on this earth, cannot rely on any life on this earth, and cannot feel any love on this earth. However, there is no one who cries out in lamentation, longing for a love that can be believed forever in their hearts, and a love that can be enjoyed forever.  
However, heaven seeks to fulfill God's will through those who are concerned for the will of goodness. When we compare the numbers of good and evil from that standpoint, we realize that evil has an immeasurable number compared to goodness. God, who observes this, is filled with a deep sorrow today, seeking goodness on behalf of humanity's sorrow. You must understand the sorrow of God, who is in a position where He cannot believe in humanity, who should originally be believed in, loved, and should have become beings of God's life.  
The Connection of Life and Love  
As you look at the earth, lamenting, "O land where God's sorrow remains! O humanity building walls of God's sorrow!" you must be mindful that a person who will feel sorrow on behalf of God may not appear in this historical end time. If such a person does not appear, we must not forget that God's history of effort will come to nothing, and we will be left in a position where we can only live in a world where the conditions for Satan's accusations, that is, the conditions for lamentation due to sin, remain.  
Today, we forget that we are sinners, do not feel that our paths are blocked, and claim to have hope from that blocked position. Thus, the heart of heaven observing this is in an even more tragic position.  
We have inherited the bloodline of our ancestors who betrayed God in the historical process. If today I am a manifestation of this blood of sin, what will I use to explode this body and eliminate that sin? Now, you must become new people. You must become heavenly siblings with new ideals, new faith, new life, and new love. You must reflect on whether you can cry out with a desperate heart, "Father, please come quickly!" feeling the earnest heart of God who has sought you for 6,000 years.  
Our ancestors appeared on this earth to fulfill God's will and to undertake some historical mission, but they all fell away. You must know well through the principles that this repetition of history is the history of restoration until now.  
God, who is filled with the grievance of restoration, has endured with a sorrowful heart until now. That is, until now, God has endured even while being rejected and has endured even on the path of betrayal. Yet, have you ever felt the heart of God, who has hoped for us until this day, deeply in your bones and in your flesh? You must truly feel that the Father who has worked until now is my Father, and that He is the Father who has labored for me.  
Even if our Korean people are said to be poor and lacking, if there is someone among us who bears the hope of heaven, who carries God's concerns, and who has the heart of faith in God, or if there is such a gathering or such a nation, who can definitively say that they cannot inherit the sovereign work of heaven? What should this pitiful nation, this nation without a place to rely on, and this nation without hope now aspire to? They must have a heart of repentance for their sins, a heart of faith in God, a heart of hope in God, and a heart of love for God.  
Only then can this nation become the children of heaven. In other words, they can dwell in a new Garden of Eden and become a new nation that can fulfill the purpose of the ideal of creation.  
God is one who cannot abandon fallen humanity but seeks to find them again. But what kind of connection did God and humanity originally have? There was a connection of life, and there was a connection of love.  
Then, what must we seek today, mobilizing all humanity at the end of the world? We must seek the very life that was connected with God, the very love itself. Today, humanity is wandering to find that.
God desires that humans become beings who can eternally believe in Him, form an everlasting family, and create a world where they can discuss matters forever. He has been working throughout history to achieve this. Although humanity has fallen, God has been seeking out these individuals until now.

Who did Jesus come as? He could not become a human who could be believed in forever in the Garden of Eden. So, who holds the standard of heart that can be believed in forever? God holds it. Humans were meant to become beings with the standard of eternal life, but because they betrayed God, that standard of life is held by God. Furthermore, humans were meant to become beings with the standard of eternal love, but due to their betrayal of God, that standard of love is also held by God.

Then, who came to present the elements necessary to build the ideal of the Garden of Eden to humanity? It was Jesus. God has worked through a long historical process to find a standard that could replace His faith, life, and love on this earth, but He could not find it. He sought through Noah, Abraham, Jacob, and Moses, but could not find such a person for 4,000 years, and finally, the one who was established was Jesus.

So, who was Jesus? He was not one who held the power of the world. He was not one who had worldly knowledge. He was a figure who was labeled a traitor of the times. He was the representative protagonist who was persecuted in place of justice in a world of sin.

The reason Jesus was persecuted was not because he had no value or because something was lacking, but because the entire world was a land of disbelief. It was a world without life, and because it was a world without love, he was rejected.

Then, what kind of representative was Jesus? Adam fell in Eden and could not become a parent who could be believed in. Therefore, Jesus came as the representative of Adam. He came as the protagonist of faith who could not help but believe eternally. He came to reconnect the lost life of God in Eden and to reestablish God's lost love in the hearts of humanity, representing God's love.

So, who is Jesus? He is the Messiah of faith, the Messiah of life, and the Messiah of love. In other words, he came as the Savior of faith, the Savior of life, and the Savior of love. God, who has been governing human history for 4,000 years, hoped that His life and love would form a standard of heart, and this was realized through Jesus. Thus, God's providential work began anew on this earth, and the new purpose of restoration was achieved.

At that time, people were to have a substantial faith before Jesus, who came with such historical significance. They were to become one with the ideals of Jesus. Jesus appeared as a manifestation of the intangible ideals of faith, life, and love that God had embraced.

However, no one testified, "Oh! You are the fruit of faith that God has sought for 4,000 years. You are the embodiment of God's hope and life that has come after 4,000 years. Oh! You are the protagonist who brings eternal love that can be enjoyed in God's ideal garden." They did not welcome him. No one could penetrate his heart and reveal his secret words on this earth. This has caused a second sorrow for humanity.

For this reason, although Jesus came to this earth, he could not testify to God's faith, God's life, and God's love as a substantial being, and he passed away without doing so.

Thus, the faith united with the spirit of Jesus, the life united with the spirit of Jesus, and the love united with the spirit of Jesus have become distant from humanity today. And the fact that Jesus became the protagonist of spiritual faith, spiritual life, and spiritual love is not a joyful matter when you understand it. You must recognize that there is a sorrow of heaven bound up in that.

In other words, God desires a substantial being that represents His ideals. Jesus came to this earth as the embodiment of God, bringing God's faith, God's life, and God's love, but because humanity destroyed that substance, God became a sorrowful God.

When God seeks out humanity, He comes through the spirit to find the substance. And through that substance, He seeks out all things. However, humanity could not become qualified to believe in the substance, could not become qualified to replace the life, and could not become qualified to replace the love, and this has only been realized spiritually. Therefore, today we only feel these things spiritually. In other words, humanity today is seeking the ideology of spiritual salvation, searching for spiritual life, and wandering in search of spiritual love.

In this way, God has worked for 4,000 years to place the substantial being of glory on this earth, and it is the providence of paradise salvation and the providence of salvation centered on the New Testament to spiritually create an environment where humanity can believe in him forever, enjoy eternal life with him, and love him forever.

However, there must come a time on this earth when the faith that the spirits in the spiritual world believe in, the life they hope for, and the love they long for will manifest as substance.

The ideal of Eden was not only to serve God with the unity of human hearts and bodies centered on God but also to serve God in unity with all things. Because this is the principle, God has sought to become one with many through the historical process of labor until now. You must understand that there has been such a longing.

If Jesus had come and established the substantial temple, and if he had established a substantial family that could replace God's ideals, the need for the millennium kingdom ideology would not exist for us today. There would be no need for the ideology of the Second Coming.

If we become people who can pass through substantial faith centered on the Lord Jesus, become people who can pass through substantial life, and become people who can pass through substantial love, then we can have substantial spouses and substantial children. In that case, we can also become substantial humans of God's faith, possess substantial life, and become beings of substantial love. However, the fact that such a foundation has not yet appeared on this earth is God's sorrow.

Therefore, Jesus said, "The kingdom of heaven is within you." The kingdom of heaven comes first from the heart. Then, one can say, "The kingdom of heaven is in your body." In other words, the day must come when one can assert that the kingdom of heaven is in my substance, so that my body can become one with the spirit and call God 'Father.'

Here lies the sorrow of Jesus. He established a spiritual kingdom that could replace the kingdom of the heart, but he could not establish a kingdom that could replace the ideals of the kingdom of the body. Therefore, he is in a position where he must come again, and through the historical process, he is in a destiny where he must pray for humanity while sitting at the right hand of God. Thus, humanity today, which is in the end times, must have substantial faith.

When you reflect on your own journey of faith thus far, it has been a heart and body that have doubted God's will. Therefore, you must become people who can say that you have realized the eternal connection of God's life and the eternal connection of God's love. And to do that, you must always pray, "Father! Please let us be able to become your substance."

If you cannot become such people, humanity cannot escape the history it has incurred until now and cannot restore the lost ideals of the kingdom of heaven.

For this reason, God has been concerned about humanity until now. Especially in these end times, He is searching for us with even greater concern. Therefore, today we must become a being of hope that can replace the substance of Jesus Christ who came 2,000 years ago.

Faith Standards that Saints in the End Times Must Have
You must always be able to report to the Father whether you are living in the form of hope for faith, hope for life, and hope for love. Thus, you must live with the mindset that says, "Indeed, Father! I will believe in you. Even if you say you cannot believe in me, I will believe in you. Even if you forsake me, I cannot forsake you."

You must be the protagonist who can say, "Even if the heavenly principles change, even if any being in the heavens betrays me, I cannot betray you." God is looking forward to the day when He can find such a person.

Is there anyone who understands this sorrowful situation of the Father? Is there a church? Humanity is a pitiful being that does not understand this.

Those who appear in the world with the will of heaven are rejected. At the time of Jesus, everyone was his enemy. Those who were not rejected or were not enemies were rather false. Jesus came to this earth and lost his place in the family. He was rejected by the group that John the Baptist belonged to, which God had chosen and prepared. He was rejected by the denomination that had been prepared for 4,000 years. He was persecuted by the chosen Israel, the descendants of Abraham. He was persecuted by all humanity. He was also rejected by the spiritual world. Furthermore, he was rejected by God.

Thus, Jesus, as recorded in the Bible, "Eli, Eli, lama sabachthani?" which means "My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?" (Matthew 27:46), ended his life in a miserable position. You must not forget that the one who felt such anguish is our Savior, the Savior of humanity, and our leader, and you must be able to empathize with the heart of Jesus.

Elijah, when he was rejected and chased away by the people of Israel, cried out, "Father, I alone am left." Have you ever had a moment to empathize with such a heart? Even if 30 million people reject me, even if 2.4 billion people in the world reject me, and even if all the spirits who have gone to heaven reject me, you must be able to say, "I will not forsake you."

A person who has experienced such a heart cannot go to hell, nor can they perish on this earth. And there is nothing that can break them.

Jesus had this heart when he pleaded, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will." (Matthew 26:39). You must understand that this one heart became a central point that could trample death's authority. Jesus came to this earth and was rejected by his nation, rejected by the church, rejected by his tribe, and also rejected by the unseen spiritual world of Satan. In other words, Jesus had no friends.

Could the people of that time have ever imagined that such a Jesus would appear as the Savior of humanity? 

In this light, the standard for creating a new history was established through Jesus. Jesus lived with the unchanging heart that the Father is the Lord of my life, the Lord of my existence, and the Lord of my love. Because Jesus' faith, life, and love could not be cut off by anyone, Christianity has developed without falling, even when beaten in any nation.

You, who are coming to the Unification Church today, must have the faith that Jesus believed in if you want to serve humanity. You must possess the standard of faith that allowed Jesus to risk death and sacrifice his life, that is, the standard of faith that allowed him to sacrifice even his own body. Heaven is longing for such a standard of faith to manifest in the saints of the end times.

We, who must receive salvation and seek eternal life, must rise above all hardships and deep wounds. Now, we must become heavenly soldiers who can charge toward the historical death of our lineage, standing in the position of Jesus, who clung only to God's will, even if family, society, nation, and the world oppose us.

How has heaven sought us out? The God who exists in spirit at the heavenly throne waited for 4,000 years from the creation to establish Jesus to seek humanity. After Jesus, He has worked for another 2,000 years in the spiritual world, which represents our hearts, and through the footsteps of 6,000 years of labor, He has been seeking us until today. But have you had the filial heart to say, "Father, I am grateful. Father, I am ashamed. Father, what shall I do?" and to resolve the sorrow of the Father who has worked to find me? You must understand what heaven desires.

If you have become a son or daughter with such a heart, then just as Jesus, who had the heart of compassion and love for 33 years, held onto the Father's heart and raised the history of resurrection amidst suffering, you too must have that heart and trample on the authority of death to raise the history of resurrection. If you cannot become such individuals, you will not be able to live in the glory of resurrection by trampling on the authority of death.

You must now know God clearly with your heart and body. The time has passed when you only knew God with your head. You must know God with your heart, and now is the time when you must know Him with your body as well. Therefore, the era of conceptual faith has passed. It is now the time to believe with the heart and experience with the body.

This is because the end times are the time to seek the substantial reality of unchanging faith and to establish the embodiment of eternal love. When such a reality comes forth, the noun of disbelief will disappear from my body.

Therefore, you must now become sons and daughters who can be concerned about the heart of the Father and serve Him. Otherwise, you will become pitiful beings. If you do not know that God exists, that is one thing, but if you do know, you must understand that the God who has worked to find us is not someone we can only serve as the protagonist of our hearts.

God is the substantial protagonist with whom I can eternally become one, eat together, and live together, that is, the one with whom I can eternally share joys and sorrows. He is the unchanging essence of love and the embodiment of eternal hope. In front of such God, Jesus was someone who could act without any excuses or manipulations, forgetting himself if it was for the will of the Father. You must become sons and daughters who inherit the footsteps of such Jesus.

Jesus, through his life of over 30 years, gave us the words of the gospel. When he was with his disciples and encountered hungry people, he immediately...
The miracle of feeding over 5,000 people with five loaves and two fish was also performed. He gave everything that needed to be given. He introduced faith, introduced life, introduced love, and introduced everything that a human can demand. 

Have you ever accepted Jesus' words as if they were the reality of Jesus himself? Have you felt through Jesus' words that he is the embodiment of the eternal God’s faith? Have you felt through Jesus' words that he is the embodiment of eternal life? Have you felt through Jesus' words that he is the embodiment of eternal love? If you listen to Jesus' words and do not feel these things, then Jesus is saddened. 

Jesus' hope for humanity and God's request

When Jesus walked for over thirty years, being chased from one village to another, he said, "Foxes have holes, and birds of the air have nests, but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay his head." (Matthew 8:20). Did the people at that time understand that these words, filled with loneliness and sorrow, represented the culmination of 4,000 years of providence? They did not know. 

The Israelites did not realize that Jesus was the embodiment of the life that God had hoped for over 4,000 years, the life that would fulfill the desires of humanity. They did not know that Jesus came with God's faith, love, and life. 

So who will help us cross this mountain that we could not cross due to not recognizing Jesus? Even if you are a poor crowd today, being pushed around and having nowhere to rely on, I hope you will become the inheritor of Jesus' will. 

The time has come for me to appear before the nation with the heart and lamentation that I am walking the historical path that Jesus walked. The time has come for me to appear before the world. 

Only by appearing before the nation and the world with such a heart can we block the history that Israel betrayed, the history that Judaism betrayed, and all that was blocked by the bloodline of Jesus. We can also block what the apostles and disciples betrayed. In other words, we must become a figure that can resolve all of that within our own reality. 

2,000 years ago, Jesus distributed bread to countless crowds in the wilderness near Bethsaida. But why did those who ate the bread all perish? Why did the people who heard the words betray Jesus? Why did the disciples who followed him through hardships for three years betray him? The reason they betrayed him is that they only understood the words as being for that day, and the bread given to satisfy their hunger for that one hour. They did not realize that the words given by Jesus were meant to be carried to the ends of the earth through themselves. They did not know that the bread Jesus shared was meant to be distributed to all humanity. 

The words and bread given by Jesus are his very essence, which means they were meant to be shared with my heart, body, laughter, nation, and all of humanity. Because they did not understand this meaning, they all perished. 

However, now when you stand before the Lord or before the Father, some may feel, "Oh, my beloved son! I give you this word, so keep it and become a son loved by God." Others may feel, "Oh, beloved sons and daughters! You must become a substantial temple where the Father can dwell during your lifetime." Therefore, you must feel that only the Father is the essence of my life, and only the Father is the essence of my love. 

Do not be discouraged by the fact that you have no friends, no family, and no one with you. However, if you have become a person who lives according to the will of the Father, feeling the essence of the Father's life and being immersed in the heart of the Father's love, then do not be discouraged. Even if we suffer many hardships today, we must endure. The reason we endure our hardships is for the nation and for the world. 

Now, if there is someone who feels the lamentation of heaven and earth and stands up to pray, he will become a friend of Jesus, a friend of the nation, and a friend of the world. Ultimately, he will become the master of the world. 

Now, the question is whether we are inside or outside of God. God wants to fulfill His wishes through our hearts. Therefore, everything we do, where we stay, and the injustices we suffer must all be for the Father. Even if we are cut off from love and have no material possessions, even if we have no friends, if we have a connection for the Father, we will have no worries. If the Father's faith, the Father's life, the Father's love, and the Father's wishes are with me, then I will have everything. When all of that is with me, I become a son of substance who can represent all living beings on this earth. 

You must feel a sense of oneness with God. 

You are shedding tears for the nation more than anyone else. You are walking a life that should bring tears when you look back. However, now that you know the Father's will to be the embodiment of the hope and faith of the Father, you must fulfill that mission. 

This nation lacks friends who can believe in each other. It also lacks a true family where one's life can settle. So what will you leave for this nation? You must leave faith for a nation that cannot believe, leave a family of life for a nation that has no home for life, and leave love for this poor nation that has nowhere to rely. 

When you have such a heart, you will feel that the situation of Jesus in the Garden of Gethsemane is my situation today. That is, his situation is our situation today, and we must feel that it is the situation of our ancestors who have gone through the historical process for the will of providence. Therefore, you must now become a person who overcomes historical rejection. You must become a person who wins 100 percent against any Satan. 

You must be able to cross over any power of death and go towards the welfare of Canaan, sharing the sorrow of the Father who has worked for 6,000 years. You must become someone who can receive glory on behalf of the Father with the heart of heaven. Heaven has traversed the difficult thorny path and come through the path of sorrow. When you are being pushed around, you must look to the Father who is worried and endure, and you must be grateful for the day that is given to you to be able to embrace the Father. 

The time when we believed with our heads has passed. Now, you must become the embodiment of faith that can believe with your heart and body. The time has come to know the living Jesus not just with your head but with your heart and body. You must know that the essence of Jesus has replaced God's faith, life, and love. 

Therefore, when you say "left," the history of God's providence that represents the history of providence will say "left," and when you say "right," God's life will say "right," and when you say "correct," God will be able to say "correct." It was the lamentation of God who created humanity in the Garden of Eden that he lost such a person and lost the family. 

Do not shed tears over your own sorrow. Someday, you will feel that the Father will wash away those tears. Do not complain that you are wronged. The Father will know that wrong. 

Now, when I thought I had left the Father, I realized that I was standing before the Father, and when I thought I did not know the Father's love, I realized that my body was already immersed in the Father's love. At that moment, I feel that the Father is my Father. The Father I want to know is not the God of faith bound by concepts, but a real Father who can be experienced, that is, a biological Father who can be experienced within my realm of life. 

Just as Jesus prayed, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will." (Matthew 26:39), you must feel the oneness and unity between the Father and yourself from a serious standpoint. 

When that happens, the faith of hope, the life of hope, and the love of hope will be ignited within me. Thus, when I move, all things will move, and when I act, everyone will follow me. When you enter such a realm, you will feel that all things rejoice over you. Also, when you enter such a realm, you will hear what others cannot hear, see what others cannot see, know what others do not know, and experience what others cannot experience with your body. 

To become true sons and daughters who can serve the Father 

This was the way humanity was meant to live, serving the Father in the original Eden. However, you must recognize that we are fallen humans who do not feel this. Therefore, on behalf of the 6,000-year history, on behalf of 2.4 billion humanity, and on behalf of countless beings across the ages, we must take upon ourselves the sorrowful heart of the Father who has suffered for 6,000 years and say, "I will take responsibility for all of the Father's sorrowful heart. Please entrust me with your worries, sadness, and pain. I will be a son who can comfort the Father who has worked hard for 6,000 years and be a loyal subject." You must pledge this. 

Have you ever called out to the Father with such a sorrowful heart and earnestly appealed to Him? If not, you must repent. 

When we reflect on our faith life today, we must realize that God sought me, but He did not seek me as an individual. You must feel this. God's love for me is not just for me alone; it is for the entire universe. His calling is not just to make me feel good; it is for the sake of heaven and earth. His desire to believe in me is not just for me; it is for the sake of the entire universe. His love for me and His desire to establish me as the embodiment of life is not just for me, but for the sake of the entire cosmos. Therefore, you must understand that your body and heart are not eternally yours. 

Have you ever received heavenly grace and been thankful for it? Before you rejoice, you must know how to shed tears. While I am rejoicing, what about the people of this earth? While I am being elevated, the glory of heaven is not being revealed, so how can I manifest this glory of heaven before all people? You must think about this. It should not just be about my own joy and happiness; you must recognize that there is a cosmic providence of God that remains through me. 

When God deals with us, He even forgets His own dignity as the Creator of the universe. He is the Creator and the master of heaven and earth, leading the providence. Heaven is dealing with you, who are currently under the power of Satan, with the faith, life, and love of heaven and earth. You must not forget this. 

You must become a person who understands God's wishes, fulfills God's faith, and accomplishes God's will of life and love. Thus, you must ensure that the eternal flame of love and the eternal flame of life can be ignited through you. You must become someone who can feel this in your daily life and realize that the mission to pave the way of suffering while serving the Father is placed before the fallen descendants of humanity. 

Therefore, now you must fight all battles, defeat your enemies, and after overcoming them, offer a victorious worship to the Father. Your body must become the resting place of the Father, and your heart must become the resting place of the Father. 

You must recall the sorrow that the Father felt at the time of creation and say, "Please rejoice as you face me, just as you would rejoice in the eternal image of Adam who did not fall. Father, please find the lost will that was lost due to Adam's fall through me." You must have such a heart. Only then can you become a son or daughter of the Father who can say, "Oh, Father! Please come quickly." 

<Prayer> Beloved Father, you have sent the righteous prophets to find us, and you have sent Jesus to cultivate the foundation of our hearts. Now we know that there is a purpose left for us to fulfill your will through our bodies. My individual self must fulfill the Father's will through the family and also present all things before the Father. So, Father, please be with us. 

It is not your will to build a kingdom of heaven that only remains with us, but we must also build a substantial kingdom of heaven where you can dwell within all things. We realize that we have a responsibility to bear this universal responsibility. When you see us remaining in the fallen world, you must be worried and saddened about our path. Therefore, please hold us, who are lacking and weak, and lead us to have eternal life. 

If you lead us, we will not be discouraged. We will not hesitate. Therefore, we earnestly ask that you guide us to become individuals who can drive away the enemy Satan to possess the life and glory of the Father, and to become heavenly heroes who can build the church, nation, world, and heaven where the Father can operate. 

Now, we earnestly hope and wish to become sons and daughters who can feel the Father's heart with our hearts and the Father's life with our bodies, so that we can present all things before the Father. 

We earnestly ask that your joyful news be heard before the countless people of today, and we pray all these things in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

5) Whose are you? 
John 15:1-27 
<Prayer> We understand that the ideology of creation is not to find a specific individual but to find all of humanity. O Father, who has worked hard to find humanity on this earth! When we think that there is a providential purpose to establish the entire universe within the ideology of goodness, we earnestly hope that even if we die a million times, we can become the fertilizer that fulfills that purpose and help the Father in any way we can. 

The Father’s sorrow is not due to the creation of all things on this earth, but because there is no individual human being who can fulfill the Father's ideology of creation. We ask that you allow us to understand this fact at this time. Now, please allow us to fight for your will with all our hearts and sincerity, and let us recognize that you are the Creator who created all things and the one who has worked infinitely for us. 

A person who does not know the Father’s heart does not know the Father’s life, and a person who cannot feel the Father’s heart does not understand the Father’s circumstances.
Please allow us to recognize that we are those who are doing, and let us realize that at this time, Father, you are looking at us who cannot accompany your heart and are grieving. We earnestly wish and hope for this, beloved Father. 

Therefore, please allow our hearts to completely become one with your will. Lead us to live like friends of the Father, and guide us to be those who can live in a way that you can operate through us. 

At this time, we come to know that Jesus was the one who appeared with such a heart of God's will for the people of Israel. The created human beings remain as they are, and all created things remain as they are; please help us to realize the reality in which the Father can be present. Beloved Father, now come to us and sanctify our bodies and minds so that we can become such beings. Thus, guide us to be pioneers of a new age who can enjoy with the Father and realize the ideals of creation, beloved Father, we earnestly wish and hope for this. 

Whether in the days of Jesus or today, or even in the future, we believe that the Father will work with a uniform love. Beloved Father of love, please allow us to feel the sorrowful heart that Jesus had at this time. Also, grant us the heart of the Father that can love all things on earth, and allow us to resemble the Father's character that can embrace and love all people, beloved Father of love, we earnestly wish and hope for this. 

Father, we know that at this time there are many of your sons and daughters scattered and chased in various regions, so please take care of them, and let them have the heart to deny all of themselves and struggle only for your will. 

May they become sons and daughters who can break through any path of the cross or path of lamentation and move toward the path of your life, and we earnestly wish and hope for you to lead them with love. 

You are the one who has allowed us to have a heart of sorrow that others do not know, so please comfort us with your heart and encourage us with your body. Thus, allow us to be sons and daughters who can defend the final battleground of the end and win, receiving worship from Satan, beloved Father, we earnestly wish and hope for this. 

Though each individual gathered may be different, we believe that our hearts for the will must become one, and our bodies for the will must also become one. 

If there are any elements of lamentation that are not in accordance with your will, please remove them, beloved Father of love, we earnestly wish and hope for this. 

Now I will convey the Father's words, so please allow those who receive the words to be sons and daughters who can confess all their things before the Father's heart and analyze and reflect on themselves, beloved Father of love, we earnestly wish and hope for this. 

Father, at this time, many people with various wounds in their hearts have gathered, so you, who have been governing our hearts, please soothe the wounded hearts, and if there is anything wrong in our hearts, please remove it. Let us always reflect on whether there are conditions for Satan to invade, and if there are such conditions, may we be able to eliminate them, and may you watch over us with your fiery eyes, beloved Father, we earnestly wish and hope for this. 

Father, now I wish to convey the words, so please allow the heart of the one conveying the message and the heart of the one receiving the message not to become two. At this time, Satan is lurking, so please allow us to move and act like friends centered on your will, beloved Father of love, we earnestly wish and hope for this. 

Father, please look upon the thirty million nations with compassion, and have compassion for all humanity on this earth. Also, we earnestly ask and hope that you will find and establish the conditions for the restoration of indemnity required by all spirits in the spirit world. At this time, we earnestly ask once again that you protect the lonely family members scattered in various regions with a uniform grace, and we pray all these words in your name. Amen. 

<Words> At this time, I will speak to you under the title "Whose Are You?" 

Every person living on this earth claims to live for some purpose. 

At first glance, it seems that our lives begin and end centered around ourselves. However, upon further reflection, you may have experienced that this life, which seems to revolve around oneself, is full of twists and turns, lamentation, sorrow, and sadness. 

Furthermore, while living for oneself and focusing only on oneself fills one with sin and sorrow, you may have felt in your actual life that if you forget yourself and live denying yourself, you can smoothly overcome any difficulties. 

The existence conditions of all beings
If we think more deeply about the essential aspect of humanity, we cannot deny that neither our body nor our heart belongs to us. Also, although it seems that the entire created world and the universe belong to the created beings themselves, upon deeper reflection, no one can deny that it belongs to the Creator. 

For example, it is easy to think that this earth belongs to the earth itself, but we cannot deny that this earth also exists as part of the universe. Furthermore, while it is easy to think that all things existing on the earth are their own masters and have begun to exist by themselves, we cannot deny that all things also cannot exist outside the connection to the earth. 

In this way, when we look at all existence, from the largest to the smallest, they are all interconnected and inseparable. When we examine the earth, we can see that this earth cannot exist by itself. That is, it only fulfills the conditions of existence as the earth when it operates in accordance with the laws of nature while being interconnected with celestial bodies. In this way, when we look at the earth, if we acknowledge that there is a Creator of the earth, then you cannot deny that this universe was created by God, that the earth was created by the universe, and that all things existing on this earth were created by the earth. 

Then, what is the source of all things existing on this earth today, that is, the existence like the body of humanity? You cannot deny that it is the earth. And what is the existence like the parent of the earth? You cannot deny that it is the universe. However, it is true that we have not yet clarified what the parent (source) of the universe is. 

All things exist as results of having gone through a causal process like that of parental relationships, yet seeking satisfaction only as the result world itself is a historical contradiction and a realistic contradiction that you must now realize. 

Then, what kind of solution should there be for the universe and all things in this position, as well as for you? A person who can clarify all of this, that is, an individual who can pass through all connections and represent the value of the entire universe, the overall ideals, and the gospel ideals must appear in this end time. If such an existence does not appear, you must clearly understand that you cannot conclude that God has governed humanity centered on humanity. 

Today, humanity, which claims to be the master of all things, is governing the visible world. If humanity thinks that it owns itself, that is a misunderstanding. Your body is not yours. Your heart is also not yours. When you are asked what the basis is for claiming that it is yours, you will find yourself in a position where you cannot answer. 

If this issue is resolved, it becomes a historical turning point and a solution point that can resolve all problems. However, today, the people living on this earth are living without remembering this issue. 

God is more saddened by the fact that such humans exist than by losing the universe. Therefore, if there are those who can feel and empathize with such a heart of God, then the fundamental providence of religion can start from them. You must understand that from here, the way to find God again can be opened. 

Everything that exists on this earth has the earth as its parent, and the celestial bodies as its parents, and furthermore, it has the Creator as its parent, just as you as an individual do not end as just yourself. 

Have you ever felt that the earth has become your parent? Our bodies are made up of all the elements of the earth. We are beings who cannot deny that the earth is our source. However, humans often forget that they are embraced by the earth. Now you have come to know that there is a material parent, the earth, and you must also recognize that there is a parent who gave birth to you as an individual. 

The structure, value, and standard of human life
Then what kind of being was humanity created as? It was to establish a being equipped with all material elements, a substantial form that can represent the ideals of heaven, which is why God created humans from dust, water, and air. Since humans were created through this ideal of the Creator, if there is no element in humanity that can harmonize with the divinity of God, then there can be no ideals, hopes, or desires in that humanity according to the principles of creation. 

When God created humanity, He fashioned the flesh as a combination of material elements that can connect with all matter and breathed the spirit that governs the flesh into that flesh to create humanity. 

Just as matter must have a connection with the earth or the universe to demonstrate its existence, humanity must believe that it has the earth as its parent and, furthermore, that it has the heavenly ideal subject as its parent. You must clearly understand this. 

Then what is humanity? It is a being made by the combination of the substantial (body) that represents all material connections and the substantial (spirit) that represents all spiritual connections. This is what humanity is. Because humanity has such value, it can rejoice before the Creator, worship the Creator, and offer songs to the Creator. In this way, humanity itself is a very small individual, yet it is a being of universal value that can represent the glory of heaven on behalf of the entire universe. Furthermore, heaven desires to meet such a perfected human being. 

Therefore, you must not have a heart that seeks to assert something for yourself. When you assert what is not yours, claiming that your body is not yours and your heart is not yours, history will not tolerate it. You are well aware of the fact that individuals, nations, and states that have done so in the past have perished. 

Because humanity must inevitably follow this path, heaven has led humanity by establishing the principles of goodness and indicating the direction of goodness, bringing history to this day. In the clan society era, it was centered on the customs of the clan; in the era of nation-states, it was centered on nationalism or statism; today, it has been centered on globalism beyond the level of the nation. 

Now, this should not end here; ultimately, we must live for the providential will centered on the heavenly way. Those who do not aim for their own ideology or their own national ideology will inevitably be broken. 

When you think about this, where will you find your place of stability? You will find it difficult to find a resting place where you can feel happiness, where you can feel satisfaction, and where you can confidently appear before all creation as a representative of God. However, this has been the common goal that humanity has sought. 

Now, standing in a position where your heart faces the heavenly nature and your body faces all things, have you ever felt the realm where you can confidently say that all things are yours? Have you ever felt that you can say that the clans, nations, and the entire humanity are yours due to bloodline connections? Furthermore, can you say that all spirits in the spirit world, not just earthly humans, are yours? 

When you reflect on these things, those who are arrogant and boast about their own something without being able to do so will face indemnity. Those who establish and boast about their own something, those who put forth their own ideological claims, will surely be broken. 

If you cannot deny these facts, then it becomes an important question of what standards you should live by. 

The teachings of religion for the restoration of the parent-child relationship
Originally, if humanity had not fallen, it could have stood in a relative position of goodness with the parent of goodness. However, due to the fall, the connection with the parent of goodness was severed. Since then, humanity has walked the path of sorrow. Humanity must restore the severed connection with the parent of goodness even if it means crossing the peak of death. 

Then how can that connection be established? That connection is not established through any global ideological claims or any national ideology or social system. It must be established from your heart. Therefore, if that fact is not determined from your heart, no matter how happy the world becomes or how good the world becomes, you must understand that it will have no relation to you. 

However, today your desires are moving beyond your individual self toward the nation or the world. While that desire for possession is precious in itself, what could be more precious than that? First, recognize that you are a being belonging to the eternal and unchanging subject, and then fulfill the universal desires. If there is such a person, there will be no power or force on this earth that can strike them down. 

However, today humanity does not think about this. What use is it for those who cannot assert their true value to take everything and govern the universe? 

Therefore, in today's human world, if there is an ideological claim that represents the universal ideals, it is religion. There is no ideological claim beyond religion. The relationship in which we can say that the invisible Creator is our Father and we are His sons and daughters, and the inseparable parent-child relationship and its value is what religion is based on. Thus, true religion does not merely remain at the level of governing a particular nation. It looks toward future nations, future worlds, and furthermore, toward the heavenly realm. It is moving toward the purpose of uniting the earth and humanity, created through the ideals of the Creator, in a trinitarian relationship. 

Since religion is aimed at restoring this, it has emphasized the master-servant relationship until now. It has also established orderly connections based on what comes first and what comes later. The heavenly principle is such. 

Then, where does evil originate? Evil originates from breaking away from the orderly connections centered on the heavenly principle. Therefore, heaven is saying that you are the universe's, the Creator's, and your own.
You have worked hard until today to establish that one standard.  
Do you wish to become the center of the future? The center of the human world established without a connection to God is not eternal. Or do you want your nation to be the center? Even if you become the center of your nation as you wish, you are a fallen human, and there will come a time when it will falter. Even if you stand proudly before the world, the time will come when it will falter. Therefore, those who wish to walk the path of religion, that is, the path of the way, are taught to give up everything. However, that does not mean to always give up everything.  
In the journey of fallen humans going through the path of goodness, they cannot avoid an indescribable series of trials and the process of revolution and struggle. Because humans must go through such a process, God knows that if any nation becomes fixated on any ideology, it will eventually break, and that is why He told them to give up everything.  
Thus, when Christianity appeared on this earth, speaking of heaven, it faced unimaginable persecution. Furthermore, in any era, individuals or nations that have raised heaven have not been welcomed. Even 2,000 years ago, when Jesus came forth with the gospel of the New Testament, He was driven out nationally and globally. Moreover, since the time of Jesus until now, there has not been a single nation that has not persecuted Christianity.  
However, God has not tolerated any national policy that does not align with the content that Jesus advocates in order to establish the ideals of Christianity on this earth.  
Individuals, families, nations, and the world that God must possess  
Jesus did not have the nation He should have, nor the country He should have, nor the world He should have; therefore, God has been working hard until now to reclaim that. So, who must fulfill that will? The one who must fulfill that will is neither heaven nor earth, but you yourselves.  
While God is working to reclaim this universe, He cannot find the entire universe at once, so He has worked hard to find one person first, which was the 1,600 years spent searching for Noah after the fall of Adam. Although God established Noah because Adam made a mistake, Noah also could not fulfill his responsibility for that will, which extended the period by 400 years until the time of Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, when He finally found one individual and one family.  
God led the family of Jacob through the journey to Egypt and established Moses to lead the nation of Israel. However, Jesus, who came to find the nation centered on the people of Israel, could not claim that nation as His own and could not establish it as heavenly, and as a result, what happened to the chosen nation of Israel? It became a nation that was scattered throughout the world.  
Thus, since Jesus came and left, heaven has been establishing the providential path of the New Testament before humanity on this earth, and what is it doing? It is trying to build a nation and state centered on God that Jesus sought and to create a world where the universal ideals of heaven can operate. Because they do not have that foundation, today’s Christian believers still have the ideology of the nation they must find and establish.  
However, they do not know this fact.  
So, what does Jesus demand of you in this age? Since heaven has lost the nation of Israel, which it has worked hard to establish for 4,000 years, it hopes that Christianity will fulfill the mission of the Second Israel that can replace that nation of Israel. However, you must understand that Christians are forgetting this.  
In this situation, if you think about yourselves moving toward the heavenly kingdom, you are pitiful people. Because humans have not been able to correctly convey the principles of the heavenly kingdom, there are no families, societies, nations, or worlds that can communicate those principles. You must realize that you are in such a position.  
Because your ultimate purpose is to find and establish all those things, heaven has hoped that until you establish that, you would not become a being that belongs to or relies on anything. In other words, heaven has hoped that you would not belong to any nation or ideology. That is why today you are in a fate where you must walk while engraving such things in your hearts.  
And today, when you ask whether your body has become a body that can represent this earth, a body that can represent the nation, and a body that can represent eternal life, you will not be able to answer that you are. Therefore, you must not claim your own body as yours. Just as Jacob had a family of 70 centered on his twelve sons, you must become a part of the nation that God can govern, and that nation must belong to the world that God can rule. Furthermore, you must ensure that all spirits in heaven can also belong to the realm of ideals governed by God.  
When you think of this, you must know what position and what status you have been chosen in today. You must also reflect on how you have developed your ideals, your desires, and your actions from your position. Thus, you must clearly understand what position you are in before the overall will of heaven and the overall providential will of creation.  
God’s providential will regarding Christianity is to find individuals that can make God rejoice and to find families that God can govern, and to unite those families to form a heavenly nation. The chosen people of Israel were supposed to fulfill that responsibility, but because they broke, God is mobilizing the global Christians to establish the Second Israel. Therefore, today, all Christians around the world must unite as one and face the evil of this earth, preparing for the final judgment day that Christianity speaks of.  
To belong to God  
Those who have completely harmonized with the will of heaven and have been recognized by the heavenly realm will know. They will feel that God recognizes them as His own while also seeing all things bowing down to them. On the day when all creation recognizes you as a child of God, that is, as belonging to God, not only countless spirits in the spiritual world but also all things on earth will bow down and sing praises to you, a fact that humanity today does not know.  
When you enter a position where God can recognize you and all things can recognize you, even those with true conscience will naturally harmonize and enter that position.  
And you must have a sense of your existence and your consciousness of existence, but you must abandon the notion of possession that it is mine, and you must have the thought that you will represent the will of all things, the will of humanity, and the will of heaven. A person who is aware of carrying such an ideology is called a person of the way. To walk the path of such a way, you must not live a life of having everything, doing everything, and enjoying everything on this earth.  
If you truly wish to establish the value of existence according to the will of heaven, you must first be able to ruthlessly deny yourself and have the determination to fight ruthlessly against your family, society, and this sinful world. However, this does not mean to do so by force; rather, you must attack sin with service and sacrifice. Through this journey, heaven has been silently fighting for 6,000 long years.  
Then, having learned that the Creator God has worked hard to find humanity again, what should you do now? You must become a being that can become one with this universe, with all humanity, and furthermore, with all creation. You must also be owned by God.  
So, what must you do to be owned by God? First, you must be able to feel that the Creator God, who created all creation, is our Father. Therefore, you must understand that the Creator God is our Father who has worked hard to restore the unbreakable relationship of Father and Son from the beginning until now as the eternal and unchanging Absolute.  
If our physical parents give us flesh and blood, what kind of parent is the Creator? He is our eternal, unchanging spiritual true parent. He is the true parent of our spirit who gives us eternal life while also being the parent of our hearts. Until today, we have been taught to honor our physical parents and to be filial to them, but because there has been no law regarding the Creator of heaven, humanity and heaven have walked different paths. Thus, there should have been someone who could represent humanity and substitute for heaven, and that person was Jesus.  
Jesus came to this earth and said, “The Creator is my Father.” He said, “God is my Father, and I am one with Him.” He claimed that He was one with His spouse and one with His Father. Therefore, it was great that He established the duties of a filial child for the sake of heaven above any other claim.  
The reason Jesus could become the Messiah  
Today, you who believe in Jesus are at the end of history. However, to come to this point, you have gone through numerous revolutionary processes. The habits and customs that centered on individuals or tribes have all been broken when larger forms of nations emerged. A single individual nation has also gone through a historical process of being absorbed by larger and stronger nations under the providence that seeks overall unity.  
The earth is one, humanity is one, and God is one; thus, in the end, God is working to create a day when these three can gather together and rejoice. And God is not a God who has any leading authority to command, nor is He a God who governs with His own desires.  
For 6,000 years, God has been approaching humanity with a heart that cares for individuals and families more than that of a parent caring for a child. The history of God’s effort to find a day when humanity can have a heart that can be more filial than a child to God is the history of God’s work regarding humanity. However, today, humanity does not know this fact well.  
Now, if you hold such thoughts in your heart and pray, you will not need many prayers. With that one word, “Father God!” you will come to feel the heart of the Father who has worked for thousands of years. You will come to realize that God has gone through the process of struggle in the 6,000-year history to find today’s you.  
Therefore, if God wishes to call you “My beloved son!” you must become a person who can relate to God as a Father while feeling the Father’s heart from the time of creation, the sad heart He felt due to the fall of humanity, and the heart He feels to save all of humanity.  
And you should not be satisfied and rejoice in the fact that God is providentially working with you today, but rather feel the heart of the Father who is concerned about humanity that must go through the arduous journey of confronting the evil that still remains on this earth and must reach the destination of Canaan, and when you call that Father, you must understand that that one word, “Father,” becomes a word that can resonate with the overall meaning of history.  
However, today, when you commonly pray, you call out, “My Father who is in heaven,” but there are many people in the world who defile that Father’s name. You must understand that the word “Father” carries with it the cries of the prophets who have traversed the altar of blood throughout 6,000 years of history. It contains the elements of the cross. You must recognize that the infinite suffering of our ancestors and the horrific historical connections are present in that name.  
Therefore, if you recognize that the Creator has an unbreakable bond with you as your Father, then that person cannot be taken away by Satan, no matter how strong he may be. No matter how terrifying the fires of hell may be, such a person cannot be melted away.  
Then, where was the reason Jesus became the Messiah? Just as the conviction to be filial to one’s parents can substitute for the history of humanity, Jesus had the determination to abandon humanity for the sake of heaven, and He honored God, the Creator of all things, as His Father, without considering His own prestige or face, whether He would perish or prosper.  
Jesus was not welcomed in His own family and was despised by His own tribe. He was not welcomed by the followers of John the Baptist and was rejected by Judaism and labeled a traitor by the nation of Israel. However, because He realized the mission to resolve the Father’s historical resentment, He did not lose heart even when all of humanity abandoned Him and rejected Him. This is the qualification that Jesus had to become the Messiah. He felt a heart that no one in human history has ever had, a heart that is more deeply rooted in God than in His own flesh and blood.  
Thus, God, who had to conclude the 4,000-year history, was able to forget His own prestige and weep over Jesus when everyone opposed Him. Throughout the 4,000-year history, many prophets have come and gone, but only Jesus truly understood God’s heart.  
In other words, Jesus introduced the laws of heaven to humanity in His life journey. When He felt that God is my Father and that my body can resonate and my blood can flow in that position, and when He looked at all things that seek to establish a connection with God, His sorrowful heart was beyond words.  
The true children of God—heirs of the heart  
Therefore, today, humanity must feel the heart of the meeting that Jesus and God had in a moment to conclude the 4,000-year history, but humanity today does not even think about this. When Jesus was praying in the Garden of Gethsemane, sweating blood, thinking of the betraying nation and the unfaithful altar, the sorrowful heart of Jesus, who was trying to step forward on behalf of the providence of the world, was beyond words.  
In this way, Jesus had a greater love for God than for the denominations, nations, and the world that opposed Him, which allowed Him to possess all the feelings that a human could feel, and because God was greater, He could feel all the feelings that God possessed, which enabled Him to confidently walk the path of Golgotha.  
That is why today, “My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me…”
Let it pass, but not as I will, but as You will. (Matthew 26:39) If we pray with the heart of Jesus who prayed this, then there will be no one who goes to hell. However, just as Jesus appeared with the heart of God's love, there was not a single person who understood Jesus' heart of love at that time. Therefore, Jesus left behind the term "bride and bridegroom" on this earth.

So why has the name of Mary Magdalene remained in Christianity? Why is her name passed down through the ages? It is because Jesus asked for her name to be introduced. Who would accept the fact that a mere lowly woman poured perfume worth 300 denarii on the feet of the young Jesus and wiped them with her hair? Even the disciples laughed at her, and Judas Iscariot protested, with everyone opposing her. Yet, why did Jesus say that the name of Mary Magdalene would be remembered wherever the Gospel is preached? It was because at that moment, her sincerity was equal to the sincerity that Jesus had for God.

When Jesus was crucified, all His disciples fled. However, Mary Magdalene and Jesus' mother went to find His tomb. They also had families and husbands and were bound by the customs of Judaism centered on the Old Testament. Yet, they disregarded all of that and sought the tomb of the dead young Jesus without considering their social status or face. That is why Mary Magdalene was able to meet Jesus.

Then where will the heavenly judgment be decided? It will not be based on how much you have done for heaven. It is not determined by that. Only when God's heart and Jesus' heart are experienced and bear fruit within you, and that becomes an inseparable connection with God and Jesus, will it become a condition for eternal life.

When we think about this, what should all of humanity do today? It is good to pursue the truth that can connect us to God and seek spiritual experiences, but we must also establish a loving relationship that allows us to dwell in the depths of God's heart and connect with Jesus' heart and love. Only then can you stand as the bride of Jesus and as the sons and daughters of God.

However, today we are sorrowful people. The 30 million people of the Republic of Korea should become the people of Israel, but they are not. No matter how many churches there are in this society, there is no church of God, and no matter how many believers there are, they are not the sons and daughters of God. Therefore, what must emerge on this earth? The sons and daughters of God who can save this nation must emerge. The church of God must emerge. The people of God must emerge. Thus, if the path to becoming the sons of God can be opened through the path of tears and abandonment, we should be grateful for that.

Just as the Israelites established a standard and an ideology centered on heaven during the 400 years of oppression in Egypt to unite as a nation and go through an unchanging period of faith before finally meeting a hopeful day, you are also in such a position today. You must also keenly feel that you are living in a land like Egypt today.

Therefore, you must become people who possess the heart of Moses, who fought with animosity against the royal court that despised the chosen people of Israel. We must have the heart of Moses, who did not change his determination made in one day, even while wandering in the wilderness of Midian for 40 years.

**Responsibility to the Three Great Parents**

Now, how should you endure such a long period? It cannot be done with any truth, movement, or ideology of your own. You must look at the nation on behalf of God's heart and possess the heart that Jesus had when He prayed for the nation and the church to settle the fact of the downfall of the Jewish nation. Thus, just like the early church of the Jewish nation, you must be able to hold hands and forget your own circumstances and prestige to step forward on behalf of heaven. Only then will this nation live.

Jesus had a heart that wanted to curse the opposing nation of Israel immediately, but because He felt the heart of God who had endured for 4,000 years, He was able to pray for their blessing instead. In other words, He was able to shed tears and pray for His enemies in the Garden of Gethsemane, on Golgotha, or on the cross.

At that time, Paul, who had Roman citizenship and adhered to all the customs and laws of that country, abandoned his honor and the Judaism he believed in, and found himself in a position of being ostracized from Judaism. Why did this happen? It was because Paul understood the great love of Jesus. Thus, even when he had no place to rely on, no place to belong, and was swept away by the rough waves of life, he forgot his own comfort and spread the words of Jesus.

It was not because of his character that Paul was able to fulfill the duties of an apostle. You must understand that he became Apostle Paul because he had a standard that could resonate with the heart of Jesus Christ, who appeared on behalf of God's love. No matter how much knowledge or wealth one has, it cannot be done with that. Therefore, you must live according to this heavenly law, and your heart and body must move toward it.

We cannot escape the connection with the three great parents of heaven, earth, and humanity. Then how will we repay the grace of these three great parents? Humanity, nations, and peoples that have been indebted until now have all perished. Because there is still a providence to establish such an ideology, the global material fortune is coming to humanity today. The time has come when material will strike humanity. This is because humanity has committed sins before all things by forgetting its position, and there is a need to restore and return this at the end before the world and humanity. Thus, today, humanity is in a position to suffer globally from material pain. Therefore, there must be those who can rise above this material pain. And there must be saints who can connect with the love of God like the early church.

Today, even though the advanced country of the United States operates with democratic principles, if it only cries out for materialism, it will be struck by material. It has come to the time when it must think of ways to use material for all humanity. That is why countries like America provide aid to other countries. However, if they provide aid to gain their own hidden benefits, this will not be tolerated by heavenly principles.

To achieve this ideology, humanity is moving toward a material cultural economic society through a democratic economic society. Therefore, humanity must become a standard-bearer that can assert the original value of material and replace the ideology of its nature, so that the three entities of material, humanity, and heaven can come together.

**Tradition of the Citizens of Heaven**

When we consider all aspects of faith today, we must not have a faith concept that is subservient to material. If there are religious organizations like that, heaven will mobilize conscientious individuals to correct such faith concepts. The time is approaching for that. Also, the consciousness of those who forget heavenly principles and assert their own legitimacy must be corrected.

Since the earth is also an existence, it must have consciousness and a purpose of existence. And since the earth is a creation, it must have a master. That master is God. Therefore, as long as God exists, a world that can move under one ideology will surely be realized.

Additionally, a unified worldview that can dominate all thoughts of humanity must emerge. An ideology centered on the existence of God must be able to dominate the human world, and if it cannot establish relationships between humans and the rich, then God will not fulfill His responsibility as the parent of the earth and humanity. Therefore, all things must move around one center, the earth must move around the ideology of the universe, and humanity must also move around one ideology.

Today, many people are boasting, "I am such a person," "I am a citizen of the country." Today, Americans are boasting that they are citizens of a great nation. However, that cannot last forever. America is living for its own country, but it does not realize that it must live for other countries. Just as the ancient Greek civilization did not know that it existed for Rome, Rome also did not know that its civilization existed for modern civilization through England. Therefore, today, American citizens must understand that while they work for their own country, they must also work for other countries. However, most Americans do not know this. In the midst of this, it is a blessing that some people have the ideology that they should work for heavenly principles rather than just for themselves.

Therefore, now you must equip yourselves with new armaments before the global providence on behalf of heaven. Until now, material civilization has dominated humanity, and the ideology through human reason has dominated the world, but this is not the end. A new ideology that can connect with heavenly nature, Jesus, and the divine ideology, and can channel God's love will surely appear somewhere on this earth.

However, today we do not have any ideology, and our country is not a globally advanced nation. But if this nation can offer itself to God, who can be the last remaining in the heavenly providence, and if it can feel the ideology that can manifest as God's ideology that all humanity relies on and hopes for, then do not be discouraged.

To all of you gathered in the Unification Church today, even though you are sitting in this small church, if you feel that expanding this can represent the world and further represent heaven, then the problem will be solved. Anything can be resolved. You must become citizens of heaven who recognize God as the Lord of this world because you are children who represent God's will. And you must always remember that you cannot deviate from the Father's will.

Among the Bible verses read earlier, there is a saying: "There is no greater love than to love your neighbor as yourself." And it says, "Pray for your enemies." What Jesus advocated is the law we must establish and the traditional customs that the eternal Father's nation should boast of. Moreover, the teachings that Jesus advocated were not limited to that time but were the heavenly laws necessary for the restoration of humanity. Therefore, now, if you want to become sons and daughters of God, you must feel God's love and possess God's love. To do this, since God has fought for 6,000 years to find loving sons and daughters, you must also fight.

**Nine Qualities of the Holy Spirit**

If you want to claim to be of heaven, first enter into the position of God who sheds tears. You will feel the painful historical process that God has gone through, and you too will shed tears. The ears that are listening will also feel the same. The rice you are eating will not go down easily. If you have become someone who can channel the painful heart of heaven, then this nation can live. You must understand that God is looking for such people.

The Bible records the nine fruits of the Holy Spirit: "Love, joy, peace, patience, kindness, goodness, faithfulness, gentleness, and self-control" (Galatians 5:22). These nine qualities of the Holy Spirit are the standards of the kingdom that God advocates, builds, and seeks to establish, and they are the institutions of that society and the ideals of life. Have you ever deeply felt this in your body and mind? If you have such a heartfelt feeling, you will feel the heart of Jesus, who wanted to speak to Jerusalem while holding a stone, but remained silent and endured.

Today, you have entered the Unification Church, but do not desire a Unification Church just for yourselves. Today, our existence is for this nation, and today this nation exists for the world, and the world exists for heaven, and you must understand this. Also, while you may be working hard and offering something at the altar for this purpose, you must understand that God is more pleased with you worrying about this purpose than with providing comfort to Jesus or throwing a feast for Him. You must also understand that God and Jesus are more pleased with you shedding tears for the world while worrying about Jesus' heart.

Jesus demanded that His disciples love the Jewish people more than they loved Him, even if it meant forgetting everything about themselves. This was true of Jesus' life, of Moses, and of God.

Therefore, you who must become filial sons and daughters, loyal subjects, and virtuous women must feel a sense of embarrassment before heaven that you cannot explain. You must also feel your own inadequacy, unable to claim what you have done, and feel remorse before your true nature, and you must fight to become not your own but the Father's. If you become such individuals, history will transition from nations to the world and into the era of heavenly dominion.

Just as humanity is trying to act as the leading force, who can guarantee that heaven will not act as the leading force? As long as heaven exists, the time will surely come when heaven must act as the leading force. Until today, because a standard of human ethics has not been established, heavenly principles have not intervened. When the prestige of heavenly principles stands before human ethics, humanity will not be able to escape from its commands and laws.

Time is passing, and humanity is unaware, so we must reflect once more. Thus, we must pass ourselves through the gate of God's love and become confident individuals who can say, "I absolutely believe in God," and become true sons and daughters who can serve the eternal Father. 

**The Heart of Jesus to Restore All Things**

Matthew 17:1-14

<Prayer> Father, we have come to know that a historical destiny to fulfill the heavenly will is set before us, so please extend Your hand of power to us. Allow only Your will to fill our bodies and hearts, and if there is anyone on this earth who bears any responsibility for heaven, do not allow them to understand that heavenly will with human thoughts. When the heavenly laws and the ideology of resurrection that You have established relate to us, we have come to understand that we can experience the heart of the Father who has been guiding history through the providence. Please allow us to have a heart of love that can connect with the Father’s heart and grant us the understanding of the heart of the Father’s restoration. 
Thus, allow us to understand the heart of the Father who is concerned about this land, and since we are lacking, we ask that You hold us and awaken us to be established as Your people, dear Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.
