We are poor and miserable like beggars, yet we are those who wish to sing feeling the infinite love of the Father, so please command us and guide us. 
At this time, we have the heart to dedicate ourselves to the will of the entire providence, so dear Father, please remove our shortcomings. We earnestly hope and wish for this. 
Thus, please allow only the heart of the Father to dwell deeply in our hearts, and let our bodies experience all the historical feelings of the Father so that we can shed tears of lamentation before the Father, guiding us to truly serve You, which we earnestly hope and wish for. 
We, who have lived in the embrace of Satan for a long time, will cut off all environments related to Satan, so dear Father, please look upon us with compassion at this time. Also, please embrace us once again at this time and manifest the power of life and resurrection. Father, please reveal the hidden words upon the sons and daughters gathered here, and allow the gifts of life to manifest according to Your will, breaking through all conditions of doubt, dear Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.

<Message> Today, I would like to speak to you for a moment under the title ‘The Heart of Jesus to Restore All Things.’ 
Just as you know through the Principle, God’s 6,000-year providential history is a history of restoration. And the purpose of the restoration providence is to find the lost humanity and to reclaim the lost creation, which you have learned well through the Principle. 
You also know well that the term ‘to save humanity’ means to achieve this one purpose, and that the universe has value because it has the conditions to achieve this one purpose. 
115 
The fallen humans’ desire for the ideal of heaven is because they are inherently inclined to long for the ideal of heaven. When I look at myself today, I understand that the happiness and unhappiness in my life are intertwined, and that the infinite and eternal world has both the happiness of heaven and the unhappiness of hell coexisting because humanity has fallen. 
You know well that God’s sorrow for humanity and the coexistence of heaven that Jesus desires and hell that He does not want are inevitable in the process of restoring fallen humanity. 
God created all things and fashioned humanity in His own image. Therefore, humans can be eternal just as God is eternal, and when God feels happiness, humans are created to feel that happiness as well. 
Humans were supposed to rejoice when God rejoices and to grieve when God grieves, yet many among you today do not even know whether God exists or not. Many cannot even think about when God is pleased or when He is saddened. 
Moreover, those who have mourned and labored for heaven have endured their feelings of injustice and resentment even if they had to sacrifice themselves, yet today’s humanity living on this earth cannot even imagine such facts. 
Who can understand the heart of God, who has endured for a long history without abandoning such humans? It is not that humanity has betrayed heaven just once; through the long passage of 6,000 years, humans have rebelled countless times, and as descendants of such ancestors, we are in a position where we cannot lift our heads before heaven. Furthermore, we are beings who are causing sorrow to God’s heart. However, very few people live feeling this. 
How can we make these humans feel the existence of God and the historical heart of the Father, and let them know the path of providence? This has been God’s sorrow towards humanity since the fall. Thus, God chose and established Noah, and He chose and established Moses. Furthermore, after a historical process of 4,000 years, God finally established one person, Jesus, who could reveal the internal and external circumstances of the Father’s providence and the internal and external heart of the Father to humanity. 
Jesus was the one who could only be governed by God, and He was the one with whom God could discuss, and He was the one who understood God’s internal love and heart the best. 
Then, what state is referred to as the fall of humanity? It was the failure to understand God’s circumstances and the failure to understand God’s reality. Therefore, God has been searching for an individual who can communicate His circumstances. And He has worked for 4,000 years to find an individual who can communicate His heart. 
Thus, after 4,000 years, God finally found one person who could communicate His circumstances and discuss His heart, Jesus. However, it was not to end there. He had a fervent wish to let humanity know His circumstances and His heart through Him. This fervent wish of God was supposed to be fulfilled by the mission of the Israelite people, but a historical tragedy occurred because they rejected Jesus. You must understand that this is where the historical rise and fall intersected. 
Therefore, today we must walk the path that can communicate God’s circumstances and walk the path that can communicate God’s heart. By possessing God’s heart and love, we must be able to rejoice when God rejoices and be glad when God is glad. 
As such, you know that Jesus was the one who appeared on this earth representing all humanity, having the nature of creation with the heavenly lineage. 
117 
Jesus came to enable humanity to establish a relationship with God, and He appeared on behalf of God’s circumstances and on behalf of God’s heart. 
Therefore, if the people of that time had united with Jesus, they would not only have been able to know God’s heart and circumstances, but they could have also become friends of Jesus, yet they could not. This one fact has placed history in a position that has not yet been fulfilled. 
What was the heart of God that was sadder than the death of Jesus? God sent Jesus after 4,000 years of effort not to let Him die, but to save humanity. The purpose of sending Jesus was not to complete the spiritual salvation providence through Jesus, but to establish a day when all people on this earth could know God’s circumstances and heart through Jesus and rejoice together with Him. However, because humanity was unbelieving, Jesus had to bear the cross, and God faced the misfortune of having His will frustrated, and as a result, God fell into even greater sorrow. 
Today, there are many people living on this earth, but their circumstances and hearts are all different. The living environments of a thousand people are different, and the living environments of ten thousand people are different. However, we should not head towards a thousand or ten thousand different destinations, but rather we must go towards one place defined by heaven, which is the original nature. Jesus gave up all His circumstances and heart, and appeared before humanity with one will, one heart, and one circumstance to establish the kingdom of God. Yet, each person approached Him with their own myriad of circumstances. However, such people all perished and fell away. When Jesus, whom God had sent after 4,000 years of effort, was crucified, God sent the Holy Spirit again. Thus, the Trinity is working hard to find people who are one with the will of heaven. 
From this perspective, you must understand that Jesus Christ, who came and went 2,000 years ago, was one individual, yet He was the main character of heaven who could represent the past, present, and future. The people of that time did not know this. Jesus was one individual, but He was the embodiment of 4,000 years of history, a sacrificial offering that could resurrect all of humanity, and a vessel of blessing that would last through the ages. 
Yet, who on earth knew this? God sent Jesus to introduce the heart of heaven to humanity, yet not a single person understood this. The humans who were supposed to understand Jesus’ circumstances and those who were supposed to understand God’s circumstances were contrary to Him. Rather, they said, ‘O Jesus! Please accept my circumstances. O God! Please understand my circumstances.’ This was the lamentable act that obstructed the providential course of heaven. 
If the people of that time had communicated with the circumstances and heart of Jesus, who represented God’s circumstances and heart, that is, if Jesus’ heart had become the heart of the Israelite people, Jesus would not have died. Furthermore, if Jesus had not needed to pray in the Garden of Gethsemane before His final death, saying, “Abba, Father! All things are possible for You; take this cup away from Me. Nevertheless, not what I will, but what You will.” (Mark 14:36). 
But who knew that there was 4,000 years of sorrow in Jesus’ heart? Not a single person recognized the sorrowful heart of Jesus, who came to relieve the painful hearts of all humanity. You must understand this. 
Today, you believe in Jesus and pray brazenly, ‘O Lord, come quickly. You have called us friends.’ However, such simple prayers are not enough. You must pray knowing the heart and circumstances of Jesus, who represented the entire restoration providence. 
Thus, you must be able to hear from Jesus, ‘Your heart is my heart, your body is my body, your circumstances are my circumstances, your heart is my heart.’ 
119 
If there had been someone who understood Jesus’ heart at that time, even if the Israelite people opposed Him, and the denominations opposed Him, and the doors and apostles turned away, Jesus could have resolved everything through just one person who understood Him. However, because there was no such person, He could not comfort God’s heart and circumstances on behalf of the earth. 
The Various Sorrows of Jesus
Jesus lived a life where He could not express everything He wanted to say. However, He did not live for His own personal purpose. For over 30 years, He worked as a carpenter and endured hardships, quietly going through the path of sacrifice for His purpose. Thus, from the day He began His three years of public ministry until the moment He died on the cross at Golgotha, He did not live even a single hour for His personal life. He never forgot for a moment that He bore the historical mission of introducing God’s circumstances and heart on this earth. Jesus was the one who wished to convey His heart to the people of that time. 
When He looked at all things, He felt that everything was lamenting, saying, “Please relieve the sorrow bound by the fall of humanity.” Because humanity had left the embrace of God, all creation had also left the embrace of God and had remained in a state of lamentation for 4,000 years, so all creation earnestly longed for Jesus. 
And Jesus was the one who could feel that all things were calling out, “O Lord, please relieve us.” Moreover, Jesus knew that countless spirits had been groaning in the spirit world for 4,000 years, longing for the Messiah who would liberate them, and He knew that He was the one who would fulfill that wish. Furthermore, when He looked at the humanity living in the hellish world of the earth, trapped in the net of death, crying out in misery and longing to be liberated, Jesus lived with an indescribable burning heart. 
You must understand that the Jesus we believe in shed tears for the people of the earth and for the spirits groaning in hell, and He shed tears while contemplating God’s historical circumstances and heart. 
Jesus did not regard even one person merely as an individual. He looked at humanity on behalf of history and on behalf of the ideals of the universe, and the greater the hope for one person, the greater His earnest heart was. 
Jesus felt sorrow when He heard the cries of opposition, but that sorrow was not for His own sake. Jesus realized that it reminded Him of the 4,000 years of opposition to God by Satan. Thus, through that scene, Jesus could feel God’s sorrow. He felt God’s sorrow through all the circumstances where the nation was crying out. Therefore, Jesus felt the indescribable circumstances and heart of God. 
Jesus felt an indescribable sorrow when He realized that God must be comforted through Him, that is, that God, who had worked hard for 4,000 years, should be in a position to rejoice because of Him. 
It is easy to believe in Jesus as testified by the disciples, but it is difficult to believe when standing directly before Jesus. It is easy to trust in the highly regarded Jesus of later generations, but it is difficult to believe in Jesus, who was crucified and labeled as a rebel of Israel. 
Then, where was God’s sorrow regarding Jesus? You must understand that it was bound in the scenes of His being mocked, chased, and nailed. 
The people of that time wanted to hear Jesus’ words, but they did not want to establish those words. In other words, not a single person wanted to practice the intentions of Jesus’ heart in their actual lives. When you think about this, you must feel that heaven is still in a position of sorrow, just as it was then and now. Now, as you are being persecuted in the name of Jesus...
You will understand the situation of Jesus when you see it. And if you experience the suffering that represents heaven, you will come to know the feelings of the wronged Father.  
The filial piety of Jesus towards God  
When Jesus was praying alone in the Garden of Gethsemane, even His three disciples could not stay awake with Him for a single night, yet why did Jesus not rebuke them? It was because He understood the heart of God, who for 4,000 years could not rebuke or judge the many humans who betrayed Him. You must become people who can empathize with the heart of Jesus, which the disciples could not.  
As He was whipped and carrying the cross towards Golgotha, Jesus could have blamed heaven, but He did not because He knew that God had gone through difficulties greater than carrying the cross for 4,000 years to bring about the providence of restoration. He had no room to think of anything else but to reflect on Himself.  
Later, when He was nailed to the cross, with nails in His hands and feet, a crown of thorns on His head, and His side pierced by a spear, Jesus did not blame the disbelieving humans. He understood that being in such a position was the will of the Father, who wished to convey God's situation and heart to all people through Him. Rather, Jesus bowed His head to heaven with a heart full of deep sorrow. Because of this, Jesus was able to become the Messiah before humanity.  
So what did Jesus feel on the cross? He was able to empathize with God's sorrowful heart and situation that had persisted for 4,000 years. It was there that God's heart and Jesus' heart could finally connect. Furthermore, that heart, united emotionally between God and Jesus, could not be severed by anyone. Here, by stepping on the legacy of historical providence, the spirits in the spirit world were able to bring about the resurrection of the growth stage providence, which was not merely a national revolution but a cosmic revolution. Moreover, until that time, even those on earth who believed in the Old Testament and practiced faith could now engage in divine faith through the New Testament. This was a significant transformation.  
Because in the world of substance, God's heart and Jesus' heart could become one embodiment, God was able to establish a direct relationship with Jesus here. In this way, because Jesus could have the same heart as God and be in the same situation on behalf of the earth, God's work could be carried out directly with humans at its center. You must once again recognize Jesus, who came as a substantial human with a universal mission.  
Now you must pray with the same heart that Jesus had when He prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane. Even though humans should undergo sacrifices greater than Golgotha, today people pray, “Oh God! Please accept this little effort of mine,” when they have done a little work, and when they experience a little of their own situation and sorrow, they pray, “Oh God! Please take care of my situation and comfort me.” When we see this, we can understand that God's heart and the hearts of humans are in opposing directions.  
Many believers stand in such a position today. It was the same during Jesus' time. The disciples who followed Jesus thought that He would be satisfied with just the twelve of them and believed they were the entirety of His desire. The people of Israel mistakenly thought that God's will could be fulfilled solely through their nation. The Jewish sect believed that their denomination alone could completely fulfill God's will. However, Jesus did not think that way. Jesus had the idea of fulfilling His will centered on Himself, which would transcend nations and reach the eternal world, yet the twelve disciples who appeared before Him thought that God's will could be fulfilled entirely through them. You must understand that the historical misfortunes and sorrows of humanity arose from this.  
The disbelief and ignorance of the disciples  
Jesus knew that He had a mission to restore not only individuals but also families, societies, nations, and even the infinite spirit world. Therefore, when Jesus searched for individuals, it was for the sake of finding nations, and when He searched for nations, it was for the sake of finding the world. And the efforts He has made for 2,000 years until today were to make the entire universe a place governed by God. Yet, people did not know this fact. Consequently, Jesus could not express God's deep heart and will to the crowds that appeared before Him, who were to realize the universal plan. You must understand that Jesus was in such a dire situation.  
That is why Jesus said, "I have much more to say to you, but now you cannot bear it." (John 16:12)  
Jesus was burning with a sense of universal mission to represent God's providence to restore the entire world, yet the humans of that time did not understand Him.  
So what about you today? Are there people who claim, "I have believed in Jesus for decades. I am a pastor. I am an elder. God must surely know me"? If such a person exists, they should bow their heads and weep before God. Who would have known that the Israelite nation, which boasted of its chosen people for 4,000 years, would fall? Who would have known that even the twelve apostles, who shared joys and sorrows with Jesus during His three years of public life, would disbelieve Him? No one knew.  
Then why did this contradictory history unfold? It was because Jesus' concepts and hopes differed from those of His disciples. That is why the disciples disbelieved Jesus.  
Have you ever felt the sorrowful heart of humans who were in darkness, praying to heaven, "Please liberate them"? Or have you heard the cries of billions of spirits in the spirit world lamenting? Jesus heard them. Jesus wept, knowing that the judgment of sulfur fire would pour down at the end of human history. But have you ever felt the situation of Jesus, who could not defend Himself while being dragged here and there in dire circumstances?  
In this age, when we must lead the destiny of Christianity in a new direction, it is fine if we have nothing. Knowing or not knowing is not the issue. You who have gathered here today! There is only one thing: even if this body is torn and trampled, you must be able to represent God's situation and heart.  
If there is someone among you who is willing to die to represent God's heart, the entire universe will weep with you. Forming a bond of tears that cannot be severed, and if you can empathize with that heart of tears, you will not mind the path of death. When Jesus came to this earth to represent such sorrow and fell, the entire heaven and earth became dark. Heaven and earth could understand Jesus' heart. However, humans did not understand His heart. Thus, Jesus could not avoid the path of the cross.  
That is why today, before praying for your sons and daughters, you must first pray for the historical ancestors who have labored until now in the heavenly realm. You must have a heart that wishes for humanity on this earth to live well before hoping for your own well-being. Before I dance, I must be able to look at and care for all people who are in the realm of lamentation. You must also have a heart that can represent the situation of Jesus, who could not show joy even when He was joyful. In this end time of human history, one person must appear on this earth to block the sorrow of God and Jesus and to block the sorrow of the universe.  
The hope of Jesus  
Now you must say, "It is fine even if I am despised and oppressed!" The figure of our Lord, who said, "It is finished" (John 19:30) and passed away silently, was the image of our Bridegroom. In the future, there will be no need for any signs or denominations. It will not matter if individuals are different or if nations are different; a true ideal world will come.  
The hope of Jesus is the hope that represents the ideals of the entire universe, and the mission of Jesus was to restore all things in the universe. You must now understand that the apostles of old did not understand this will of Jesus.  
You must comfort the fact that the first Israelite nation, the Jewish people, could not comfort the heart of Jesus, so that this nation can appear as the second Israelite nation.  
Jesus came to this earth seeking an individual who could believe forever, but He could not find such an individual. Therefore, God sent the Holy Spirit to find people who could believe secondarily through the Holy Spirit in today's Christianity. Thus, the era of salvation through the name of Jesus alone has passed.  
Ideals can resonate with all people, but the substance can only resonate with one. Therefore, there are many who claim to believe in ideals, but there are not many who claim to believe in substance. There is no believer who can say, "Your heart is my heart, and my heart is your heart, and your sorrow is my sorrow."  
Have you felt the heart of heaven's resentment that has been accumulated until this day, the sorrowful heart that feels as if your bones are melting? You must understand that Jesus spent over 30 years on this earth with a heart that lost consciousness and fainted in relation to heaven wherever He went.  
Therefore, today you are in a position where you must pass through the gateway of judgment centered on a single day. Who will guarantee this path of judgment? Jesus will not guarantee it. God cannot guarantee it either. Just as the path of ancient Israel was not guaranteed by Jesus or God, the path of the Christians at the end of time will not be guaranteed by Jesus or God. You must clearly understand this.  
So who will be guaranteed? Only those who can feel God's situation and heart and the extraordinary heart that Jesus had, who wished to embrace all humanity, will be able to receive guarantees from God and Jesus.  
Today, people who believe in Jesus think that salvation is achieved to the extent that they believe and that the entire kingdom they demand is built, but that is an absurd thought. When they go to the spirit world, it is not like that. Those who boast that they are the best find themselves in a pitiful position in the spirit world. What is the reason for this? You must understand that while you may seem to be on the right path today, if you are even slightly off course at the starting point, you will end up millions of miles away from the destination of eternal life.  
So what can connect this? It is not our logical knowledge or any doctrine. It is a heart that can love God. You must be able to say that God's heart is my heart, and my heart is God's heart, and there must be a gravitational pull of heart that draws each other. Only then will God's ultimate emotional focal point and my emotional focal point connect. Here, we can say that God is the Alpha and the Omega centered on love.  
Today is the time to dedicate our lives to fulfilling the wishes of Jesus. 2,000 years ago, Jesus was rejected by individuals because no one came to fulfill His grief, rejected by families because no families came forth, rejected by societies and churches because no one came from those, and rejected by nations because no nations came forth.  
However, you must understand that Jesus, while being rejected and oppressed, has fought to fulfill the heavenly will even to the stage of the world today, transcending individuals, families, churches, and nations. Therefore, Christianity has not been welcomed by any nation or people since its early missionary days because the path Jesus walked was a path of rejection.  
What we must understand, empathize with, and restore  
Therefore, today, while you may comfortably sit with a Bible by your side, singing hymns or praying, thinking you will go to heaven, it is not so. The fact that you can be in such a position and receive heavenly grace is due to the efforts of heaven, which has been rejected and trampled for 2,000 years, coming back around to find you. And it is thanks to the many historical ancestors of faith who have pioneered despite being rejected to establish us. Therefore, you must understand that today, as we face the end times, there remains a mission to save the world even if we must sacrifice. You must empathize with this.  
Even if you do not know every detail of the historical process that has passed, you must have only one thing: the heart of Jesus, who came to restore the entire universe. And you must have the determination to embrace the world and fight with the heart of Jesus.  
God endured for six days while all creation was mocked by enemies because He had a heart that could love even His enemies. Thus, He has endured through the long historical process of 6,000 years. Until He has passed through the period of creation that took six days, God has been patient and has embraced creation.  
Because humanity, created in six days, fell, God has been shedding tears of sorrow for 6,000 years, laboring until the day He can find a person to love. In other words, God has been enduring until today, hoping for the appearance of a human who can receive His love and resolve historical resentment.  
However, there has not yet appeared a being on this earth who can bear such a heart and will of God. That is why, although it has already been 2,000 years since Jesus came and went, He is still fighting in the heavenly realm on behalf of the 6,000-year history.  
The day when a being who can represent the heart of Jesus comes to this earth and connects humanity with God will be the day of the Second Coming.  
In the not-so-distant future, when all creation will be caught in the resentment that cannot escape judgment, you will hear the cries of humanity. "Oh! Save me! Please remove the resentment of restoration from us," will be the voices of prayer you will hear. Not only all creation but also the 2.4 billion people on this earth will hear that cry.  
Furthermore, billions of spirits in the spirit world will cry out, "Oh! Brothers and sisters on earth!"
"Please grant us the resolution of our historical grievances." You must become those who can hear this prayer's voice. Thus, you must understand God's circumstances, who has sought humanity for 6,000 years and has worked hard for it.

So now, what must you restore? You must restore all things that are within the realm of lamentation, restore all of humanity, and even restore the spirits in hell. Then what comes next? You must restore God's sorrowful heart to a heart of joy.

Who has torn apart the sorrowful heart of the Father, who has been wounded for 6,000 years? The question is, who will heal the torn heart of the Father and become sons and daughters who can be the objects of Heaven's love? It must be you. Humanity has inflicted wounds on God's heart for 6,000 years and has violated God's heart for 6,000 years. Therefore, you must understand that Jesus is still appealing for humanity to resolve all grievances regarding this celestial nature.

The good people on Heaven's side have lived with an indescribable sorrowful heart and a heart that is torn apart, holding onto Heaven's will while living in hunger. Jesus lived that way 2,000 years ago as well.

Become the warriors of Heaven who are prepared to die.
In the past, when Jacob was fleeing from his brother Esau to establish the foundation of Israel and was sleeping with a stone as a pillow in the wilderness, and during his time living as a shepherd in his uncle Laban's house, what kind of heart did Jacob have? Jacob sought to have a heart of love like God's love for his kin. He tried to inherit God's heart, which had loved and cared for his kin for 2,000 years. Thus, he worked hard to resolve the deep sorrow of Heaven that had been accumulated. There was a period of suffering to transfer God's sorrowful heart to Jacob.

Today, do not be discouraged by the trials you face. Because of the opposition to Jesus, the foundation of blessing that the Israelite people had built over 4,000 years has been transferred to those who believe in Jesus in later generations. When you stand with God's heart today and face opposition, do not be discouraged. Opposition will eventually pass, but the blessings of those who oppose will be transferred to you. When Jesus came to this earth, those who tried to harm the true from the false were all broken and scattered and disappeared. There has never been a case in history where one who has endured and triumphed has not faced opposition.

Therefore, you must have confidence in your heart and body, and have conviction in your actions as you live your faith. If you do so, God will comfort you when you are in pain. Furthermore, you will become those who can feel God's true love.

No matter how great the power of Satan may be, it cannot swallow or digest God. When it tries to digest and fails, it rather falls away. No matter how great a person may be in the world, if there is no denomination that can practice and digest the power of Satan with the ideology and conviction centered on Heaven's will, the world will fall to Satan. This is what Jesus claimed. Because there remained conditions on earth that prevented Satan from swallowing Jesus, He was resurrected.

Now, children who can absorb the ideals of the universe must emerge. After understanding the heart of Jesus, who must restore all things, you must not yield even a single root of a tree on this earth to Satan.

My body and my life belong to the Father, and all the material possessions I have also belong to the Father. This nation, this world, and this heaven and earth all belong to the Father. Therefore, you must become heavenly heroes who can return all that was lost due to the Fall back to the Father so that Jesus Christ can reign on this earth for a thousand years.

Now, you, members of the Unification Church, must have a determination that no believer has had until now. You must be prepared to die and move forward. In the process of moving toward Heaven's will, if you claim to understand the historical providence, you cannot have the conditions that anyone in history could have had. You must create conditions that can be achieved in environments that seem impossible. Today, we must do what others cannot do, so that future generations will not fail to fulfill Heaven's will.

Just as the staff that was heard by Moses struck the Red Sea, Jesus hoped that people would emerge who could deeply feel His life and become that staff. 7) What Will God Do with the Oppressed Humanity?
Matthew 10:16-42
The title I wish to speak to you about at this time is "What Will God Do with the Oppressed Humanity?" I will speak briefly on this topic.

The Reality of Humanity in Oppression
Among you gathered here today, there is likely no one who can boast that they are happy or joyful. Each of you will admit that while your heart and body are yours, you cannot stand in the place of your heart or body. In other words, my heart is not in the position of an eternal heart, and my body is not a body where the heart can dwell forever.

If there is someone who can confidently say they have lived centered on their heart, they would be considered a success in the journey of life within this universe. However, in all of history, there has not been a single person who has claimed to have done everything according to their own heart, who has made such a claim with confidence.

You will also feel that this is not the case.

What Will the Future World Be Like?

When you realize that you are a sinner who cannot be accepted before heavenly principles, and that you are a self who cannot be accepted before principles and human ethics, what should you do? The desire for humanity to move in unity with their hearts centered on their wishes has been a deep hope throughout history and is being urged by heaven and earth. While this is fortunate for humanity, the fact that it has come to be is something that cannot help but be sad.

Even if someone is in a position of power and glory socially, if they cannot unify their heart and body, they must realize that they are an unhappy person.

Our hearts are connected to the intangible heaven, and our bodies are closely related to the tangible earth, and you must acknowledge that while my existence is exceedingly small, the hearts and bodies we possess are connected to a vast and grand world. You must feel that your body and heart, though small, are connected to something exceedingly great, and that your surrounding environment urges you to establish a relationship with the world of heavenly principles with your heart and with the ideal historical world that will come in the end times with your body.

You must particularly reflect on the question of what kind of being you are before heaven and earth. You need to think about this.

Even if today you have peace and joy in your heart, for it to be eternal, each of you must create an eternal environment of joy and happiness on this earth, which you have not achieved.

Now we must overcome these obstacles and allow our bodies and hearts to unite, seeking the joy of establishing a relationship between the ideals our hearts desire and the ideals our bodies wish for. If we do this, you will enjoy eternal blessings in heaven.

The center of the heavenly principles requires that the center of the heart can engage with the heavenly principles, and the question is how to establish a connection with the center of the heavenly principles. This is a problem that you must resolve. God is always concerned about this issue.

Now, where should your hearts go? First, you must unify your body and heart from within yourselves to represent heaven and earth. And even if you possess such abilities, you must not seek only your own happiness but must seek the happiness of the whole.

If you cannot do that, you must reflect and critique your past. You must also analyze yourself concerning the future.

A universal success
You must reach a standard where your heart and body can unite centered on your individual self and can fulfill the will of providence. If you know this path and live according to the will of providence, you will feel happiness. By reflecting your body in your heart, your body's movements can follow your heart, allowing you to claim to represent heavenly principles. If you are recognized as such, you can enjoy joy and establish a loving relationship with God, centered around heavenly principles.

Therefore, you must have the strength to overcome any elements on this earth, uniting your heart as the priority so that your heart and body can be one. Thus, you must become someone who can find a safe position in any circumstance. These people will form families, build churches, establish nations, and ultimately create a world united with God Himself, and you must understand that this is God's will.

Thus, now is not the time to cry because you have no money, nor is it the time to weep because you lack honor and power. No matter how complete those external conditions may be, they cannot be the conditions that will make you eternally happy. However, looking back at the historical path, many have fought with tears and risked their lives to secure such external conditions, but very few have fought with tears and risked their lives for internal conditions.
So who is Jesus? Jesus is the one who shed tears and fought with His life to establish internal conditions, blocking and stopping external conditions. 

When you come to believe in a religion, the first thing you feel is that a battle is taking place within your heart. In that battle, what is the enemy? It is the body. 

If one can win the struggle centered on such an individual, and possess a body united with a heart that is one with the heavenly principles, that person will be a universal success. 

God's heavenly law is an unchanging principle, and if one becomes a heart that can harmonize with this heavenly law, and if the body is transformed to become one with that heart, then there is nothing on earth that can change such a transformed being. 

Today, we have been engaged in an incredibly fierce struggle to establish external conditions, and it is essential that we also engage in a struggle to establish internal conditions, which are the center of these external conditions. In this regard, we must understand that without an intense struggle today that is incomparable to external conditions, there is no way to initiate an internal revolution that can correct all these external realities. What we should be concerned about now is not the external world, but the internal world. 

However, until now, we have sought leaders to find external conditions in our own life paths, sought friends in external fields, and tried to establish our ideals in external environments, but all of these are not eternal. 

We must recognize that our individual selves are in a position of conflict between the world pursuing external conditions and the world pursuing internal conditions. Heaven knows this, and you must understand that you have come forth on this historical path, walking the way that others dislike while avoiding the way that others like, for the sake of all humanity in your sorrowful position. You must realize that you are individuals, yet not merely individuals. You must recognize that this form of reality exists within you. 

So, have you had a day when your heart and body became one, allowing you to demand from heaven? Heaven will question you about this. 

The posture that the saints of the end times must take is that in the world of establishing external conditions, one cannot avoid going through the historical path of being pushed and oppressed. Therefore, in these end times, you will be swept away into an era of apocalyptic fear that you do not even recognize. 

Why does this phenomenon occur? It is because to strike the external center and unify it with the internal center, social conditions, habitual conditions, or cognitive conditions must be ruthlessly discarded as they threaten the internal conditions. Thus, one becomes engulfed in fear without even realizing it. 

In such times, what does Jesus require of the saints of the end times? He emphasizes that we must block external conditions and establish internal conditions. Today, if you have friends or teachers in the world, you must analyze whether they are friends or teachers centered on external ideals or those centered on internal ideals. You should also pay attention to whether denominations, nations, or the world flow in the direction of forming external connections or internal connections. 

As we face these end times, before seeking any leader on this earth, you must first seek your original heart. To find this, Christianity seeks to sever all external ties through prayer and enter into God's heart, while Buddhism seeks to find the original human heart from 6,000 years ago through meditation. 

We must understand that this is a historical tragedy for humanity. 

To those of you here! Is there anyone who claims based on the body? This is treason against heavenly principles. Why? Because humanity has never once boasted before the universe that the body and heart have united. In other words, there has never been a moment when the heart and body became one, nor when the Creator and I became one. As beings who have not had the time to unite heart and body, how can you dare to boast before heaven while living centered on the body? Heaven cannot tolerate this. Those who boast of what heaven does not acknowledge will also face judgment. Originally, one must first become a true heart and body that heaven can boast about, and only then can all things boast. 

Today, you say you have set out to find heaven and are wandering in search of the truth. However, even if there is a truth that represents heaven and earth, in order to relate to that truth, your heart and body must first become one, so that when the heart is sad, the body is sad, and when the body is sad, the heart weeps together. You must have that day. If you cannot experience this in your faith journey, you must understand that you will never stand before heavenly principles. 

Now, as the time to fulfill heavenly principles draws near, the human heart becomes anxious and thirsty, unknowingly relating to the will of heaven. Thus, even if a country like America lives in economic and social abundance, the number of people committing suicide is increasing exponentially due to the anxiety and thirst of the heart. 

So now, what should I prioritize in my heart? If there is an inexplicable sadness in your heart, you must recognize that it is your teacher. As the judgment of the end times approaches, the heart can sense this, leading to an unintentional sadness. Therefore, if you feel loneliness and impatience in your heart, you must strive to become a body that can be a friend to that heart. This applies not only to individuals but also to nations. 

If there is a nation on this earth that can represent heavenly principles, that nation will be thrust into a more miserable environment than any other nation, and similarly, there must be such individuals who emerge. You must recognize that you are in such a position now. And as this phenomenon unfolds globally, there will also come a time when, regarding your individual selves, you must strike the body three times centered on the heart. However, fallen humanity is spiritually dull and does not know this. Yet heaven has a mission to ensure that humanity is made aware of the time of heavenly principles. It must be made known at least three times, whether through the heart of a person or through revelation. 

However, the human body stands in opposition to the heart. The heart is internal, while the body is external; there is no one who would say that the heart is false and the body is true. Therefore, only those who strike and subdue their bodies centered on their hearts can experience a new world of ideals. This does not only happen within individuals but also occurs centered on denominations. 

In the world, there are countless religions and denominations, but there is not a single church that fully aligns with God's will. If there is a heaven, it must establish the center of truth and create relationships between the internal and external realms based on that center. Additionally, as a phenomenon of the end times, struggles between denominations will arise. Any religion or anything else starts from the individual and unfolds in the order of family, denomination, nation, and world. Nations have both internal and external dualities, and the world is divided into left and right. Originally, these should be one. 

You, who long for the original world and hope for heavenly ideals, must not allow history to be ruined by failing to overcome difficulties when others persecute you in whatever environment they may be. 

You must unite centered on your hearts, first building an internal foundation, and then seeking an external foundation. Thus, you must transcend your individual selves centered on God to find family, society, nation, and world, and ultimately reach for heaven and earth. 

So, what is the most important issue for humans seeking one world and one ideal? It is not the ideology of a nation or world that exists for a time and then disappears. No matter how much power or status one has, that is not what is important. The issue is the ideology and the protagonist that can unify the two worlds. 

When considering humanity, there is the internal world centered on the heart and the external world centered on the body. Just as the world is divided into these two realms, the spiritual world also has the realm of goodness governed by heaven and the realm of evil governed by Satan. 

Do you know that the culmination of God's 6,000-year providence lies within my body? A person without a principle that can unify body and heart cannot lead or govern humanity. This is the crux of the matter. It is not a problem of the absence of God or the absence of Jesus. The first problem is that I have not become one. 

Every person has two paths. One is the path leading to the world, and the other is the path of abandoning the world and heading toward heavenly principles. This is reflected in the materialistic worldview that advocates external ideals and the idealistic worldview that advocates internal ideals. 

So when will these two worldviews become one? Where will the adjustment to unify them begin? This is a significant task. 

When God governs this created world, He also faces two worlds. There is the world of the heart that God engages with and the world of the body. Thus, we must understand that God is hoping for a person on this earth who can unify the two directions in which He governs. 

God has demands through the internal realm and through the external realm, and we must recognize that the day will come when the world of the internal realm absorbs the world of the external realm, and that is the purpose of God's providence. 

For this reason, the more revolutions there are in religions that uphold the will of providence today, the more they are developing. The more they are struck, the more they prosper. This is the history of heavenly restoration and indemnity. The first to strike loses according to heavenly principles. In the First World War, the side that struck first lost, and in the Second World War, the side that struck first also lost. Therefore, in the Third World War, the side that strikes first will also lose. 

People in the world often like to strike first. However, those who strike first will not be tolerated by heaven. Today, even in the church, people enjoy slandering and criticizing others, but those who strike first will never be tolerated by heaven. 

Why must the Lord return? 

Today, among many people, there are many who worry about the world, but few worry about their own hearts and the inability of their bodies to become one. 

To the members of the Unification Church gathered here! You should be concerned about the nation and the world, but first, you must worry about the fact that your individual selves have not united heart and body. It is those who have united heart and body that gather together to form a nation and a world, which is what God truly desires for us. If God's wish is such, then even when worrying about the world, He hopes that such people gather to worry, and when worrying about the nation, He hopes that such people gather to worry. This is the true attitude of believers. For this purpose, Jesus came, but He could not fulfill that wish and returned, so He wishes to come again to fulfill that purpose. 

So what is the purpose that the Lord will fulfill upon His return? Is He coming back to judge this world with fire? No, that is not the case. God can do the judging with fire without Jesus coming. So why does He come? Jesus comes as the center who can represent God's internal and external providence, aiming to establish a point of unity and create a flat relationship. 

Now, as we have reached the end of the age, when you have taken responsibility for such a will of God, just as the human heart has been ruthlessly violated by the body, and just as all figures who have pioneered the internal realm in the past have been violated and opposed by the external, if you proclaim the Lord for the world, you will be struck by the world; if you proclaim for the nation and the people, you will be struck by the nation and the people; if you proclaim for the denomination, you will be struck by the denomination. 

In a fallen world, it is easy to drive away those who weep for the world, and when one weeps for the nation and people, it is easy for the nation and people to drive away such a person, and it is easy to drive away those who weep for the denomination. 

The one who comes to unify the internal and external realms and restore the original form of the world is referred to as the Lord of the Second Advent in Christianity, the Maitreya Buddha in Buddhism, and the True Person in Confucianism, each religion giving different names. However, in reality, this is merely speaking of the one returning Lord that all religions anticipate. 

So who was Jesus in the past? When viewed from the perspective of the individual, He represented Adam; when viewed from the perspective of the tribe, He represented Jacob; when viewed from the perspective of the nation, He represented Moses; and furthermore, when viewed from the perspective of the world, He came bearing the responsibility of representing all humanity. Moreover, He came to this earth carrying not only the world but also the sorrow of heaven within His heart. So who will spend their life weeping personally for the Jesus who came and went so pitifully? Jesus will seek such a person. God will also seek such a person. 

Fallen humanity seems to be born in joy, but when leaving, they go with tears. However, now, those who weep for the pitiful nation will receive blessings for the nation, and those who weep for the pitiful denomination will receive blessings for the denomination. And those who weep for the pitiful world will receive blessings for the world. 

So, South Korea! This pitiful nation, which has been divided since liberation and has longed for unification, has not yet achieved it. Rather, it has been torn apart by mutual distrust among the same people. Yet, it is a pitiful nation that does not recognize the impending judgment like the falling autumn leaves. So what should we do in such times? We must seek the roots that do not change even in autumn. There, everything will be different in shape, color, and all aspects from the world we have seen until now.

So where is the flock that can bring joy to God and Jesus? If you truly want to become the true flock, you must be able to hear the voice of the true shepherd.

The eyes that look upon the spirits in hell in the spiritual world are filled with a sense of responsibility to relieve the grievances of the spirits in paradise. When looking at the earth on behalf of God's sorrow, and witnessing the chosen people of Israel and all of humanity opposing Him without a bond with Him, the gaze of Jesus was one that represented the sorrow of God, who had mourned for 4,000 years since the fall of Adam and Eve. 

How could the chosen people of Israel, who were to receive heavenly blessings and live eternally with Jesus as family or household, instead oppose Him? Today, you must become friends of Jesus, who could not speak to the opposing Israel, and who mourned for their ignorance while holding onto the temple. Are your eyes the eyes that Jesus desires? The eyes of Jesus were those that looked upon the sorrow of God, and they were also the eyes that recognized the circumstances in which the restoration of paradise and the earth needed to take place, as well as the eyes that saw that even hell must receive benefits through Him. 

And do you have your ears opened? The ears of Jesus heard the voice of God coming from heaven and the cries of countless spirits in sorrow. When He heard the sounds of lamentation and cries that were directed at Him, you must understand that Jesus found Himself in a position where He could not have a peaceful day. Moreover, when He looked upon the earth, He saw evil trampling upon good and even betraying heaven, and He heard the cries of the nations. Thus, Jesus felt a sense of mission not only to resolve the grievances of heaven but also to lead even those who opposed Him to repentance. 

Furthermore, what did He speak with His own mouth? He spoke new words in the midst of paradise and hell. He sought to lead the spirits of paradise into heaven and even defended the spirits in hell. He shouted words meant to bring the invisible world and the spirits in paradise into heaven, that is, words to resurrect the spirits of paradise. He even spoke words that defended the spirits in hell, including Satan. Therefore, His words were conditions to resolve the grievances of the spiritual world and were also words meant to liberate humanity on earth, who were bound by the death rights of Satan. 

These words of liberation should have been welcomed on earth, but instead, they faced opposition. How could this happen? As a result, they could not establish a bond with heaven. 

What about His hands and feet? Those hands that were laid upon the sick! Those hands that brought the dead back to life! Those hands that shared bread with the hungry! And His feet, which were driven from village to village, from valley to valley, praying for His enemies despite being pursued by the opposing people of Israel and Satan. Moreover, those hands that blessed His enemies and those feet that were nailed to the cross. 

What about the body of Jesus? His body was one that could not have a day of rest wherever it went. Everything He saw did not align with the heavenly principles, and everything He heard was in conflict with the heavenly principles, so He was always under pressure. Thus, He could not find a place to lay His head, nor could He have a day of rest where He could feel secure. You must understand that Jesus' body was one that was not welcomed wherever it went. Because of this, even though He had much to say, He could not express it all. He could not speak heavenly words before those who could not understand earthly words. Eventually, Jesus was branded a traitor before the nations. The entire religious community and the ruling power at that time did not welcome Him. 

However, He developed a strategy to unite with the masses. Heaven is unfolding a dual strategy. Therefore, while it seemed like He was yielding on the front lines, it ultimately led to Satan working for Him. 

For this reason, in the history of the world, those who struck first have lost more than 80% of the time. In both World War I and World War II, the side that struck first was defeated. When you understand this principle, you can immediately discern which side is Satan's in today's spiritual battle. You can tell by what they are fighting for. If they are not fighting for the whole but for themselves or trying to sacrifice the whole for themselves, then they are on Satan's side. 

Jesus, who is responsible for the first line, and the Holy Spirit, who is responsible for the second line. 

So, who is God? From one perspective, it may seem like I am the sacrifice, but the one who sacrifices for me is God. If humans give for heaven, heaven will give all the ideals of the universe to humanity. The world of Satan, on the other hand, will take away even my life and ultimately lead me to eternal hell, taking back the ideals that were given. However, if I fight while receiving accusations from Satan, it will become a gain for heaven. That is why there are those who go to heaven. Since Satan is in a position where the more he goes out, the less he can turn back, he is in a position where he must yield here. 

Jesus had to fight on all fronts. However, due to the failure of the primary providence, He established a secondary purpose and carried out providence centered on the altar of sacrifice and service. Thus, even until today, He is constructing paradise while being pursued and chased. In the end, those things will become the front lines of Satan and the front lines of God, creating confusion that neither you nor I can comprehend. Therefore, you must become someone who can find the first line of God's work here. 

Only then can you have the authority of heaven to strike down Satan and start anew as a new front line. God sent the Holy Spirit because Jesus could not fulfill His responsibilities on this earth. What is the Holy Spirit? It is the one who is responsible for the second line. The Holy Spirit is the one who is responsible for the truth of the cross. Then who is responsible for the first line? Jesus is responsible for it, confronting Satan. Therefore, today, when we follow Jesus and the Holy Spirit, they too will establish a new front line. Thus, today, we must equip ourselves with a new second line in place of the Holy Spirit, so that we can block Satan and become true soldiers of God. Only then can we overcome Satan and reveal his true nature. This is something that neither God, Jesus, nor the Holy Spirit can do for us. 

When that happens, such qualified individuals can become friends of God's heart, friends of Adam before the fall, and become those who can govern the archangels and all creation. You must understand that God is seeking such a person. Each of you must fulfill your mission from your respective positions. Whether in religion or science, heaven is calling for those who can stand as true sons of God from such perspectives. 

In the end, we cannot judge others. We stand at the crossroads of life and death, where the question is where we must go to receive heaven's recognition. Therefore, if a nation can gather conscientious individuals and build walls to fight on behalf of heaven, that nation can represent God's overall sovereignty. 

Do not envy countries like America today. Do not envy any great civilized nation. The question is how much we can establish connections with heaven and earth within the principles of heavenly law. No matter how good the external conditions may be, there will come a time to settle accounts. God is a being with profound indignation, but He is not merely a God of indignation. Deep within that indignation lies a foundation of righteousness that Satan cannot fathom. Because there is a standard of righteousness that allows Satan to eventually submit, he finds himself in a position where he must yield. 

Human responsibility.

Only then can you truly understand God's heart.

Only from there can a new heavenly history unfold. 

God approaches humanity with infinite heart, but humans only consider their own perspective, as if it were the entirety of heaven, that is, 360 degrees, leading to a misunderstanding. The time that distinguishes this difference is the day of judgment. How will heaven's love be manifested on this earth? A static ideal and our hearts must unite forever without deviation. Thus, we must be able to turn eternally in 360 degrees, and only when we can unite within the realm of one ideal, not two, can God feel secure and at rest. Now, you must become individuals who can forsake the desires of the external world and instead embody God's heart. Even if you face thousands or tens of thousands of people, you must be able to feel God's heart through them. In other words, you must become someone who can see God's heart through any person. 

To truly become such individuals, even if you face sorrow, you must be able to surpass the greatest sorrow, and even if you face anger, you must overcome a greater anger than that of heaven and earth. Moreover, when the heart of indignation against Satan erupts, you must harbor the intention to one day bring down that Satan, enduring to secure even one more person or one more comrade. When you pray before heaven with such a heart, you must be certain that heaven can connect with you from a new ideological standpoint that transcends the history of sin. 

Let us understand the heart of the resurrected Jesus. 

Mark 16:1-20 

This day marks the day of resurrection when Jesus, who came and went 2,000 years ago, rose again. Even until today, there have been many Christians in this world, but when considering that they do not even know the day of His resurrection, you should reflect on how frustrating and sorrowful heaven's heart must be towards humanity who does not know this day of resurrection. 

The heart of Jesus towards heaven and His desire for humanity. 

And you who are here must celebrate this day, which no one knows on behalf of heaven and all humanity, and you must become His internal and external friends who feel the heart of Jesus Christ at this time. In that sense, you should feel that this one place where you are sitting today is a precious place given by heaven, earth, and all creation. 

I remember 13 years ago today when Jesus appeared and revealed that today is the day of His resurrection. 

What kind of person did Jesus wish to be for all humanity? And what kind of person does heaven wish for us to be? Jesus came to this earth as a bridegroom, but because the people on earth could not accept Him as a bride, the bride and bridegroom had to be separated. Knowing this fact, you can also understand that heaven hopes for you to become a bride who can feel the unspoken heart of Christ on behalf of all humanity. 

Jesus knew that He had the great responsibility to fulfill the purpose of God's 4,000-year providence and to atone for the sins of humanity that had accumulated over 4,000 years with all His heart and sincerity. Therefore, He lived a life of internal and external sorrow and suffering more than anyone else in history. 

What Jesus desired was the restoration of the created world, and the target of His message was the people of the world who must accomplish that work together. Therefore, Jesus expressed God's earnest heart to humanity and urged them to fulfill His will, but the people of that time did not accept or recognize Him. As a result, the ones who accepted Jesus' words could not exceed a limited scope. Furthermore, even within that limited scope, He could not speak freely. We must become those who sympathize with and mourn for the heart of Jesus who struggled in such an environment. 

After enduring three years of suffering, the time should have come for Him to be welcomed by all humanity, yet not a single person acknowledged Him as the Son of God who represented God's will. Even the family of Joseph, who should have recognized Him, did not, nor did the Jewish community or the nation of Israel, and ultimately the world opposed Him. 

Even when Jesus was in a position of being opposed by everyone, He was in a position to comfort heaven, which was mourning, while looking upon the land of disbelief. He was also in a position to be concerned about the earth and even blessed the unbelieving people until the moment He died on the cross. You must understand the heart of Jesus. 

If you truly wish to become the bride of Jesus, you must understand the heart of the Jesus who came and went, you must atone for the sins of your ancestors, and you must become someone who can embody the heart of the Lord in your life. 

And if there is no one on this earth who knows the sorrow of heaven and the sorrow of Jesus, then you who are here must strive to possess that ideal and heart. If there exists someone on this earth who possesses the heart that Jesus held, they will not know where to place themselves and will weep in sorrow. Even though there is a 2,000-year temporal gap between such a person and Jesus, it is the same heart that beats within them.

The disciples who had to inherit the will of Jesus

So what should you do? You should have the same humble and reverent heart that Peter had after the resurrection of Jesus, and you should strive to resemble the heart of Mary Magdalene, who was struggling and wandering. However, until the moment Jesus bore the cross, he did not have even one friend or companion. 

Then what was the heart of Jesus immediately after the resurrection? His heart, which rose after three days, was filled with a sorrowful feeling that could not help but offer a prayer of shame before heaven. When he faced the Father, who had worked for four thousand years, and the many prophets and saints who had labored, he felt both joy and infinite sorrow, and he had to shed endless tears. You must understand the heart of Jesus. 

While the saints in heaven rejoiced, Jesus was sad, and God also had a heart that was both joyful and sorrowful. Today, among the people living on earth, there is not a single person who knows the heart of Jesus. However, you must know this and make a new resolution in your heart. 

What should you resolve? The cause and motivation for what happened to Jesus were not because of the nation or heaven. It was solely because of Satan. Jesus set out to trample on this Satan and to find the lost apostles. When thinking about the fact that the apostles, who once swore to risk their lives, allowed the wicked to guard even the body and tomb of Jesus, if Jesus were an ordinary person, he would not have gone out to find them again. 

However, because Jesus had a deep-seated determination to find the disciples, the nation, and humanity that were in the embrace of the enemy Satan, he set out to find them. Moreover, when he looked at the Father, who had endured and managed the betrayal of humans for four thousand years, he bore a solemn resolution to find the pitiful humans, and thus Jesus set out to find them. You must also hold onto this solemn resolution of Jesus today. 

Furthermore, Jesus, who inspired the remaining apostles with the determination to fight against Satan once again, could not stay with them forever. Looking at the disciples who had to inherit the will and walk the long historical path, who had to overcome the unspeakable path of blood and the critical moment of the cross at Golgotha, the sorrow and hardship in Jesus' heart were like those at the moment of the cross. Additionally, after forty days, Jesus had to bear the sorrow of leaving his beloved disciples in the land of enemies. 

Then what kind of heart did the saints on earth have? They should have understood the sorrow of Jesus who had come and the sorrow of Jesus who had to leave, but they only mourned the separation from their beloved teacher, and the heart of Jesus looking at this was so sorrowful that it could not be expressed in words. 

So what kind of heart should you have? Even if you have to take on the tasks that follow after Jesus has gone, fighting a life-and-death battle against Satan, you must become someone with an unwavering heart that will not yield even an inch. Thus, you must directly experience and resolve the heart that Jesus had, which he could not let go of until he passed away. 

If the apostles at that time had all shared the same heart and had reached the cross together with Jesus, God would not have been able to resurrect only Jesus. If that had happened, all the apostles would have been resurrected, and Christianity as we know it today would not exist. 

Now, you must inherit the mission left by these apostles, taking the heart of Jesus, who was indignant against Satan, as your own heart, and the determination of Jesus, who overcame the cross, as your own determination. Thus, you must become the second apostles who appear in the form of resurrection by overcoming the cross without dying. You must become apostles who can defeat the Satan that has tormented God for six thousand years in a single day. And even if you walk the path of death with a solemn resolution, you must be able to fight against Satan and leave a mark. 

The great mission of the saints of the last days

You who are gathered here! Does each of your hearts and each of your cells become beings that can harmonize with God? Only when your hearts and cells can harmonize with God will God come to you just as Jesus visited the apostles after his resurrection. These apostles must gather and go out to find all of humanity on behalf of Jesus. Until now, the apostles came out believing that they had come to kill Jesus, but you who know that Jesus did not come to die must make an even more solemn resolution. 

Peter, who could not keep his vow to follow Jesus to death, made a second vow after the resurrection of Jesus, and it can be said that heaven has been working until today based on that condition. Therefore, now you must vow only before Jesus, and not only vow before the resurrected Jesus like Peter, but take a step further and vow before heaven, earth, and the Lord. Thus, you must fulfill the vow that Peter could not keep before he died. Only then can the grievances of heaven be resolved based on that condition. 

You must fulfill your wishes before God as children and before Jesus as siblings. The apostles of the past were in a priestly relationship with Jesus, but you today are in a brotherly relationship with Jesus. Therefore, you must feel the responsibility to look clearly at God and Jesus from the perspective of a brother and to resolve their grievances. 

Just as Jesus endured suffering, you must also understand that you have a great mission to endure such suffering and fight against adversity. That is why you must always listen carefully to what voice is heard in the last days, and you must understand the wishes of heaven and earth and fulfill them. Only then can you stand as the sons and daughters of God. 

Let us become the true sons that God desires

Romans 5:12-21

Today, I would like to speak to you for a moment under the title "Let us become the true sons that God desires."

When we think about this, we see that the true God, the true truth, and the true human each have different ways of existing, but in terms of internal standards, they are all moving in the same direction. In other words, God and truth exist eternally in the same direction. 

The suffering of believers

Today, anyone looking at this earth laments that this world cannot become a true world. On April 20, 1958, at the former headquarters church.

The land and history stained with the blood of goodness

You know this well through principles. The one whom God has sought

This is not a public opinion nor a delusion. 
Jesus could have harbored resentment against Satan and disbelief, but He did not harbor resentment because He knew that it was a nation loved by God. When you find yourselves in such circumstances, that is, when you feel resentment, you must become those who pray instead. Thus, we must become members who revive the denomination that our fallen ancestors sought to restore, moving this nation and further innovating global Christianity. This is the mission that we have. 
Then today, especially young men and women, where will you die, and in what field will you set conditions before heaven? Also, for whom have you lived until now? In terms of that ideology, in terms of that conscience, in terms of that life, whom have you relied on? If you have lived only for yourselves until now, you must reflect and chastise yourselves. 
A group that can move based on eternal ideology will not perish as long as the ideological subject does not vanish. Jacob held onto the will of God and endured the contempt and disdain of Laban for 21 years. He lived each day for 21 years without forgetting the will of his father and the blessing of his father. Abraham did the same. Moses also endured for 40 years in Pharaoh’s palace and 40 years in the wilderness of Midian, worrying about the chosen people, and you must know that Jesus did the same. 
So what will happen if we, who are in the end times, engage in a struggle to save humanity, which is engulfed in the world of Satan and bears the conditions of God’s sorrow? If there is someone who is sacrificed to save humanity in this struggle, God will establish his grave, and His footprints after death will be revealed by God. You must remember the biblical words, “Whoever seeks to preserve his life will lose it, but whoever loses his life will preserve it.” (Luke 17:33) Those who betrayed Jesus while laying conditions for Satan all perished. When our nation was under Japanese rule, those who worshiped at Shinto shrines to avoid their unfavorable positions and sold out their denominations all perished. A church, nation, and world without tears will all perish. Therefore, you must understand that there is a hidden providential purpose for this nation to be moved more quickly than any other nation before God’s providence. 
Thus, now that you know the circumstances of Jesus, you must be able to represent God’s position so that when the age of God’s ideology comes, you can become the sons and daughters of life permitted by heaven who inherit the second gospel of Christ on this earth. You must keep this in mind. 
And you have a responsibility toward your nation and a responsibility toward numerous denominations. But have you ever worried infinitely for this nation while eating, dressing, or sleeping? If there are sons and daughters who worry about this world and heaven and earth, you must surely know that such people will become the protagonists of the new era. 
When we consider the providential historical process, we cannot help but hold back our tears. However, you must not remain there; rather, using it as a mirror, you must not become a loser in the environment you must endure today, but rather become someone who can be raised as a heavenly son or daughter who can make heaven rejoice.
