The forsaken Jesus
1 Peter 2:1-10
This scripture likens Jesus to a stone. It also states that the forsaken stone became the cornerstone of the house. 
We can see that even His family, denomination, the nation of Israel, and even His beloved three disciples did not recognize this situation of Jesus. 
God sought to save the chosen nation of Israel by bringing them out from their enemies and sought to fulfill His great purpose through this nation. However, the nation of Israel looked at God’s will from both an ideological and historical standpoint, but they could not fulfill that will in their lives. 
And God has gone through the labor of revealing His will to each individual to find a being of hope. That is, through 4,000 years of effort, He sought to reach the living realm, but no one recognized it, and while they awaited the Messiah in their hearts, there was not a single person who welcomed the Messiah when He actually appeared. 
Anna devoted her life to fasting and did not leave the temple, awaiting the Messiah, but because she could not testify to or receive the Messiah when He appeared, she too became distant from the will of heaven. This was the sorrow of heaven. 
On June 22, 1958, at the former headquarters church.
* This message has been summarized from the ‘Summary of Sermon Content No. 49’ published by the Seonghwa Youth Association’s Preaching Department.
Jesus came as the culmination of 4,000 years of God’s providence. If Jesus’ parents and relatives had known that He was the Messiah who would save their nation, they would not have allowed Him to be born in a stable, and if the Jewish people had recognized Him as the Messiah, they would not have chased Him from town to town during His 30 years of private life and 3 years of public ministry. 
God, who saw this, was saddened, and Jesus Himself was saddened as well. 
Moreover, because He was labeled a rebel, there could be no connection between God’s will and the hope that the Jewish people had awaited. God could not establish a connection either. Thus, unable to bridge the gap between heaven and Jesus, He could not help but worry about the past history of this nation, the reality of that time, and the eternal future. 
Because they did not know Jesus, that is, because they could not recognize Him as the Savior and Messiah of this nation, no creature in the created world or human beings on this earth could establish any direct relationship with God. 
When Jesus was a carpenter’s son, He thought of carving away the sins and faults of the nation while working with wood, and in His words, actions, and thoughts, He lived a life in preparation to establish a heavenly ideology centered on goodness. However, there was not a single person at that time who understood Jesus’ situation and heart. Therefore, even though Jesus wanted to speak, He found Himself in a situation where He could not openly share His thoughts with anyone. Unable to be understood or supported by His family, Jesus eventually left home and sought refuge in the church, but He was also forsaken by the church that did not understand God’s heart and will, and later was labeled a rebel of the nation. Yet, knowing that a greater path of Golgotha lay ahead, Jesus resolved to become one who could not fall away from heaven. 
Thus, only those who establish a connection with God and the universe can be granted universal and global value. Jesus felt that He was connected with the spirits of the family, church, nation, the spirits of the earthly world, and the spirits in hell, and although He was forsaken by His family and church, He did not become discouraged by it. The Jewish people thought that everything would end when Jesus was crucified as a rebel of the nation, but because there was a spark in the remaining group, including the twelve disciples, Jesus was able to work through them. This is how Christianity has been able to expand globally as it is today. 
In the end times, we must become those who understand God’s heart above all else. Humans have three elements: knowledge (智), emotion (情), and will (意), and we must achieve a heavenly emotional connection (天情) based on knowledge and will. Because there is a divine providence concerning our Korean people, we, more than anyone else, have a strong heart of earnestness and loyalty toward heaven. 
We do not need a leader to understand God’s heart and truth. We must recognize that the fact that Jesus said, “My God, My God, why have You forsaken Me?” when He was crucified became a new turning point in history. 
We must understand that after Jesus died, the gathering of women who could connect with His blood and flesh moved the entire universe. Therefore, even if this nation has nothing, we must possess the deep core of God’s heart. This nation must become one that, even if it loses everything, does not lose the heart of God. Thus, if this nation can become an altar of bloodshed for heaven and earth and can weep for all people and all things, there will be a way to live. 
God is the one who wields the whip of wrath while also shedding tears. However, those who rejoice in seeing this will fall under the conditions of judgment. Therefore, you must now seek the Jesus you once forsook and become a friend before Him so that you can stand as a bride before the returning Jesus. * 
Let us participate in the remaining group.
Romans 9:25-29
Just as God is eternal, He created creatures with an eternal ideology. However, because individuals, nations, humanity, and all things have not remained as eternal creations, God has been grieving and seeking them until today. In other words, due to human fall, God lost the garden of creation and has not given up on His hope for the created world, striving to fulfill the grand ideology of creation through a long historical process while engaging in fierce battles against Satan, enduring until today. 
The remaining heirs of hope and ideology
God has such a great hope, but on the other hand, there is the sorrow of having to seek even the smallest things. 
This great hope was to be realized starting from individuals, but since individuals fell and the hope of the whole was not realized, before the hope of all humanity and all things can be realized, God’s hope must first be realized in individuals. This is God’s hidden circumstance. 
God sought to establish hope centered on individuals by raising Cain and Abel, but when this collapsed, it took 1,600 years to finally find and establish Noah’s family. However, even the family of Noah, which was to remain at that time, was broken due to Ham’s mistake, and the hope was extended through Abraham and Moses to Jesus. 
Before Jesus came, many prophets were to realize God’s ideology starting from individuals, but they could not, so this hope remained until the only begotten Son, Jesus. 
Jesus came as an individual, but He was not an ordinary individual. Jesus embodied the patience and ideology that God had endured for 4,000 years, and He was the one who shared God’s heart. He also bore all the hopes that the prophets who came and went over 4,000 years tried to realize but could not, coming as the culmination of 4,000 years of goodness, with the ideology to resolve the grievances of heaven and earth on the levels of individual, nation, state, world, and cosmic dimensions. 
Thus, the humans of that time should not have limited Jesus, who brought God’s great ideology, to just the ideology of one person, but should have allowed it to dwell in the hearts of the Israelite people and every individual of humanity. However, because people did not know or accept it, God’s great ideology ended up being limited to the ideology of just one person, Jesus, and when Jesus passed away, that great ideology could not remain as an earthly ideology but only remained as a spiritual ideology. 
As a result, humans living on earth became those who had to wait for the ideology that should remain on earth forever, and Jesus found Himself in a position where He had to return to leave that ideology on earth. 
Then when will individuals, families, nations, and humanity possessing the ideology that remains on earth appear, and where will they appear? We must understand this. 
When Jesus left, He left behind His words and hopes, but His ideology...
could not leave behind, so that ideology must manifest. 
Then, who will be the person who can possess his ideology at the end? 
That person must first have the hope and will of Jesus, and above that hope and will, 
must have the heart and the historical sorrow that can hold the ideology. Therefore, 
that person must be one who can connect with God's creation ideology.

Let us participate in the remnant. 
Jesus, when he came to this earth to proclaim the words of the gospel, earnestly hoped 
for, "Love me more than anyone else." (Matthew 10:37) 
So, has there been anyone who deeply understood the true meaning of Jesus' words, 
"Love me more than anyone else," and practiced it? There has not. Among the 
disciples who followed him for three years and lived together, there was no one who 
practiced his words as they were. 
Moreover, Jesus said to love one's brother. After the resurrection, he appeared to 
his disciple Peter and asked three times, "Do you love me more than these?" (John 
21:15), and when Peter answered, he said, "Feed my lambs." (John 21:15). Furthermore, 
Jesus told his disciples that he would come again, so they should prepare and wait. 
If we summarize the important words Jesus spoke while he was on earth, it can be 
condensed into these two points.

Jesus' earnest request left behind 
So, who will fulfill the earnest words left by Jesus? The one who fulfills these words 
will escape the judgment at the end and will be able to meet Jesus. 
Have you ever loved Jesus in your lifetime? And can you confidently say that your 
degree of love for him was greater than for your parents, spouse, or anyone in the 
world? You all should think about this again. What Jesus in heaven earnestly desires 
for this earth is for someone to appear who can love him more than anyone else. If 
such a person exists on this earth, he would be one who knows God's creation ideology 
and sympathizes with God's 6,000 years of toil and Jesus' bitter heart. 
Jesus represented the value of God's creation principles and is within the law of 
heaven's creation, where there is no contradiction or conflict. Because Jesus was in 
such a position, his body and heart became one, and although he was 4,000 years 
removed from Adam, he transcended time and space. 
For this reason, Jesus could intuit that God's creation ideology was present in Adam 
4,000 years ago. 
What mission did Jesus have? It was a mission to connect humans, who should be 
linked to the eternal love of God, with that love, as they had failed to connect with 
God's love. He also had the mission to establish love between humans and all things. 
He came to fulfill this mission, which is why he told the world to love him more than 
anyone else. However, at that time, there was not a single person who loved Jesus 
more than anyone else. 
From this perspective, when we gather our hearts and examine the historical path, 
we can recognize that we are individuals who have inherited the bloodline of sin, 
who do not possess the ideology of creation, and who have not been able to serve 
Jesus, who came as the bridegroom, from the position of the bride. Although we 
encountered the environment to love Jesus, we failed to love him, and thus, for the 
humans on this earth, there remains a condition to love Jesus more than anyone else 
at the end. 
Is there anyone among you who has experienced a love that has never existed in 
history, standing as a faithful servant before Jesus, who is the King of Kings, and 
the bridegroom? If not, you cannot claim to love heaven more than anyone else. 
God has come seeking foolish sinners for 6,000 years, and if I cannot welcome such 
a God with love, I must understand that the ideology of God, who comes seeking me, 
is halted because of me. 
Therefore, at this time, when you pray for your families, you should pray for 
sons and daughters who can love God and Jesus more than anyone else. When you pray 
for your nation, you should pray for many people who can love God and Jesus more 
than any other people. When you pray for humanity, you should pray that the 
Christians of the world can love God and Jesus more than any other religious 
people. If you cannot love God and Jesus more than anyone else, then you should at 
least pray for this. 

Let us participate in the remnant. 
What does all of creation, which has been created today, desire from humans? It is 
to bring forth beings who can fulfill Jesus' earnest request, that is, to love him 
more than anyone else. All of creation longs for such beings to appear, and because 
they have not appeared, all of creation is groaning, and heaven is groaning. You 
must understand this. 

We must love God and Jesus more than anyone else. 
Then what is this groaning? It is the groaning that arises because Adam and Eve, 
who were to establish a relationship with God's love and ideology in the Garden of 
Eden, could not establish a proper relationship due to their fall, and it is the 
groaning that longs to restore and establish a relationship with God's ideology, 
love, and connection. Therefore, those who cannot resolve this groaning will be 
subject to judgment at the end. 
So, who will remain in this judgment? It will be those who know the heart of God 
and Jesus better than anyone else and can love them more than anyone else. 
Only by knowing God's heart can one connect with God's ideology through that heart, 
and thus gain the strength to drive out enemies from this universe. The reason Jesus 
could pray for blessings for his enemies even on the cross was that God's heart was 
always surging strongly within him. Therefore, Jesus was able to show a courageous 
attitude even in the face of death. 
Jesus left behind the words of the bridegroom and the bride. So what are the 
bridegroom and the bride? Has there been a bride who loved God and Jesus more than 
anyone else up to today, 2,000 years after Jesus left? There has not. Many people 
have spoken about Jesus and the history that came through him, but no one has known 
the heart of Jesus that could not manifest God's creation ideology before humanity. 
While it is important to talk about Jesus and his history, it is more important to 
experience his heart. Therefore, only when the heart of Jesus and my heart become 
one can I become a person who can represent God's ideology and remain at the end. 
Jesus loved his disciples more than himself. If there is sorrow in heaven, what is 
that sorrow? Jesus loved his disciples more than his own body to leave God's 
creation ideology on this earth, but the disciples followed him with other thoughts, 
not caring about Jesus' circumstances and heart. The sorrow of heaven is that this 
love could not bear fruit on earth while Jesus was alive. The disciples only felt 
this love after Jesus had passed away, and from then on, they began to understand 
the intention of the words Jesus had spoken. 
Who was the person Jesus longed for and sought? It was those who hated and 
abandoned themselves more than anyone else. Jesus sought out such people with a 
heart to love them more than anyone else. Therefore, the person who can meet Jesus 
at the end will be one who, even while hating and abandoning themselves, seeks 
heaven with a heart of love. 
The people of the world are hoping for Jesus to come. However, we should not just 
hope for Jesus to come; we must become people who seek the Lord. To do this, we 
must overcome the peaks of sorrow that heaven has experienced in the historical 
course and the difficulties of the cross that Jesus bore. By doing so, we can shorten 
the period of providential history and transcend time and space to experience the 
bitter heart that Jesus held 2,000 years ago. 
Then, who was the person who went to find the tomb of the deceased Jesus? It was 
Mary Magdalene, who, though seen as a weak being by humans, followed Jesus with a 
heart that loved him more than anyone else, despite being chased from town to town, 
ridiculed everywhere she went. Before this earnest Mary, Jesus appeared in his 
resurrected body, which serves as a symbol showing the way for Christians around 
the world at the end. 
What kind of life did Mary Magdalene lead? She loved Jesus so much that she forgot 
about everything, including food and clothing, and lived solely for him. Her path, 
which transcended life and death and disregarded her own dignity, was the path that 
the saints at the end must walk. If there is still someone on this earth who has 
the heart of Mary Magdalene, that person will have tears of God's 6,000 years of 
providence in their eyes and will recognize that they are infinitely indebted to 
heaven. 
Moreover, they will know that even if they burn their own body, there is no way to 
repay the love they have received, and they will know that they are on the path of 
death. Have you ever had such a heart at any time? If such a person exists, they 
will know the heart of heaven that has come seeking them, having abandoned everything 
throughout the past, present, and future from the time of creation. And that person 
will not be able to lift their face before heaven because they will know that they 
are infinitely indebted to heaven. Only those who feel this heart and abandon 
everything to follow heaven will remain at the end. 
Therefore, those who believe in Jesus and wish for comfort will be servants of 
Jesus but will not be his friends. Also, those who believe in Jesus but do not know 
his heart will be friends but will not be his bride. Therefore, what heaven desires 
and what Jesus desires is not servants, nor friends, but brides. 

Those who can remain at the end 
When Jesus, who loved God and humanity more than anyone else in history and was 
qualified as the embodiment of the creation ideology, calls upon God, there was a 
moment when God forgot all dignity and face as the Creator and held onto Jesus. 
No one knows this. Furthermore, no one knows that God treated Jesus with a heart 
that could elevate him to a position even higher than himself, the Creator. 
Jesus was in an environment where he was rejected by the chosen people, but because 
he knew God's heart of patience over 4,000 years, he could not help but endure. 
Moreover, knowing that God had sacrificed everything over 4,000 years to find one 
son, Jesus thought that he must endure any sacrifice and rejection to find a bride 
on earth. Thus, he did not curse the nation that treated him as an enemy. 
However, even Mary Magdalene, who knew a little of Jesus' heart, was told not to 
touch him when she tried to reach out to the resurrected Jesus. This showed that 
unless a person qualified to serve Jesus completely as a bride appears, the hearts of 
the Holy Spirit, Jesus, and God's heart of resentment cannot be resolved. 
Therefore, at the end, we must find a being who has appeared as the embodiment of 
God and love him more than anyone else, and we must be able to represent him, and 
furthermore, there must be a church and a nation composed of such people. Such a 
church, such a nation, and such humanity must be centered around the heavenly 
principle. However, as long as humans today cannot feel this heavenly principle, 
they will not be able to remain at the end. 
Now, you must recognize that you are historical sinners, and before criticizing 
others, you must first know yourself and learn to pray, and you must become people 
who think of and pray for the nation and humanity. Thus, when you face humanity, 
which must realize the world of God's creation ideology, humanity will infinitely 
welcome you, and when you face all creation, they will comfort and welcome you, 
knowing that they were sacrificed and abandoned for you. Furthermore, when such 
people appear before heaven, heaven will wipe away their tears and comfort their 
labors, and only such people will remain at the end. Also, you must understand that 
heaven, Jesus, and all creation long for such people. 

The relationship of restoration brought by Jesus 
Acts 3:13-24 
Many people may habitually or customarily think that today is Sunday, so they come 
to worship before the Father. 
You must understand that this place where you are sitting is not a place that can 
be thought of or realized at such a level. In other words, the reason you have 
gathered here is due to some unknown background connection. 
That connection is a relationship that is related to my individual self in front, 
behind, left, and right, and also a relationship that is related above and below, 
which you must deeply keep in mind. 
The background of Jesus' coming and the result of the Jewish people's disbelief 
The fact that Jesus appeared in the historical course was not a coincidence but 
was due to the predetermined will of heaven. In other words, Jesus appeared to 
establish historical, temporal, and future connections. If someone had known this 
fact at that time, Jesus would not have had to die on the cross. 
Although Jesus was just an individual, when he connected the relationships he 
was forming to the whole, the historical relationships of humanity would come along, 
and the contemporary and future relationships of that time would also come along. 
No one at that time knew this. Furthermore, no one knew that Jesus came with a 
central mission that required the heavenly hosts and God the Father in heaven to 
move based on their relationship with him. 
Moreover, the ignorant Jewish people, who did not know this fact, were proud of 
being the chosen people and thought they were standing in the will promised by 
heaven, but by opposing Jesus, they fell away from that will and established a 
historical denomination that could not be on heaven's side. Although they had 
hopes of achieving the blessings of the end times for the Israelite nation, which 
boasted of its chosen status, they fell into a position of ruin because they did not 
recognize Jesus, who is the subject of the universal ideology. In this way, while a 
great tragedy unfolded on the historical course of humanity, people at that time 
were unaware that Jesus responded with tears of sorrow and blood of sacrifice. 
However, the words Jesus cried out were truths that arose from his earnest heart. 
Moreover, the thirty years of life he lived were not for the fulfillment of his 
own desires. Furthermore, his hope was not for himself alone. 
Yet the Jewish people, who should have known this fact, did not realize it and 

Only Jesus, who tried to fulfill the will of heaven while forgetting his own sorrow, knew this, and this sorrow has become the root of our sorrow today. We must understand this. Furthermore, from the perspective of a believer, you must take a step further to realize that the path Jesus walked is the path I must walk, and the ideal garden that Jesus desires is the ideal garden I must realize.

Jesus longed for and hoped for the ideal of a bride and groom who could dwell within God's realm of blessing. He wished to hold the 144,000 gathered around the Lamb's Feast, singing songs of joy and glory before the Father. This was Jesus's earnest desire. However, due to the disbelief of the Jewish people, Jesus was ultimately unable to fulfill that original hope and was instead crucified on Golgotha. The prayer that Jesus prayed in Gethsemane, sweating blood, was a heartfelt prayer that represented God's earnest and sorrowful heart. That earnest prayer was not for his own solution but for the ignorant and sleeping people (the nation), Satan, and his three beloved disciples.

Then, what must have been the heart of Jesus, who bore the responsibility of leading the ignorant people while holding onto God's hope, when the Jewish people, a race deserving of judgment for obstructing the heavenly principles, had to pray again for the hand of forgiveness towards heaven? Furthermore, as he endured the suffering of the cross, what kind of connection was the prayer of Christ, pleading, "Do not hold their sins against them," meant to establish before humanity, before the providential path, or before the heart of heaven?

Today, we must go back and reflect on the heart of Jesus and bow our heads to that heart. I must walk the path that the Lord walked, follow the footsteps the Lord took, and become a figure who can faithfully bear the resentment of the Father at the altar where the Lord returned. Moreover, we must reflect on whether we can hold onto the heart of Jesus, who represents the connection of heaven, and whether we can grasp the heart of Jesus that represents the historical connection with all humanity. In other words, we must ask ourselves if we can become friends of Jesus who can represent his historical, temporal, and future connections.

Self-awareness
There is nothing in this world that one can do alone. Just as one cannot clarify what kind of being one is without defining the relative relationships one has, the same applies to God's providence of restoration. Where there is one, there is two, and where there is a gathering of one, there are connections in front, back, left, right, above, and below. Thus, when that one existence is equipped with a subjectivity that can pass through history, time, and future, a new history can begin from there. You must understand that God is pulling up and raising fallen humanity every time they fall further, unfolding providence beyond time and place.

Today, when you are asked by others how long you have believed in Jesus, it is easy to respond immediately with "I've believed for 10 years," "20 years," or "a few years." However, when examining the history of connections, you must recognize that you stand in a position where 6,000 years of history is accumulated. In other words, you must learn to find your position of faith.

Moreover, because humans cannot escape the history of connections, you must become someone who can confidently claim to have a central faith that is indispensable within the realm of temporal connections today. Furthermore, from now on, the foundation of faith you establish must be something that future generations can emulate for thousands of years. The question is how you will build that foundation of future connections within your current realm of faith.

Therefore, you, standing in this position today, must confidently present yourself before God in place of 6,000 years of history and call out, "O my Father, who has labored for 6,000 years!" You must also become someone who can call the Father, who has endured the path of labor to embrace 2.7 billion people, as your Father. Furthermore, you must stand before heaven with the conviction and determination that the faith cries you raise today will resonate with countless future generations. Only then can you call God, who moves according to the eternal principles of providence, your Father.

Thus, the question is whether you have become someone who can draw the future into the present and the past to testify before God, or whether there is another person who can testify to such a being.

It was only after 4,000 years of history that Jesus came to this earth to bear such a mission and pioneer a realistic path. Therefore, you must not engage in conceptual faith today. You must not remain trapped in the knowledge-based concepts known through historical understanding. However, if you find yourself blocked in that path, you must recognize that it is time to look back on the historical path and reanalyze it. The fact that numerous churches that have walked the path of faith until today, or many religions that boasted of their ideals, have reached a dead end proves that they have become unable to establish connections with historical, temporal, or future hopes.

The mission regarding truth and its protagonist
So, what kind of believer are we looking for today? We are looking for a believer who can establish a relationship with us in place of historical, temporal, and future connections. However, today you may feel something seeping from your heart, body, or life. In other words, we are sensing something through our five senses. The question is whether there is any truth that can encourage the world of the heart through the sensations of those five senses.

Such truth may seem to have no relation to our living environment today and may appear to have started in a new field, but that is not the case. It is a truth that can be fully aligned with our current lives. When we forget the ideals we hoped for and find ourselves in a daze, when the barriers of darkness block us and we are unable to establish the center of our hearts, that is when we need this truth.

Therefore, you must earnestly seek the truth that has not yet appeared in the historical path and can penetrate the future while connecting it to the past. Thus, you must keep in mind that you bear a global mission to plant such truth on this earth, regardless of your own efforts, sacrifices, and sufferings.

Therefore, the statement that there is one person who has established such connections is truly the gospel among gospels in the history of humanity. When you think of this, you must pursue the truth that Jesus advocated. You must equip yourself with historical connections or blessed connections of faith from the present time.

Have you become one with the historical connections flowing from the heart of Jesus? If not, you must recognize that you are a sinner who has violated the connections that Jesus has established throughout history and must humbly bow your head. You must also realize that you are the one who has trampled on the life journey of Jesus, who preached the gospel in place of temporal connections and walked the practical path to fulfill his responsibilities.

Those who do not understand the words of the gospel introduced through these connections and do not know such connections are burdened with a great debt. It is the truth of Jesus Christ through the connection of God's providence, and we must recognize that we are indebted to that truth today. Until Jesus stands before heaven, there has been 4,000 years of God's labor, and the blood of many ancestors who have gone through God's heart and historical process is stained here. You must feel this once more.

Now, if you have a heart that longs to find the connection of ideals and wishes to find your position based on that connection, have you ever felt the weight of the great debt you carry on your shoulders? The connections and laws that move the heavenly principles are urging us in these fields today, but we remain trapped in personal connections centered on ourselves. If you live only in such connections and cannot break free from them, judgment through heaven awaits you. Perhaps the blood of countless martyrs from the historical path will cry out.

You must understand the heart of Jesus, who could call upon heaven as Father even in such a realm. Thus, the heart of Jesus and the heart of God could resonate, and the heart of the Father, who has labored throughout the historical process, could find comfort through Jesus. Moreover, as one individual, Jesus could represent God's entire hope for the future. At that time, no one realized that Jesus was an extraordinary being, incomparable to anyone else in the historical process.

Thus, the will of God was for the historical sorrows that were unknown to be resolved and to move forward in glory and joy, but that will appeared instead as sorrow, manifested at the altar of the cross. So, what will you offer today to resolve the heart of the Father who looked upon that? This is the greatest question of all. Therefore, you must understand that the spiritual restoration history has been turned upside down in our journey of spiritual restoration since Jesus came and went.

Our responsibility to bear the sorrow and wishes of Jesus
Today, in the mission field that must fulfill the universal connections, both the upper and lower relationships must be unified, as well as the hearts. Just as a single cell of my life moves by a unified heart, that fact must also be able to resonate in my heart through the historical process.

Thus, it is important to consider what kind of connection you have with Jesus, who bore the historical responsibility, who thought of God's will, who prayed all night, and who was crucified. Therefore, you must be able to say, "Father! I am weak, but I will take on even a part of Jesus's burden." You must have a solemn heart that can feel the sorrowful heart that could not discuss its pain with anyone and weep together, and with that heart, you should take on at least a part of Jesus's difficult circumstances.

You must surely understand this.

However, when heaven tries to create this for fallen humanity, each situation is different. Moreover, those circumstances are not simple; they are historical circumstances. Because these circumstances have appeared to humanity in the historical process, you must understand that until now, human history has been a tragic history that has given rise to immense struggles and bloodshed.

So what are those circumstances? In order for God to find just one of you, He must first face the value of you against Satan. God must first face the value of the world before reclaiming the world. The price must be paid according to how much is sought. This was God's strategy and God's circumstances.

God has allowed humanity to go through the place of death in order to place them in the position of life. Furthermore, if there is someone in a position to die, God has crossed over to find the opportunity to save them. You must understand that even amidst infinite despair, He has crossed over the peaks of infinite sorrow and pain.

God has gone through 6,000 years of sorrowful historical paths to introduce the ideals of love that I have hoped for, and today He is pouring His heart, will, and character into connecting with just one individual. When you feel such a heart, you will finally be able to feel the common heart of all the historical prophets and sages, or the heart of someone like Noah from ancient times.

While there is distance from the life history centered on Abraham, in the world of heart, that distance is transcended. Today, I can connect through my heart. The same goes for the times of Moses and the times of Jesus. Therefore, now you must connect with the heart of God who has been providentially working for 2,000 years through Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Only when you stand as a person who has established a focal point of one heart can Jesus finally call you a bride.

You must remember that Jesus referred to such people as "You are not servants, but my brothers." Furthermore, when you come to know this, you will feel that when I have sorrow, my Father has already sorrowed before me. When I feel indignant and wronged, my Father's indignation and wronged feelings were there first, and when I am despondent, my Father was already in a place of despondency.

In order to stand as God's direct children
From this perspective, I must become a true son or daughter who can comfort my Father, who is sorrowful, saying, "Father! Do not sorrow for me; rejoice instead." 

Even when I am wronged, I must do it for the sake of my Father, and I must have the heart of a true son or daughter who can comfort my Father, who is sorrowful for our body and heart. If you have such a heart, even if you go down the path of the cross, you cannot say, "Father! The pain of my death today is heavy; please let me avoid this sorrowful path!"

Thus, while it may seem that Jesus prayed in fear and anxiety to avoid the pain of his own death, it was not so. When he felt the heart of God, who had crossed over the peaks of the cross for 4,000 years to find just one Jesus, his own individual death was not a problem. That is why Jesus prayed, "My Father! If it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will." (Matthew 26:39) You must understand that only from such a heart can God's will be fulfilled.

Today, dear members of our Unification Church! Do not hold onto your own circumstances and weep! Each person's circumstances are diverse, but you must become sons and daughters who can weep while holding onto the heart of the Father. You must become devoted sons and daughters who can comfort the Father, who has wept for you first with tears.

Thus, when Jesus prayed, "Not as I will, but as you will," (Matthew 26:39) he received the grace of resurrection, and just as he was embraced within God's realm, we too must overcome this peak. In other words, we must wear the reality that has not died and transcend the realm of resurrection. 

Only then, in the substantial world, can we love all people on behalf of the True Father, and at that time, all people can live with you, who have become such. Only then can we see the conclusion of the ideal for which God created the earth and the conclusion of God's providence for humanity today. Furthermore, we can also see the conclusion of the hope we have longed for until now and the conclusion of the providence regarding my love and life.

Only when such a world is realized can we understand God's heart, which has labored to find me, God's heart that has suffered, and God's heart that has been wronged and sorrowful. We will also come to know the love of the Father, who has wept while holding onto the hands of sorrowful circumstances today, and even the heart of the Father who rejoices.

However, the love of God, who sought to hold onto Jesus and complete the ideals of heaven on this earth, has not yet been revealed. Until now, countless humans in history have come forth to comfort God's hidden sorrow, but the scene where the child who is held and the Father who holds can rejoice and create the original garden of flowers, singing and dancing in love, has not yet appeared in the human world.

So how can we today know the sorrowful heart of the Father? We can only feel it when we are in such a position. Only those who can feel the sorrowful and joyful heart of the Father can possess the remaining love of God and stand as direct children of God, not as adopted children. 

God's freedom, liberation, and unity that He seeks
John 8:31-47
<Prayer> Father! Please do not forsake your sons and daughters who are prostrated here, and allow us to be sons and daughters who do not hesitate to give our whole body and heart to You. Although there are many shortcomings and inadequacies in our sight, we offer our whole body and heart to You, relying on the historical heart that has labored to find us. 

Please burn away our shortcomings with the fire of the Holy Spirit and sanctify us so that we may become worthy of being taken by You, and allow us to be able to bind our whole body and heart into one and offer it to You at this time. 

Father! The steps that your sons and daughters have taken to follow You to this point have been steps that substitute for Your tears, and they have been steps that substitute for Your sorrowful path, which is like tearing away flesh and blood. Therefore, Father, knowing what we have resolved in our hearts and what we are moving our bodies to do, please embrace us with Your deep love, and allow not a single life to fall under the conditions of Satan's accusations. 

We know that You are trying to proclaim a new word before this nation through us, Father, but we have a restless heart that we cannot fulfill the mission and responsibility You desire due to our unfaithfulness and inadequacies, and we ask that You look upon the inadequate facts up to now and grant us the power of Your life and love to supplement them. We earnestly wish that You would bestow upon us direct gifts that can fulfill any mission and responsibility. 

As we go forth, countless satans will try to block our path, so may our determination of body and heart be complete, and may we become living sacrifices before You, enduring to the end so that we do not fail in the battle against Satan. 

Please allow us to advance with the initial resolve and determination we had, striving and fighting to manifest only Your glory, loving Father, we earnestly wish and ask for this. 

Now, please look upon the children gathered here with compassion and allow them to be embraced in Your love. 

Remove all elements and conditions of darkness, and as a bundle with the authority of life, may we serve You, and may this time be one where we can give glory and thanks before the gifts of glory. 

From the beginning to the end, please do not allow Satan to appear in this gathering, and may only Your glory be manifested through our hearts and bodies, we earnestly wish for this and appeal in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

<Word> The title of the message I wish to share with you is "The Freedom, Liberation, and Unity that God Seeks." I will speak for a moment with this title.

God's position and His hope
I wish to speak about "The Freedom, Liberation, and Unity that God Seeks" from a faith perspective. 

You all know that God is omnipotent and that there is nothing He cannot do. However, no matter how powerful God is, when we ask whether His heart is truly in a position of freedom, having intruded upon His heart, I cannot answer affirmatively. When we ask whether God's true heart is in a position of joy in liberation, placed before the hope-filled providence, I must also say that it is not so. Furthermore, if we ask whether the humans and all creation that God has created are moving motivated by God's heart, that is, whether God's heart moves and humans move and the entire creation can be united in that position, we cannot conclude that this is so either.

It is God's nature and original heart to desire to be free. And God is the Father who must govern the universe from a liberated position.
However, the fact that God cannot do so is the sorrow of God, the sorrow of all creation, and the cause of sorrow in history. Although God should govern the entire created world with a unified ideology, the fact that He is not in such a position is the sorrow of God, the pain of God, and the injustice of God, which we cannot deny. 

The original ideal when God created all these creatures was a garden of freedom, a garden of liberation, and a garden of unity. However, there were some twists and turns that prevented God's ideals from being realized, and this has become the source of sorrow from God to humanity and all creation. You cannot deny that. So, what is the source of that sorrow? We know well today that it is the fall of humanity. 

Then, God, who seeks to save fallen humanity, has an ideology that He desires for this society, and there is an ideology that we are searching for. What is the standard of that ideology? The freedom that represents God's heart, the liberation centered on God's circumstances, and the unity centered on God's ideals are God's wishes and, furthermore, our wishes, and you must understand that they are the standard of that ideology. 

"The Lord is the Spirit, and where the Spirit of the Lord is, there is freedom." (2 Corinthians 3:17) It is recorded in the Bible, and today, our Father, who is the God of freedom, the God of liberation, and the God of unity, how can the heart of freedom that can transcend any trial seep into your own heart while living with that Father? How can the point of liberation that can overcome all barriers of trials be found? When will the time of unified rest that the center of our ideology desires, that is, the whole being unified, be found? This is an important issue that you must think about. 

As God is still not in a position of freedom, not in a position of liberation, and not in a position of unity, the cries for freedom on this land today do not become the true freedom that we should enjoy. Although liberation is being spoken of, that liberation is not complete liberation. Although unity is being claimed, that unity is also not perfect unity. Human society has unified from clans to tribes, nations, but such partial unity is not true unity. 

The standard of true freedom, liberation, and unity
Because of God's will, even for us who were created by God, the perfect freedom we desire, the perfect liberation we desire, and the perfect unity we desire can only be achieved on the day when God can be free, and God becomes the protagonist of liberation and unity. Therefore, we cannot logically deny that God's freedom, liberation, and unity are the standards of the freedom, liberation, and unity that humanity desires. 

Looking back on our historical journey today, after the feudal society of the Middle Ages, humanism has been promoted, centered on the ideas of freedom, equality, and fraternity. So, whose attributes are the original freedom, the original equality, and the original fraternity? They are precisely God's attributes. 

If Christianity in the Middle Ages had been established in a position of freedom that could connect with God's heart, or in a liberated position, or in a united position, then there would have been no need for terms like revolution or reform on this earth. Because Christianity did not take the position of centering on God and proclaiming perfect freedom and perfect liberation, the movements for freedom, liberation, and unity shifted to the external world. This is what we call the Renaissance today. 

Afterward, the idea of freedom was raised, revolutions were made against monarchies, and again, freedom was promoted against imperialist nations, but it all fell apart. Revolutions were initiated to seek freedom, but they did not completely overcome the form of imperialist states and ultimately fell apart. And with ideologies and political thoughts established, we have come this far, but this too is gradually falling apart. 

Human beings, longing for freedom, have not been able to stand in a position to find and possess the ideal of complete freedom, and by merely claiming external freedom, they are losing true freedom more and more. That is, although they have claimed freedom nationally, socially, domestically, and even personally, they have repeatedly gone through a history of not finding and losing complete freedom. 

The freedom that people claim today is not the freedom that humanity can enjoy eternally by nature. Moreover, those who claim freedom are flowing into excessive individualism and becoming increasingly isolated. You cannot deny this. 

Therefore, as long as we cannot establish the ideal of perfect and unchanging freedom that can communicate with heaven and resonate with the ideals of heaven, and when that freedom does not align with the freedom that heaven and earth desire, we will find that the more we move to seek freedom, the more we will head toward the peak of unfreedom, as we can see from the movements of the present age. 

Thus, when we reflect on our hearts in our quest for freedom, the question is whether we have a heart of freedom that can harmonize with all creation. If we stand in the position of God's freedom, then our heart of freedom would have become a standard that can be enjoyed with all the people of the world. However, today, humanity cannot take such a position of freedom. They claim freedom but are establishing their perspectives on freedom only within the scope that affects them. 

If we discuss true freedom here, freedom that departs from principles is not true freedom, freedom that shirks responsibility is not true freedom, and freedom that does not leave any results is not true freedom. Therefore, any action of freedom must not deviate from principles, must bear responsibility, and must have results. However, if one tries to be free without meeting these conditions, then naturally, they will be placed far from the natural order, and you must recognize this. 

Thus, although imperialism emerged after the Middle Ages, it fell apart, and everything that has taken on a philosophical form up to today will also fall apart when true ideologies of freedom emerge in the future. This trend is gradually affecting individuals as well. When you focus on yourselves, you will feel that if you claim freedom, society must also innovate, and families must also innovate. Furthermore, history is now flowing in a direction that separates even my heart and body. 

When we think about the democratic camp, we see that its ideology tries to take from Christianity, but in real life, it is soaked in the individualistic thought centered on science. Therefore, while the ideology of democracy is based on freedom, it fundamentally contradicts Christian thought. 

The ideology of Christianity claims freedom but advocates for the freedom of the entire universe, looks for liberation but seeks liberation that can achieve the liberation of the whole, and claims unity but advocates for unity that can replace the heart of heaven, meaning that if heaven rejoices, the world can also rejoice. 

However, the people of the democratic camp today, focusing on individualistic thoughts, discuss freedom, and in the end, they deny the nation, deny society, deny organizations, and even deny family and marital relationships. Ultimately, they have reached a point where they deny even the center of their own hearts. 

So, what will be left for them in the end? Loneliness will remain. When this loneliness reaches its peak, they will become beings of disbelief, unable to believe in you or in themselves. And when they become beings of loneliness and disbelief, a cosmic fear will sweep over them, ultimately leading to self-destruction. Today's history is moving in this trend. 

Therefore, if we are to cry out for freedom, we must cry out for true freedom accompanied by the ideology of God's love, not the irresponsible freedom that was cried out in the past or is being cried out today. We must cry out for freedom that can communicate ideologically and emotionally. Thus, it must become a world that does not change, like an unchanging principle of life, or a legal freedom that cannot help but move. 

Then, where is the source of happiness that all humanity commonly desires, and where can one confidently say, "I have been liberated from all sins," and feel the joy of liberation transcending time? Where is the source of unity that transcends nations, transcends states, transcends races, transcends all thoughts, and transcends ideas? 

We, who are in the historical end times today, have never once taken this ideal that we must adopt. Therefore, even if an ideal world comes in this historical end time, or a garden of freedom is established, or a garden of liberation is built, or a garden of unity is constructed, you must understand that these will have nothing to do with you. 

Because our hope is like this, we see that God's hope is like this as well. So, when will God's hope and our hope be realized within ourselves, and when will we be able to discover the freedom, liberation, and unity that God feels and hopes for regarding us? If we do not discover this, you must realize that you cannot escape being a sacrificial offering of judgment along with the historical tragedy. 

Up to today, humanity has fought to build a world of freedom. They have fought to gain freedom. However, God has not used the strategies that humans think of. Although God had to go through the process of struggle to achieve the purpose of liberation, in terms of method, you must understand that God has taken a different approach than the struggle methods that the nations of the world have developed through bloody battles. 

What kind of person will be the protagonist of freedom? It will be a person who can host God. And because God's strategy for achieving freedom is like this, if we want to find the ideology of freedom that we can feel like heaven, we must follow heaven's strategy. That is, to find a family, one must first strike oneself to the extent that one can liberate the family, and if one wants to find a nation and a world, one must know how to strike oneself to that extent, and for heaven as well, one must strike oneself accordingly and be able to rejoice while being struck. Only those who possess such a heart of freedom may not be left behind in the end times of history. 

The protagonists of freedom, liberation, and unity that God desires must appear on this earth as individuals with the value of that reality. Otherwise, the ideals of God's freedom, God's liberation, and God's unity cannot be related to humanity. To practice this, you must understand that the one who has come as the embodiment of freedom itself, liberation itself, and unity itself on behalf of heaven is the Jesus you believe in today. 

Therefore, you must feel the heart of value that holds onto the freedom that has been intertwined with God's heart, the heart of value that has achieved liberation, and the heart of value that has achieved unity. If you cannot possess such a heart that can rejoice even when putting aside everything in this world by holding onto Jesus alone, then you cannot reach the realms of freedom, liberation, and unity that God can enjoy with humanity. 

The freedom that the world is seeking today and the freedom that God is seeking are in different directions. The world has fought for freedom, risking lives, with nations attacking nations, and sovereigns confronting each other. However, heaven is striking itself, taking responsibility, and establishing solutions from within itself, expanding to the entire scope. You must understand that this is the secret of God's movement to restore freedom. 

When you focus on yourselves today, if you possess a heart of freedom that can rejoice even in a position where you can sacrifice your life, then you can be seen as a person who possesses the highest freedom. 

Reflecting on the providence of restoration, there has been a liberation movement on earth, and at the same time, there has been a liberation movement in the spiritual world. And because God cannot directly deal with humans on this earth as His representatives or children, humans must rise from being messengers to the position of children and ultimately reach a place where they can directly face God. This is the historical journey that has been traversed. 

In the context of the Old Testament era, God established angels as messengers and built the garden of God's freedom, the kingdom of liberation. To enter the grace of liberation as a son from the position of a servant, one must be able to rejoice even while losing one's life. Only those who possess such a heart of freedom can transcend the position of a servant and find the position of a son. 

Thus, the historical ancestors who have upheld God's providence up to today have been able to possess a heart of freedom that can rejoice even while losing their lives, and they could bravely overcome all trials, even surpassing death. Because this standard of heart has been established, they have been able to hope for the transition from the position of a servant to the position of a son, from the era of servants to the era of children. And because this standard has been established, heaven could send His only begotten Son to this earth. And Jesus had to rise from the position of a son to the position of the Father. 

To achieve true freedom, liberation, and unity
Jesus stood in a position where He could freely offer His life for God until He received the recognition of the Father upon coming to this earth. And He was able to fulfill the eternal, unchanging ideal of the only begotten Son of God. Thus, until today, He has liberated those who were in the position of servants before all people, making them children. This is something you are well aware of. 

Today, Jesus, having come to this earth, overcame the path of suffering that led to death and established a standard that is one with God's inner heart, so that we may...
When you come to believe, you will receive the benefits of being able to go to the position of a child.  
If you sincerely desire the freedom, liberation, and unity that God is seeking, you must find your way from the era of servants to the era of children, and from the era of children to the era of families that serve parents. However, you must understand that this can only be determined by the principle of freedom.  
It is not achieved under any command, sanction, or coercion. You must be able to think of God and Jesus beyond even the issues of life and death, so that the feelings of joy and freedom can be exchanged, allowing the ideals of God and our very selves to establish a relationship.  
The history of restoration has also repeatedly gone through a history of liberation. Until now, we have gone through the era of servants and the path of liberation as children through Jesus and the Holy Spirit, but now we must become the sons and daughters of God centered on God's love and be children who can inherit God's legacy in God's family.  
And in order for you to establish a standard of life that can never be separated from God, you must become a person who can freely govern even death. Only then will you have the authority to inherit God's legacy as sons and daughters of God.  
Today, this land is also searching for freedom, and God is working in providence for freedom. Just as Jesus fought without regard for death for God, God also worked for Jesus without regard for even greater difficulties. Therefore, if humans in the position of servants live with a heart of freedom that does not fear death for heaven, in the end, God will come to humans with a heart that can freely overcome the brink of death.  
If you establish a standard of freedom that can overcome any suffering with joy, you will be able to overcome the fears, anger, sadness, and injustices of the past, and even transform the authority of death into God's authority of life. Only when such a time comes, where we can resolve the fundamental issues of rebirth, can we serve God freely and God can also serve us freely. And when God and we become one, the heart of God's freedom and liberation and the ideal of unity will transform into our hearts of freedom and liberation, and our ideals of unity.  
Although Jesus sacrificed his life for God, there remains a part where Jesus and God cannot connect. Jesus also freely walked the path of death for us, but there remains a part where the Holy Spirit and Jesus cannot unite. This is because Jesus is in heaven and the Holy Spirit is on earth, and there is a gap that can only be in one place, whether it be earth or heaven. Furthermore, there is also a gap between us who look at the position of children centered on Jesus and the Holy Spirit.  
To eliminate the gap that exists between Jesus and God, God must be able to love all humanity on this earth as children and must be able to hold humanity freely. Only when that day comes can all the walls that have been blocked between God and Jesus be resolved at once.  
Today, if we desire to freely overcome the path of death for God by following Jesus, this must not remain merely as an idea or thought. A standard must be established today that can freely overcome any suffering, a standard of liberation that can forget the pains of death. Because only there can a free connection with God be established, a connection of liberation be formed, and a connection of unity be formed. To do this, even if we go beyond the trials, we must have a heart that does not feel this as pain, sadness, or injustice, but rather a heart that earnestly longs for heaven, becoming a person of freedom who can overcome the peak of death.  
If such a person exists, heaven can hold onto them without caring for their own suffering or trials, even to the point of giving up all authority and prestige. Only in such a realm can God become my God, and we can also become the sons and daughters of God.

This is what you must understand as the condition of God's great lament.

The ideal of unity cannot be achieved either. That is why Jesus is still in a position where He must always pray in the other world.  
Today, a standard must be established among us Christian believers, where the principle of freedom that has penetrated God's heart, the principle of liberation that has penetrated the heart of heaven regarding all evil and death, and the principle of unity that has penetrated the heart of heaven can be established as an unchanging standard among you.  
If such a standard is established, when you look at this world, you will be able to look with the heart that God has looked at for 6,000 years, and you will be able to look with the earnest heart that God has while enduring countless sorrows, pains, and adversities to find His beloved son.  
When such an individual emerges, and a family is formed centered around that individual, and society, nations, and the world are built, you will be able to construct God's garden of freedom within your living sphere. You must understand that the garden of liberation that God hoped for, or the world of unity, also starts from such a standard.  
Until now, the world of Satan has established a sovereignty of a form of freedom that is not true freedom. It may seem like freedom, but it is not. It seems to start from the individual, passing through tribes, nations, and ultimately uniting the world, but in reality, it is far from freedom, liberation, and the principle of unity.  
As the trend of providence and the attitude that humans must have  
The more we establish the form of unity, freedom, and liberation in a position that opposes God based on the standards desired in the world, the more we will be swept away by internal anxiety, complaints, and fear. Externally, it may seem to be progressing, but internally, it is collapsing.  
Even if it appears that the external form of unity is being established, internally it is splitting apart.  
Then, how can we supplement this internal collapse? The one who performs the history of supplementation is God. If such a God does not exist, today, humanity would reach a state of despair and ultimately perish in the authority of death.  
In countries like America, people have no parents, no children, no relatives. Because of this world, many people give up on their nations. There are even many who, when they find no benefit in the religion they believed in, completely abandon it in pursuit of their own interests. However, the world was not created for the sake of one individual; it was created for the entire world. Therefore, those who live only for their own interests will face hardships proportional to the extent to which they have lived only for their own interests in front of the global ideals.  
That is why in today's society, where individualism is rampant, a society that revolves around oneself will eventually become a society of isolation, distrust, and fear.  
Thus, in the end, they will inevitably reach a state of despair and self-destruction. You must understand that we are entering such a historical end of fate.  
In light of this reality, we must have the ideals of freedom, liberation, and unity, but where should we start to achieve this?  
If you start from the individualistic thoughts you know and assert them, you will unknowingly lose the world and find yourself in a position of detachment from this world.  
Today, if there is nothing that can restore from the original individual to the original family, to the original society, to the original nation, and to the original world, it is a significant problem for both God and humanity.  
God has the responsibility to achieve the ideals of freedom, liberation, and unity with humanity in this end-of-century era. Therefore, although the external world has taken on a form of division, God has established a fundamental source of one power in the world to set the standards of absolute freedom, absolute liberation, and absolute unity, and to create a person with such standards, a family of such people, and a nation and world formed by such people.  
That is why the Bible describes Jesus as the King of kings, the protagonist of our lives, and the protagonist of heaven and earth. He is also depicted as the subject of life, the subject of ideals, and the subject of love. Therefore, until I establish an eternal relationship with this subject, Jesus, and that established relationship can again reach the stage where it can be eternally connected with God, we cannot fill the gap between God, Jesus, and us.  
Even when a society of disbelief, loneliness, or fear comes sweeping in front of us today, if you have the life force that can boldly overcome it in preparation for your death, and can freely overcome even death, then no matter what judgment world or world of destruction unfolds, your life force will not be destroyed. As long as such a standard remains, you must understand that you will not become a sacrificial offering in the realm of judgment within the authority of death.  
What is the reason God has labored for 6,000 years?  
This standard must not be established merely ideologically; the spirit and flesh must become one in reality to establish that standard. Whether you possess that standard will determine whether you can remain in the future. Only by possessing such a standard can you become one who can serve God with your life, as God comes to find us with all that He has, risking His life.  
Only then can God establish a free lifestyle by finding me, and can God establish the ideals of freedom, liberation, and unity by finding me. If you become such a qualified person, as long as God exists eternally, there will be no relationship between us and the authority of death.  
Now, when you return to your individual self and ask yourself, do you have the heart of freedom, the life of freedom, and the ideals of freedom that can be enjoyed centered on true life in your heart? This is where the problem lies.  
As long as you have such a heart, such life, and such ideals, you can freely digest and overcome any path of death, any path that follows with death and suffering, and you can become one who can restore the elements of life. Thus, you must understand that you can become an existence that can live forever in God's world of freedom, in God's garden of liberation, and in God's garden of unity.  
While we seek the path of freedom, we may face tests and sufferings, but who can block the earnest heart toward God, the surging heart of freedom? No one can stop it. Everything can be broken, but that cannot be broken. That surging heart cannot be stopped, no matter how strong the authority of death is.  
When the connection of life that can eternally unite God and me is centered around your life, the eternal freedom of God, the liberation of God, and the unity of God will finally be established in your heart. Unless such a standard is established in your heart, the relative ideals of freedom, liberation, and unity that you desire will have no relation to you, no matter how much they are achieved.  
Then, what is the reason God has labored for 6,000 years? It was to find a form that can possess, feel, and achieve that freedom, liberation, and unity that God hopes for, in place of God's heart. Just as God exists eternally, there must be a standard that cannot change eternally for such a world of ideals to come before you.  
If you do not have such a mental standard, no matter how much the external world is established, that is, no matter how much the world of freedom, liberation, and unity is established externally, it is not a complete world of unity, nor a complete world of liberation, nor a complete world of freedom.  
Then, today, if the life force is surging in our hearts, if the power of ideals is surging, if the power of love is surging, unless the firm standard of that surging power, the standard of sincerity toward God who has labored for 6,000 years, is established within you, when the authority of darkness and death that has fought against heaven for 6,000 years covers your life, you must understand that you will not be able to remain.  
In the realm of God's love, possessing your life force, your ideals, and your power of love, and based on that, the freedom you sing about is true freedom, and liberation based on such principles is true liberation, and unity based on such principles is true unity.  
If you do not establish such a standard, when the world is swept away by chaos, confusion, and fear, you will not be able to stop it. The only thing that can move it is the life force, the power of ideals, and the power of love. If you do not establish a standard that can overcome this, no matter how much God's providential work has labored, you must remember that you will not be able to find the freedom, liberation, and unity that God sought through providence.
<Prayer> Heavenly Father! Please have mercy on humanity that has lost the garden of freedom, the garden of liberation, and the garden of unification. We thought that all the lost things would be resolved in the external world, but we have come to understand the historical sorrow that has been divided internally while appearing to have certain standards externally.  
Now, may the life force of God, the power of love, and the power of ideals that can seize the internal world of freedom, the internal world of liberation, and the internal world of unification overflow in us, establishing a standard of heart that can laugh at death and overcome all pain, sorrow, and injustice. Thus, may we come to know that in the world of heart, we can feel the freedom of all saints, perceive the entirety of our environment, and even move the entirety of life.  
Heavenly Father! When we look at today's historical world, we realize that while promoting internal division, it outwardly presents a plausible form of unification, centered around materialism. Only those who have such a heart can possess the kingdom of heaven, and such people are qualified to fulfill the ideals of the kingdom of heaven. Therefore, you said to us, "I am in your heart," and Jesus also said to us, "I am in your heart." I earnestly wish and hope that you will allow us to understand that all solutions can only be realized from the psychological standard that believes the kingdom of heaven is in our hearts.  
Heavenly Father, now I wish that we may feel your heart as more precious than our own bodies, more precious than our own freedom, and more precious than our own lives today, and that we may recover a heart that can feel your sorrow more painfully than the death of the entire world, and allow us to stand before you as sons and daughters who can understand this.  
Before the historical journey of seeking and wandering, please allow your heart to explode in our hearts, and based on your life, your ideals, and your love, may we possess the entirety of freedom based on life, freedom based on ideals, freedom based on love, and the liberation and unification based on these.  
Heavenly Father! Now, comfort yourself! I have come to know that this is your heart. Please allow us to establish a psychological foundation that can fulfill the wishes of the Father who has labored in the historical process. Thus, may we be in a position to sing of life, ideals, and liberation that can glorify you, and may we resolve all the sorrows and pains of restoration and the heart of the Father who has governed the restoration movement of freedom, so that all humanity in the world can sing of freedom, liberation, and unification as your sons and daughters.  
If we have the heart of freedom today, if we have the heart of liberation, we know that even if there are countless satans and countless enemies, they cannot do anything to us. We also know that we are not bound by ideals, and on the day when our hearts move in unison with you in a unified standard of freedom and liberation, heaven and earth will automatically move according to that unified standard. Therefore, I earnestly wish and hope that you will grant us such a standard in our hearts.  
For this life and this hope, please allow us to set a standard that can unite with your heart, even if it means we must face death, and do not let us become those who fall into the mockery of enemies until we can hold you in our hearts.  
Please allow us to be sons and daughters who do not change until your heart dwells in our hearts, overcoming the persecution of enemies. I earnestly ask that you allow us to be sons and daughters who can overcome all fears, and I pray all these words in your name. Amen.  
22) Who Will Be the Friend of Golgotha?  
Luke 23:26-43  
<Prayer> Today, we have gathered again before your knees, Father, and we are afraid that we may not give glory to you, our sorrowful Father, and we are afraid that we may reveal our foolish faults before your desired will. Heavenly Father! If we are unworthy, please allow us to have at least a sincere heart that can lower ourselves and seek your mercy.  
Without your care, how can we behold your glory on this earth, and if we cannot become those who remain in your heart, how can we behold the will of the garden you have granted? Father! We have always envisioned being a group that can remain in your heart, a group that can resonate with your heart, and a group that can live with you.  
At first, we sang of you by experiencing your heart, but we know that many have hearts that have been wounded along the way, so Father, please have mercy on all their difficult circumstances.  
We have learned through the path of restoration that the determination we made before you at the beginning must remain in the garden of restoration at the end. Among the people of Israel, there were those who did not fall in the wilderness because the earnest heart they had when they left the palace of Pharaoh in Egypt did not change even during the 40 years in the wilderness. Furthermore, we know very well that those who left a heart of loyalty toward you received the blessings of the Second Israel on October 19, 1958.  
May this time be a moment for us to reflect on whether we, who swore before you and made resolutions before you, have become those who can obey your commands.  
The end is approaching, and we know that you must be sighing because there are no groups to take responsibility for you. We, who seek you and behold your glory, claim to be your children, but we see that there is no group that can take responsibility in any area of your will, your providence, or the path of your struggle, and we know that you are sighing. Heavenly Father! Please allow us to build an altar of atonement before you and shed tears of repentance at this time.  
We know the group of Israelites who fell in the wilderness, blaming you with a heart that longs for rest. Today, we have gathered to avoid becoming such a group, longing for your hand, so please lead us to be a group that participates in your glory, beloved Father, I earnestly wish and hope.  
Father, now please have mercy on this 30 million people. Father, please have mercy on this nation. There may be many altars being raised for this nation that are far from the people and far from the will of heaven, so if there is a providential will that must be fulfilled through them, please intervene directly, and if they do not listen to your counsel, please teach them their path even if it means lifting the whip. Beloved Father, I earnestly wish and hope.  
If there are to be those who bear the mission of awakening this sleeping nation, there must be a group that remains until the end, so Father, please allow even one more life to resonate with your heart of love. Please lead us to be your sons and daughters who can hold on to the Father who has sighed for 6,000 years, repent before you, and fight against Satan, beloved Father, I earnestly wish and hope.  
You have worked and governed, but due to the mistakes of humanity, regret, sighs, and grudges have accumulated, so please resolve those grudges through us.

Beloved Father, I earnestly wish and hope.

Father, the timing and the will you have permitted must be manifested and fulfilled through us today, but when we cannot face your will, we cannot help but worry that the time will come when you will raise a group prepared by you to shame us. Heavenly Father! Please manifest a glorious day through us and resolve the heart of your resentment.  
Thus, on the day of joy that you establish, may we also be able to rejoice together, beloved Father, I earnestly wish and hope.

Beloved Father, I earnestly wish and hope.
