Thus, may we center our lives around you whether we live or die, and may we be those who are owned by you whether we live or die. Heavenly Father, I earnestly wish and hope, and I entrust this remaining time to you, so please govern it according to your worthy will.  
Today, there are lonely groups praying earnestly throughout the regions, so Father, please extend your hand of grace uniformly to them and grant them the grace of counsel so that they may experience the glory of heaven. I earnestly ask all these things in your name. Amen.  
<Word> The title of the message I wish to think about with you today is "Who Will Be the Friend of Golgotha?"  
Jesus, who brought the truth, life, love, and ideals of heaven,  
Golgotha means the place of the skull, and thus it signifies the place of death. Therefore, to become a friend of Golgotha means to become a friend of the path of death.  
Christian believers believe in the Lord of Golgotha. When we think of Golgotha, we recall the cross of Jesus, and when we think of the cross of Jesus, we recall the image of Jesus, and when we think of that image of Jesus, we remember that heaven mourned with his passing.  
However, while heaven mourned for Jesus, the earth rejoiced. Jesus came for the earth and came for heaven. Yet, while heaven acknowledged Jesus, who was going for both heaven and earth, the earth did not recognize him. We must understand that this is the historical sorrow.  
If the people of Israel had stood in a position to know Jesus, whom heaven sent, as God knows him, the history of humanity today would not have been shaped in such a stark manner. Jesus came as the representative of truth, life, ideals, and love, but the truth, life, ideals, and love he proclaimed were not based on humanity but on heaven. The truth that fallen humanity must seek, the life fallen humanity must possess, the ideals fallen humanity must pursue, and the love fallen humanity must eternally own were all brought by Jesus. However, after Jesus passed away on earth, humanity could no longer find the truth they were seeking, nor could they find the life, ideals, and love they desired.  
Thus, we must once again realize that humanity has been wandering until today.  
Until now, there has been no one on this earth who possesses the words of truth that flow from the heart of Jesus, nor has there been anyone who possesses the life that permeates the bones and flesh of Jesus. Furthermore, there has been no one on this earth who possesses the love of Jesus that could unite all people and enable them to run toward a single purpose. Jesus, who brought the truth, life, ideals, and love of heaven, sought to fulfill the will of heaven through the fallen humans of the earth and aimed to achieve a unified purpose with the Creator God. However, because our ancestors disbelieved and betrayed,
After that, there was no place for the truth that God intended to establish throughout history, and all the life, ideals, and love that God wanted to establish have also disappeared. Therefore, humanity, buried in the bonds of the fall, had to wander in search of the true word, the true life, the true ideals, and the true love. Because of this, there must come a time when the people of the end will have to go through the sorrowful struggles of the historical process to find one life. A movement of one life must arise that can move the world and achieve a common purpose encompassing all humanity with one ideology. 

Thus, it is hoped that all of humanity will unite as one, an inseparable entity, and that a unified movement of love capable of melting anything will unfold in the end. Countless prophets and righteous people who came and went to fulfill this purpose have longed for this day. Furthermore, it is a critical time for the first-class people of the world, who live today in sorrow, resentment, and fear, to feel once again that many of them fought without concern for death to realize such a day. We must feel this. 

Although Jesus was crucified and died, it was not a complete failure. After Jesus died, rather, his words, that is, the truth remained, life remained, and love remained. So how will humanity today find these remaining words, remaining life, remaining ideals, and remaining love? You must understand that this is the ultimate problem that humanity must solve together. 

What was the sorrow that Jesus himself, who came with God's will, felt? What was the injustice he experienced, and what was the resentment he felt? What was the greatest pain of pains? Knowing that he possessed the heavenly words overflowing with life, ideals, and love for humanity, you must understand that the greatest sorrow for Jesus was his heart that could not fully deliver the word, his heart that could not give all his life, and his heart that could not provide the ideals that humanity could rejoice in, as well as his heart that could not give the heavenly love. 

God, throughout the thousands of years of historical processes, established our ancestors to cooperate with the will of heaven, but our ancestors betrayed heaven in every era. Therefore, since we are descendants of ancestors who betrayed heaven, we must realize that we ourselves, facing the end today, are also standing at a tremendous crossroads where we could easily become a historical and cosmic betrayal once again. 

God, after thousands of years of labor, chose the people of Israel as the center of one word, the center of life, the center of ideals, and the center of love, sending the Messiah, who is Jesus, to them. However, the Jewish people, who had awaited and prepared for thousands of years for this one Messiah, failed to welcome him. Jesus, who was to be the historical protagonist that countless ancestors had hoped for, was not received by a single person. 

Today, we should not become a group that boasts of the Jesus who lay in the manger in Bethlehem. There was a prophecy that the Messiah would appear in Bethlehem at that time, but there was no group that built even a small hut to wait for the Messiah according to that prophecy. 

I do not know if there was any hut owner who worried that the Lord might come unexpectedly to Bethlehem and prepared for that time and season, but when the Messiah actually appeared, there was no one to receive him. When Jesus was born, the entire city of Jerusalem was in turmoil. The rumor spread that the Messiah was born in Bethlehem. Yet, there was not a single person in the city of Jerusalem or Bethlehem who prepared for the birth of the Messiah. Christians today must reflect once again on the pitiful state of Jesus, who was to be the prince of heaven and the Messiah of all people, lying in a manger. 

Furthermore, because the Israelite people failed to recognize the Messiah, who spoke of and testified to the heavenly circumstances, today Israel cannot stand before heaven. The Messiah, when he comes to the earth, must have clothing and a place to live. Yet, among the Pharisees, Sadducees, and all the Jewish people who believed in heaven at that time, there was not a single person who prepared even a single room to receive the Messiah who appeared. 

We must grieve over the sins that our ancestors, who believed in heaven in such a foolish manner, have left behind. Today, in order not to walk the same historical path, we must become a group that worries in our hearts and appeals to heaven. 

Heaven prepared the Israelite people for 4,000 years to send one Messiah, and how could it be that Jesus' situation turned out this way! Where did the labor of 4,000 years go? Heaven sent a chosen son, but the Jewish people, who were unaware and in a deep sleep at that time, were in a deep sleep. 

They were a group that boasted of their own sect that could replace sovereignty. They were also a Jewish sect that sought to uphold the will of heaven. The appearance of Jesus before such a people was a fact that lay between humanity, who had to face God's will, and God, who was guiding that will. However, you may not be aware of this fact. 

Jesus worked as a carpenter until he was 30 years old. If there is anyone who has had a spiritual experience, they would know a part of Jesus' 30 years of life. If someone knows this, they will feel pain even when eating good food, feel pain even when wearing good clothes, and live a sorrowful life even when in a good environment. 

When Joseph brought Mary according to God's will, God was with him. However, after that, Jesus, who grew up in Joseph's household, was treated as a stepchild. As Joseph's children increased, Jesus became increasingly isolated. Thus, he spent over 30 years working with a saw and plane, making doors for others, unable to express his own circumstances and feelings. Who knew about Jesus' situation? No one knew. At that time, Jesus did not appear as the historical Jesus that you believe in today, nor as the Christ with a historically evaluated personality. 

So who will be the one to welcome the Messiah who appears in the end today? It will not be someone who receives the historical Jesus. You must understand that it will be someone who receives the contemporary Jesus. 

He was Jesus, who bore the will of heaven in his heart and worried about this land, yet found himself in a sorrowful position where his parents did not recognize him, and even his brothers did not recognize him. 

We must believe in such a Jesus now. We, the members of the Unification Church, must believe in that Jesus first and know that Jesus first. We know the Jesus of the cross, the Jesus who walked the path of death, but we must also know that he was the Jesus who came to find the way of life. We should not just be a group that holds on to the dead Jesus and weeps. 

Before Jesus died, he could not express his heart, which was looking forward to death, to anyone, and he was in a miserable situation where he could not express his heart, which was filled with the worries, sorrows, and desires of heaven and earth. If there had been a group that could hold onto such a Jesus, understand his situation, and be friends with him, they would have become the apostles of Jesus. 

But what about Peter? How did Peter, a fisherman catching fish by the Sea of Galilee, become the chief disciple of Jesus? This was a fact that should have caused a stomachache. Where did Judaism go, where did the chosen people go, and how could this unexpected Peter or these fishermen become disciples of Jesus? Jesus could not help but feel resentment. He was a Jesus who was saddened by the lack of welcoming Jewish people. 

Therefore, today you must believe in the Lord, but do not only believe in the Jesus who died; you must believe in the Jesus who lived and worked. You must believe in the Jesus who worried about the will of heaven throughout his life of over 30 years, not just the Jesus who died on the cross. You must understand that his life was filled with sighs for the purpose, a heart of sorrow, and also the sorrow of the cross. 

Where is there anyone on earth who knows the heart of Jesus suffering on Golgotha? Where is there a friend of his? Jesus needed friends from his family, friends among his brothers, friends who could replace all fathers and mothers, friends who could bear the cross that Jesus had to bear, and friends who could walk the path of the world's cross, the path of Golgotha. However, today, there is not a single person who knows that will and believes in Jesus. 

The Jesus who came for the historical purpose appeared as a human in the flesh but fell while working in an unfavorable environment of the times, and those who walk the historical path left by Jesus are also in an unfavorable historical environment, crying out for Jesus. Furthermore, the reason Jesus bore the cross on Golgotha was that the entire universe was at stake. Therefore, we must understand that there is a heavenly heart seeking a friend of Golgotha. 

In other words, heaven is searching for a friend who can understand the heart of Golgotha. Then, Jesus likened himself to a bridegroom and the saints to brides. Who will be the bride of Jesus? It will be those who can be friends on the path of Golgotha. 

Historically, when evil becomes strong, good becomes weak. When evil becomes strong and good cannot lead evil, evil has flowed while occupying good. However, amidst this, small good has emerged and has advanced toward a greater good, achieving the purpose of good. You must understand that this is the historical development process that has continued to this day. 

Thus, history starts from individuals, flows through families, and takes on a social character. It has passed through collective clan forms, tribes, nations, and has reached the world. Furthermore, history will not end in the visible world but will advance to the world of the spiritual universe. 

In the history of humanity, there is an era of good that asserts itself centered on individuals, an era of good centered on clans, an era of good centered on tribes, an era of good centered on nations, an era of good centered on states, and an era of good centered on the world. In this way, history has developed from small good to greater good. 

Therefore, in the struggle, the struggle of individuals becomes the struggle of families, the struggle of families becomes the struggle of clans, the struggle of clans becomes the struggle of society, the struggle of society becomes the struggle of nations, and the struggle of nations becomes the struggle of the world, leading to a struggle with the spiritual world, if it exists, and a struggle with the countless evil spirits on this earth. Moreover, if God exists, the struggle with the countless evil spirits on this earth must end for a peaceful era to come to this universe. You must realize this principled process through which God is guiding. 

God must resolve all issues by fighting against Satan and the evil forces on this earth for a universal peace era to come. 

Then, as the struggle of individuals grows to clans, tribes, nations, and the world, what will happen in the future? If there is a spiritual world and heaven, we must fight against that spiritual world. How will you escape the fear that comes to you in your hearts, facing the end? A time will come when you will feel fears greater than atomic bombs. That is, not only the fear of the atomic age occurring externally but also the waves of fear that will invade you internally. 

For this reason, humanity today is filled with fear. Moreover, the number of mental illness cases is increasing. This is because we are in a struggle against spiritual Satan. We must end this struggle and become one with the good God, taking on the fight of our heavenly Father, becoming the person who takes responsibility for the Father's sorrow, pain, and injustice. Thus, the day that will take on the Father's pain, sorrow, and injustice is the day of the Second Coming of Jesus and the day of the great judgment that humanity must face. This is how God's providence is set. 

Then, what will happen today, having gone through this historical process? This time is when the era of national struggles is passing, and democracy and communism are going through a global struggle process, so they will inevitably become one. Then, how did the history of Christianity come to go through such a process? When Jesus bore the cross on Golgotha, the forms of the thief on his right and the thief on his left are now appearing globally. The thief on the right appears as a global democratic form representing heaven, while the thief on the left appears as a global form opposing heaven and centered on material and humanity. 

What will appear next? It is the turning point of resurrection that comes with the death of Jesus. That is, the personal left thief started and developed at the family level, and this has formed tribes, nations, and the world, and the right thief form has also formed the world. The very fact that Jesus was sown on the earth has manifested in this way at the end. 

Then, what we need to worry about here is what position democracy has been established in. You must understand that you should be able to rejoice in yourself when the kingdom of God comes by knowing the heart of Jesus at the time of his return. You must realize what will happen to this democracy, which lacks an ideology that can replace the heart of Jesus. We, who belong to the democratic camp today, must become like the thief on the right, who knows that he deserves to die a million times and can weep for the death of Jesus. 

You must understand that the time has come for you to become such people. 

Peter and the 12 disciples, who should have been friends of Golgotha
When viewed from a Christian perspective, the phenomena occurring worldwide today are the conclusive phenomena of history. You should pray to understand what historical processes God has gone through to reach this conclusion. Thus, you must pray, "Father! As the chosen people of this nation, let us receive the blessings of the world. Judge Judaism and judge the ranks of disbelief." You must understand that this was the situation Jesus experienced. 

What was the resentment Jesus felt when he died? The chosen Judaism caused pain in Jesus' heart, and the chosen people crucified him. This was what was resentful and unjust. Although Jesus had great sorrow, you must understand the situation of God, who walked the path of building an altar of tears for 4,000 years.
and when I think that they were the Jewish people whom God chose and nurtured for 4,000 years, 
it makes me realize that He was able to forget His own death and pray for them. This spirit of Jesus 
should be felt once again by Christians scattered around the world today. 
If Jesus had not raised His hands to pray, the Jewish nation would have been judged first, 
and the Jews would have been judged first. You must understand that Jesus, who left blessings 
hoping that Heaven would leave a process of grace for those who are dying to follow in His footsteps, 
was indeed that Jesus. 
When I see Jesus’ words concerning the thief on His right, tears come to my eyes involuntarily. 
It is sorrowful and heartbreaking. The nation that did not know the sorrow of God for 4,000 years... 
This was a sad scene. At that time, there were countless people simply lying before Jesus. 
The group that should have been united with Jesus' blood and flesh had to be the Jews and the Jewish people, 
but they were not. They should have shed blood together with Jesus at His crucifixion, 
yet instead, a murderer was accompanying Him. Jesus was a Savior for all people, yet the fact that 
the only companion at His death was a murderer is an extremely embarrassing fact. 
If Peter had become the friend of Golgotha, or if he had become one of the 12 disciples, 
there would have been no resentment in Heaven. If that had happened, Jesus would not have died. 
If the 12 disciples had united and wanted to die together with Jesus, a miracle would have occurred. 
In that case, Jesus would not have died. 
However, Jesus, who looked upon the chosen nation with sorrow for 33 years,

had hoped in Jesus go? Where did the church that was watching go? Where did the disciples who

and joyful for them, they said, "I am a friend of Jesus, I am a disciple of Jesus." 
They tried to stand in Jesus' position more than anyone else. However, in the end, they found 
themselves in a position completely unrelated to the path Jesus was taking. This has also become 
the root of the new historical beginning, and history has developed in such a way that it has led 
to today's end. 
Then who received the blessings of Jesus? It was not the 12 disciples who followed Him, 
nor the Jews who believed in Heaven, nor the chosen people of Israel whom He blessed. 
It was the thief on the right who died alongside Him on the cross, shedding blood together, 
who received historical blessings and entered paradise before the chief disciple. 
This fact is the tragedy of tragedies. If even one of the murderers had not participated 
in the day of Jesus' death, the providence of salvation would have been frustrated. 
Because the blood of the murderer shed could establish the condition to build a welfare paradise 
on earth in place of Jesus' heart, you must understand that Jesus was able to resurrect and 
appear again on earth to face the people who had doubted Him. 
And because there was someone who welcomed Jesus as the bridegroom at the place of death, 
it is through that foundation that the fruits of goodness will surely appear on earth. 
It means that Jesus will appear instead. 
No matter how strong the forces of Satan are, you must understand that they cannot eliminate 
the very essence of goodness. Not only is there a person who stands in the place of sacrifice and death 
for goodness, but if there is a person of loyalty who holds onto that goodness and falls, 
then you must understand that goodness will multiply many times over because of that fallen individual. 
This is a principle. 
The people who opposed Him at that time thought that if they executed Jesus on the cross, 
He would perish. They believed that because there was not a single person following Jesus, 
they had taken everything from the realm of Satan. However, they do not know that the resurrection 
was raised based on the condition of the dead thief. 
The Path to Golgotha that Must Be Overcome 
Satan struck Jesus and the thief on the right and then struck the twelve disciples. 
After Jesus died, Satan struck the twelve disciples. Heaven had given the twelve disciples over to Satan. 
Then why did it have to strike them so? The path of Jesus was a personal path of Golgotha, 
but because Jesus walked the path of Golgotha, the twelve disciples also had to walk the path of Golgotha, 
the Jewish people had to walk the path of Golgotha, and the nation of Israel had to walk the path of Golgotha. 
And today, all Christians around the world must walk this path of Golgotha, 
and all of humanity must also pass over this path of Golgotha, you must understand that. 
However, today, this democratic world does not know that it must overcome the global Golgotha 
that Jesus traversed centered around democracy. 
As you know, when Jesus prayed, "My God, my God, why have You forsaken me?" (Matthew 27:46), 
it was not because He was sad about His own death, but because He was concerned that if He died like this, 
all humanity would have to pass over the Golgotha of the cross because of Him. 
Thus, He prayed, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me." (Matthew 26:39). 
If Jesus had not crossed this Golgotha, there would have been no global Golgotha. 
After Jesus crossed the Golgotha, those who followed Him, that is, individuals were left with their own personal Golgotha, 
and in the providential time and era centered around families, there was a familial Golgotha left. 
Also, when the providential will expanded to the societal level after passing through the family era, 
there remained not only the path of the cross for families but also the path of the cross for society. 
Furthermore, in the era of national providence that believes in and upholds the will of Heaven, 
there was a need to walk the path of the cross for families, society, and nations. 
Therefore, if the global Christ were to come to this earth today, He would have to carry all the crosses 
for the world, the nation, society, family, and individuals. 
The fact that such a fateful peak remains is something that today's world Christians do not know. 
What kind of Lord do Christians today want to meet? If there is Heaven, where will they meet Jesus? 
They must cross the peak of the cross and meet Him in the place of resurrection. 
This is the resurrection of the Second Coming. That is why the historical path from the time Jesus came 
until today has been walking the Golgotha path toward individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world, 
being pushed and beaten. 
Today, this era is when the democratic camp is facing the communist camp. 
Then how will we overcome this global Golgotha? Just like Jesus, we must harbor a deep heart for this nation 
so that the entire nation can move as one body. You must understand that until such a nation is formed, 
the path of the global Golgotha will be blocked. 
Therefore, in the most wicked place, we must find and establish a root of goodness or the fruits of goodness, 
so that a way can be opened to make one from the wicked sinner to the good person. 
Thus, we must seek to find the lost twelve disciples relying on the authority of the resurrected Jesus. 
At that time, individuals should have welcomed Jesus in place of the twelve disciples. 
However, because they could not do so, most of the twelve disciples were massacred. 
When the twelve disciples were to walk the path of death, there was one person who was pushed out among them, 
and that was Apostle John. And one of the thieves was pushed out by the Jews, the nation of Israel, 
and the betraying twelve disciples. Heaven established one Jesus among the nation it raised, 
and through His resurrection, it raised the twelve disciples again. 
Furthermore, Heaven established one person who would take the place of the twelve disciples, 
and that person was Paul. 
A New Providence Centered on Paul 
Today, Christians say that Paul loved Heaven and knew God's will. 
However, at that time, Paul was pushed out by the twelve disciples. 
Although he preached the gospel as an apostle, Paul was pushed out by the twelve disciples. 
Paul met the resurrected Jesus and received Heaven's mission. 
Thus, he was not a betraying apostle but a living apostle who did not betray, 
who went to the foreign land of Rome, preaching the gospel while facing persecution. 
Because Paul sought the Lord in place of the martyrdom of the twelve disciples, 
and in place of the death of John the Baptist, the providential trajectory on earth was shifted to the foreign nations. 
Do you understand what this means? Thus, Paul entered the Roman Empire and faced persecution alone. 
He found himself in a position that was not welcomed religiously. 
However, Paul, holding onto the one providential will set by Jesus, walked the Golgotha path of humanity, 
and he did not yield to any arrows of persecution from Rome but pierced through and advanced. 
His appearance, not caring about death for the will of Heaven, resembled that of Jesus. 
Thus, centered on Paul, Christianity moved through a form of family, 
through a form of tribe, and then through nation, state, and world forms. 
Just as Jesus walked the path of Golgotha, Paul took on the heavenly mission and voluntarily walked the path of Golgotha of death, 
facing the world of Satan. Thus, you must understand that he went through the extreme persecution and massacre 
during the reign of Nero in Rome. 
Also, Paul's personal sacrifice raised up tribes of that time, or people like the twelve disciples, 
and like Israel. Thus, because the individual fought to overcome the path of death, 
the Roman Empire could be taken away. 
As a result, Christianity flourished during the approximately four centuries that followed. 
In the medieval feudal society, centered around the Roman papacy, Christianity entered its golden age. 
Thus, Christians began to dominate the entire world. 
However, the Roman Catholic Church had a direction to go, 
which was to overcome the national Golgotha and pioneer a global stage, 
but because they were caught up in the desires of national ideology, Heaven struck them. 
Through the Renaissance, it broke in, and through the Reformation, it shattered the old consciousness, 
leading to the fundamental downfall of the papacy. 
Thus, they gradually fell into decline. 
However, among these believers of Christianity, a new revolutionary force emerged. 
These were the rebels centered around Luther and the Protestants. 
In the process of attacking the group centered around the old church, 
the oppressed groups formed the new church centered around Luther, that is, the Protestants. 
The Puritans who inherited this spirit went to America and established a new continental civilization, 
building a global Christian kingdom. 
However, even though global history has flowed like this, Heaven will now strike the world. 
Therefore, we must learn to look for the oppressed groups among humanity. 
We must find out which is the most oppressed group among the democratic camp, 
which is the most pitiful country among the democratic camp. 
This means that just as the thief who became a friend of Jesus on the cross, 
there will emerge a group, a nation that is not friends with the Jewish nation that betrayed Him, 
as they pass through the global Golgotha. 
The emergence of such a group, such a nation, is historically valid in light of the providential perspective. 
God's Providence Centered on the Oppressed 
However, when we look at the world today, communism, which does not believe in God, has emerged. 
They say there is no God. Where is God? 
Therefore, just as the thief on the right appeared who became a friend of Jesus at the place of Jesus' death, 
today, communism is going out with a policy of massacre to realize all their ambitions, 
and you must understand that this massacre becomes the sacrificial condition to side with the democratic camp. 
Then, how should today's Christians, who are being pushed out globally, 
overcome this Golgotha? They must become the group that first walks the path of Golgotha before the world. 
They must be the oppressed group at the forefront of all Christianity, 
just as Paul was oppressed before the apostles, the thief was oppressed before the Jews, 
and the Protestants were oppressed before the Roman papacy. 
We must always look for the oppressed groups that will emerge from the perspective of the new reformation today. 
This is a fact proven by history. 
Now, today, we, the members of the Unification Church, must be the new reformed religious organization of the 20th century, 
and we must be the oppressed group from all ideologies and thoughts of the 20th century. 
We must become the oppressed group in the democratic camp and the sectarian situation of this world. 
Moreover, if there is a nation that has come out with the ideology of Heaven, 
that nation must also shed blood before the world like the thief. 
Thus, Korea, centered around the 38th parallel and through the Korean War, 
has placed the fate of life and death of the world on the line, 
and the left and right are clashing in a position of shedding blood. 
When we think of this, we cannot say that today's Golgotha of democracy is not similar to the new world of the right-hand thief. 
Then, if there is a grievance before the Korean people today, what should we hold onto? 
It is not the time to fight holding onto the Lord's ideology. 
We must have the heart of Jesus who died on Golgotha, 
the heart that knows the betrayal of the nation, the heart of historical betrayal, the heart of global betrayal, 
and we must have the heart that says, "I will take your place so that you do not have to walk the path of suffering." 
Thus, if this nation has the heart of the right-hand thief who wanted to praise the glory of Jesus, 
wouldn't we welcome the resurrected Jesus on the path of death of Golgotha and enter the age of resurrection glory? 
That is why, today, you members of the Unification Church, do not be sad about being persecuted. 
As you are pushed and pushed, you will come to know the heart of Jesus, 
and when you meet Jesus, you will come to understand the heart that prayed earnestly in the Garden of Gethsemane before the Golgotha of death. 
Just as Jesus stood at the extreme of oppression and united with Heaven to bring forth the gift of resurrection, 
if you are being oppressed, a new history can begin from here. 
If we have a global ideology, we must be the group that is oppressed globally, nationally, ecclesiastically, socially, domestically, and personally, 
but only by becoming the remaining group here can we become the original sons and daughters of Heaven 
who can bear the qualifications of a bride before the Lord who comes after crossing the cosmic Golgotha in the age of cosmic resurrection. 
Thus, today, you have been searching for true friends. 
You have been searching for true families and true teachers. 
You have been searching for the true Lord, the true nation, and the true world, but you have not yet found them. 
When viewed centered around Jesus, you must realize that you have lost the position to achieve that purpose. 
Therefore, if today I desire to find true friends, 
I must become a true friend at the Golgotha of friends, 
and if I wish to find a true family, I must become one who bears the responsibility of the family's Golgotha. 
Furthermore, in the Golgotha path of the nation or the world, you must carry the heart of Jesus and take responsibility for the path of Golgotha. 
Thus, everyone must cross their eternal path.
Even if you entrust and rely on life issues, you must be able to handle them, and furthermore, you must become a person who can manage global problems. You must remember that only then can you become a friend before heaven on the path of the global Golgotha. *
